# Planyr тАФ Backlog

Single source of truth for bugs and feature requests. Repo: `planyr` (product: **Planyr**).

> *"Single source of truth"* = the one file everyone trusts for what's done and what's left, so status never has to be tracked in anyone's head or in a chat thread.

---

## How this file works тАФ Claude Code, read this first

- **On each run:** address every item under **ЁЯФ▓ Open**. Do **not** action anything under **ЁЯХУ Later / Roadmap** unless it's been moved up to Open. **тП│ Verify** items are already implemented and only awaiting a live check тАФ they **park**, they never block a session (see the lifecycle below). Completed items live in `BACKLOG-DONE.md` тАФ do not read it unless looking up a specific past item.
- **IDs are permanent.** The next B# = highest `B#` across **both** `BACKLOG.md` and `BACKLOG-DONE.md` + 1. Never renumber or reuse a number, even after items are done.
- **Items pasted from another chat are "blind" to this file** and may carry provisional `NEW-#` (or stale/colliding `B#`) labels тАФ treat those as scratch references only and assign the real next `B#` when filing. When you file a chat item, add an **`Origin: filed <date> from chat`** line so its provisional `NEW-#` resolves to the real `B#` later.
- **Before filing, DEDUPE-FIRST.** Search **Open, тП│ Verify, AND Done** (`^### B` headings) before minting a `B#`. If an arriving report matches an existing item, do **NOT** create a new number тАФ apply the **recurrence rule** below instead.
- **Bracket tags** like `[Site Planner]` mark the module. `(bug)` / `(feature)` / `(task)` marks the type. **`#tags`** (from the legend below) mark the theme тАФ every Open / тП│ Verify item carries one or more.
- **Always commit after editing this file or finishing a fix** тАФ never leave the working tree dirty. A fix that isn't committed doesn't count as done.
- **Regenerate `BACKLOG_OPEN.md` in the SAME commit as any `BACKLOG.md` edit** (`node scripts/build-backlog-index.mjs`). It is the small, committed, chat-readable index of every Open/Verify item (B#, title, module, tags, Verify status) тАФ **derived, never hand-edited**. CI runs `--check` and fails the build if it drifts from this file.
- **Never delete items.** Completed ones stay in `BACKLOG-DONE.md` as a record.
- **If an item is ambiguous,** don't guess. Mark it `[?]`, add your question inline, and leave it in Open.

### Item lifecycle тАФ ЁЯФ▓ Open тЖТ тП│ Verify тЖТ тЬЕ Done (three states, B636)

Items no longer jump straight from Open to Done on a sandbox pass тАФ live-only bugs (dependency arrows, export furniture sizing, тАж) kept boomeranging back. Every item carries a **`Verify:` field**:

- **`Verify: sandbox`** (the default) тАФ a green build + the right unit/headless self-test is sufficient proof. On completion, move the whole block straight to `BACKLOG-DONE.md`.
- **`Verify: live`** тАФ the fix can only be *confirmed* in the live app. **Mandatory `live` classes:** timing/race bugs ┬╖ concurrency / multi-writer ┬╖ GIS endpoint behavior ┬╖ zoom- or data-density-dependent rendering ┬╖ PDF / export parity ┬╖ anything whose repro cites real project data. (This is the **LIVE-VERIFY** rule in `CLAUDE.md`.) After implementing, move the block to the **тП│ Verify** section with a dated note; it moves to Done **only after** a verification note is appended (date ┬╖ method тАФ Cowork or Michael on planyr.io ┬╖ observed result). **Moving a `live` item straight to Done is a protocol violation.**

тП│ Verify items **park** тАФ they never block a session; the session that implements one keeps going.

### Recurrence тАФ a fix that didn't stick does NOT get a new number (B636)

When a new report matches an existing **Done or тП│ Verify** item (search titles, tags, symbols): do **NOT** mint a new `B#`. **Move the original block back to ЁЯФ▓ Open**, append a `Recurrence: <date> тАФ <one-line report>` line, and add a visible count to the title, e.g. `(├Ч3)`. Non-sticking fixes become visible on the one ID instead of scattering across new numbers.

### Theme tags (legend) тАФ a tag may be used only if it appears here (B638)

Add a new tag to this legend **in the same commit** you first use it (this prevents tag sprawl; CI's `build-backlog-index --check` fails on an off-legend tag):

`#persistence` `#gis` `#gantt` `#export` `#site-planner` `#doc-review` `#scheduler` `#selection` `#pond` `#drive` `#testing` `#ui` `#markup` `#infra` `#auth` `#perf` `#files` `#compare` `#stitching` `#yield` `#filing` `#library` `#road` `#coordinates` `#thoroughfare` `#entitlements` `#floodplain` `#grading`

### Item template

<pre>
### B### тАФ &lt;title&gt; `[Module]` (bug|feature|task) #tag1 #tag2  *(provenance note)*
`[ ]` &lt;one-line summary&gt;
- Verify: sandbox            # or `live` тАФ see the mandatory-live classes above
- Origin: filed &lt;date&gt; from chat   # only when filed from a pasted chat item
- &lt;detailsтАж&gt;
</pre>

---

## ЁЯФ▓ Open

### B826 тАФ Proposed-surface engine: auto-grade the concept from FFE + rules, then earthwork balance and mitigation priced off the real surface `[Site Planner / grading ┬╖ yield]` (feature) #site-planner #grading #yield #floodplain  *(owner 2026-07-14 тАФ "get it to auto consider that"; minted **B826**; concretizes the `docs/ROADMAP.md` "Tier 2: earthwork / cut-fill, soils" tier тАФ the soils half stays unscoped)*
`[ ]` v1 = screening planes, not a TIN. NO proposed-surface / auto-grade / cut-fill engine exists in src/ today (audited). **HARD dependencies, all currently unshipped:** **B808** (Open тАФ the existing-grade lattice; its site-extent grid helper is itself new work), **B809** (Open тАФ the cell-overlay renderer; nothing renders cells yet), **B825** (the grading records this engine consumes), plus **B822**'s auto-engineered ponds as cut. Sequence after those seams exist.
- Verify: live (real-project-data repro + zoom-/data-density-dependent rendering + mitigation parity)
- Origin: filed 2026-07-14 from chat ("NEW-7")
- **(a) Auto elevation model per element:** pad flat at FFE (B805 seed); dock/court breaks тИТ`dockDrop` (the B713 setting) then slopes per the B825 records; paving anchors to pad at the building edge (threshold tie тЙИ pad тИТ 0.15тА▓), field allowed to float lower (see balance assist), slope + direction auto тАФ direction toward the drainage target (detention pond / outfall low side; the **B705 flow field is a HINT only** тАФ `flowField.js` holds per-tile pure fns (`d8Direction`/`flowArrows`) computed for the current map view, there is NO persisted site-wide queryable flow field and flow accumulation is explicitly future work, so the primary derivation is the pond/outfall target), clamped to the class's min/max; landscape transitions tie to existing at the parcel line (3:1/4:1), NO fill across the PL.
- **(b) Composite proposed grid** on the same lattice as the B808 existing grid тЖТ cut/fill map as a second mode of the B809 overlay renderer (diverging ramp, same engine-truth rule: render the cells that priced) тЖТ **Yield earthwork rows EXTEND B712's already-shipped "Earthwork cost (screening)" section** (`SitePlanner.jsx:10254-10293`, `prices.earthworkCy` тАФ pond excavation + mitigation cut CY already price there): cut CY, fill CY, net import/export with a shrink/swell input (labeled screening). Not a parallel earthwork surface; preserve B804's remembered-state handling.
- **(c) Balance assist:** suggest the uniform paving-field raise/lower (within threshold-tie and slope constraints) that nets the dirt closest to zero тАФ one chip, one click to apply.
- **(d) Mitigation upgrade:** floodplain fill = proposed тИТ existing, clipped to zones and the governing WSE, replacing the flat-pad `depthAt` closure (`floodplainMitigation.js:508`) when a proposed surface exists (the flat-pad path stays as the pre-grading fallback, labeled); ponds (B822) participate as cut.
- **(e) Violation flags:** ADA >2% in accessible areas, paved cells under min grade (ponding), PL fill encroachment, dock-approach slope breaks тАФ each one line + тУШ per the B823 cap.
- Terminology guard: pond volume math is `detentionStorage` average-end-area slab integration (`pondGeom.js:170`), not prismoidal.
- Acceptance (live): Bain тАФ the auto surface generates with zero typing; earthwork rows + cut/fill overlay render and tie out; mitigation volume shifts from flat-pad to surface basis with the basis labeled; forcing a 3% accessible stall trips the ADA flag.
- **Session note 2026-07-14:** B825 (grading records) and B822 (auto-engineered ponds as cut) shipped this session, so two of the four seams now exist. Still HARD-blocked on open **B808** (site-extent existing-grade grid) and **B809** (cell-overlay renderer) тАФ building the engine on the site MEDIAN would price earthwork dishonestly on sloped sites (the exact flat-grade lie B808 retires). Next session: build B808 тЖТ B809 тЖТ this.

### B808 тАФ Mitigation volumes integrate per-cell 3DEP grade (retire the single centroid-line median) `[Site Planner / yield ┬╖ floodplain]` (feature) #site-planner #yield #floodplain #gis  *(owner-dropped 2026-07-13 as "NEW-2"; minted **B808**)*
`[ ]` `computeMitigation`'s depth callback is a zero-arg closure over ONE grade тАФ `depthAt = () => Math.max(0, Math.min(wse, pad) - grade)` (`lib/floodplainMitigation.js:493`) тАФ even though `gridIntersect` already invokes it WITH each cell's point (`:137`). And today's "grade" is weaker than a site median: the median of a 9-sample 3DEP line (~230 ft) through the LARGEST parcel's centroid (`sampleGround`, `SitePlanner.jsx:6175-6181` тЖТ `drainCtxData.groundElevFt`). On sites with relief (Bain's corridor falls toward the creek) that single number materially mis-prices fill.
- Verify: live (GIS endpoint + data-density class; note V243's existing-grade expectation needs updating once gradeBasis=grid ships).
- Origin: filed 2026-07-13 from chat ("NEW-2"); upgrades a designed-in limitation of the B707 engine (its spec deliberately chose manual override > the drainage ctx's 3DEP median), surfaced via B712.
- **DEM grid:** fetch a site-extent bare-earth grid via the B704 plumbing тАФ the pure pieces are ready and worker-safe (`lib/demGrid.js`: `gridRequest` / `decodeGrid` (LERC тЖТ survey-ft NAVD88 with validity mask) / `maskedSmooth` / `sampleAtLatLng`; `terrainWorker.js`), but the fetch orchestration (`fetchGridBytes`/`computeTile`) is module-private to `terrainLayers.js` and map-tile-keyed тАФ a small site-extent fetch helper is NEW work (compose gridRequest+fetch+decodeGrid, or export/refactor). One grid, cached; site-feet тЖТ mercator transform helper.
- **Depth:** `depthAt(pt) = max(0, min(wse, padAt(fp)) тИТ demAt(pt))`; void cells excluded + counted тАФ LOUD-FAILURE if >5% of intersect cells are void.
- **AO design point:** the AO path derives WSE as `grade + z.aoDepthFt` (`floodplainMitigation.js:449`) тАФ decide whether AO WSE goes per-cell too (`demAt(pt) + depth`) or stays median; settle it in the close-out.
- **Fallback:** the median stays as the explicit fallback when the grid is unavailable тАФ result carries `gradeBasis: "grid" | "median"` (extend the existing `elev.sources` provenance idiom, `sources.existGrade 'manual'|'3dep'` at `SitePlanner.jsx:6413`) and the ledger labels the median case ("flat-grade estimate"). Manual `existGradeFt` entry still overrides everything (flat-grade mode, labeled) тАФ that path already works (`SitePlanner.jsx:6400`), keep it.
- **Delta flag:** surface when grid-based volume differs from median-based by >15% тАФ those are the sites where the old number was silently wrong.
- **Retention (feeds B809):** per-cell results retained per footprint├Чzone тАФ today `gridIntersect` returns only `{ areaSf, sumDepthArea }` and discards the cells (cap `maxCells` 1500 / `minCellFt` 2, `floodplainMitigation.js:118-119`) тАФ same array, no recompute.
- **Unit tests:** synthetic tilted-plane DEM where the closed-form volume is known; void-cell exclusion; fallback labeling.
- **Acceptance (live):** a sloped test fixture prices тЙа median-mode and matches closed form within tolerance.

### B809 тАФ Fill-depth heat map overlay: render the exact cells the engine priced `[Site Planner / yield ┬╖ ui]` (feature) #site-planner #yield #floodplain #ui #export  *(owner-dropped 2026-07-13 as "NEW-3"; minted **B809**; the "don't trust numbers on a screen" layer)*
`[ ]` Owner requirement: visual verification of what the tool thinks is being filled and mitigated тАФ no unverifiable scalar. Non-negotiable design principle: the overlay renders B808's retained cell array тАФ the same cells and depths that summed to the ledger volume, never a parallel computation тАФ so picture and number cannot diverge (the PDF-PARITY discipline applied to pixels). HARD dependency on B808: today `gridIntersect` discards cells and returns only aggregates (`lib/floodplainMitigation.js:117-143`), so there is nothing to render yet.
- Verify: live (zoom-/data-density-dependent rendering + PDF/export parity тАФ both LIVE-VERIFY classes).
- Origin: filed 2026-07-13 from chat ("NEW-3"); extends the B712 surfacing (which has NO map overlay or exhibit of the priced cells) over the B707 engine.
- **Overlay:** layers-panel toggle, default ON while the Yield mitigation section is open; cells colored by fill depth (sequential ramp, ~0.5 ft bins, legend in ft); zone-class distinguished тАФ floodway (`cls === "floodway"`) renders as hard-prohibited hatch, never a depth color. The cells live in SITE FEET, so the natural surface is the planner SVG canvas z-anchored like B739's composited layers (`buildExportSvg`, `SitePlanner.jsx:7123`), not a Leaflet layer; panel-toggle precedents: TERRAIN contours/flowdir (`lib/layers.js:233-244`) and the B753 corridor (`pipelineCorridor` + `vectorOverlay`).
- **Hover:** a cell тЖТ depth, WSE (with provider tag incl. DRAFT), grade source (grid/median), cell area; a footprint тЖТ its subtotal ac-ft.
- **Tie-out:** a readout chip pins the overlay total against the B712 card/ledger number тАФ identical by construction (same retained array) тАФ render both so the user SEES the tie-out.
- **UNKNOWN:** the engine's honest UNKNOWN bands render as grey diagonal hatch with the reason тАФ "not priced" is visible geography, not absence.
- **Print/export (PDF-PARITY):** the mitigation exhibit joins the sheet with legend + totals тАФ `buildExportSvg` compositing (B739/B745 precedent, LOUD `warnDroppedOverlays`) + `buildPrintSheetSvg`/`printSheetLayout` (`lib/printSheet.js`; B712 already put the mitigation summary in the print metricPairs).
- **Perf:** cells are already тЙд1500/footprint├Чzone тАФ draw to one canvas layer, re-render only on check/input change (ride the `mitigationForFootprint` LRU memo, `SitePlanner.jsx:652-684`).
- **Acceptance (live):** Bain тАФ overlay total equals ledger to the displayed precision; floodway hatch matches the NFHL floodway; toggling inputs (manual BFE) recolors and re-ties.

### B810 тАФ Terrain honesty: provenance line + structure-masked flow arrows + canopy/vintage disclosure `[Site Planner / terrain ┬╖ GIS]` (feature) #site-planner #gis #ui #export  *(owner-dropped 2026-07-13 as "NEW-4"; minted **B810**)*
`[ ]` Owner-reported: drainage arrows render on rooftops of existing buildings тАФ the bare-earth DEM under a structure is interpolated (no ground returns), so an arrow there asserts confidence the data lacks; same concern class for tree canopy (sparse ground returns тЖТ interpolated, though NOT treetop elevations тАФ 3DEP is a bare-earth DTM, already the right source).
- Verify: live (zoom-/data-density-dependent rendering + GIS endpoint; the mask must also hold in the PDF/PNG export тАФ B745/V259, PDF-PARITY).
- Origin: filed 2026-07-13 from chat ("NEW-4"); extends B705 (arrows) + B706 (hover readout), rides the B704 pipeline.
- **(a) Provenance, everywhere elevations surface** (hover readout, contours/arrows тУШ, the mitigation grade row, print sheet): "USGS 3DEP bare-earth LiDAR (trees/structures removed) ┬╖ ~1 m ┬╖ flight vintage &lt;year&gt; ┬╖ NAVD88 survey ft". This UPGRADES existing partial disclosure, not net-new: unify `GROUND_EL_TITLE` (`components/useGroundElevation.js:61-62`, already says "USGS 3DEP LiDAR bare-earth, NAVD88"), the relief/contour layer `note`s (`lib/layers.js:226,236`), and `LAYER_VINTAGE.contours` (`layers.js:369`, today a static "varies by county" string). Resolve vintage via the 3DEP metadata/identify endpoint per site if cheap (nothing fetches it today), else a registry-documented regional note тАФ ride the B236/B760 vintage plumbing (`layerVintage` тЖТ LayerPanel/RowInfo тУШ). Explicitly state grades are pre-construction where the flight predates site work тАФ the correct basis for existing grade; say so, don't hide it.
- **(b) Structure mask for arrows:** skip flow-arrow lattice points inside existing-building footprints. Today `flowArrows` (`lib/flowField.js:47-70`) suppresses only on the DEM validity mask + `minSlope` (default 0.0008 ft/ft) тАФ zero footprint awareness тАФ and NO site/GIS geometry reaches the terrain path (`syncOverlayLayers` gets only onStatus/onError, `SitePlanner.jsx:1762`), so a mask must be plumbed into the worker job or `renderArrows` (`terrainLayers.js:168`). Footprint source: no building layer exists in `GIS_SOURCES`/`ALL_LAYERS`/`vectorLayers` тАФ Microsoft Global ML Building Footprints would be net-new, but the existing `kind:"overpass"` OSM plumbing (osm_power/osm_hydrants, `layers.js:145,158`) is ready-made for OSM buildings; registry entry + coverage fixtures + cache; county-gated rollout is fine (Texas first). Masked points optionally render a faint dot ("interpolated ground") instead of an arrow; hover readout over a masked footprint carries an "interpolated under structure" tag.
- **(c) Canopy:** no per-pixel canopy flag exists in the DEM service тАФ keep `maskedSmooth` (`demGrid.js:148`) + the `minSlope` refusal ("Ground too flat to call"), and put the interpolation caveat in the provenance тУШ rather than inventing a confidence layer; if NDVI/canopy raster masking ever justifies itself, log it separately.
- **(d)** Arrows stay OFF the planner's drawn (proposed) buildings too тАФ proposed pads have their own designed drainage, same rooftop-arrow objection; needs the same mask plumbing as (b).
- **Degradation (LOUD-FAILURE):** a mask-source outage degrades to today's behavior with an honest note тАФ never blocks arrows entirely.
- **Acceptance (live):** Bain + one Harris site тАФ no arrows over existing structures; provenance line renders in hover тУШ and on the sheet.

### B778 тАФ Tighten the migrated `planar_*` tables off wide-open anon RLS `[Infra / Scheduler]` (task) #infra #scheduler #auth  *(spun out of the B408 consolidation on merge, 2026-07-11; minted **B778**)*

That was safe parity while the Scheduler lived on its own disposable project; now those tables sit in the same production project as real user data, so the same-shaped exposure carries more weight even though behavior hasn't changed.
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-11, follow-up flagged in `docs/REFERENCE.md` "## Supabase" during the B408 consolidation (PR #591).
- **Why not folded into B408 itself:** the Scheduler currently has no sign-in / auth of its own тАФ it talks to PostgREST straight with the anon key. Locking the policies to authenticated/owner-scoped access needs the Scheduler to grow an auth layer first (who's allowed to write, and how do they prove it) тАФ real feature work, not a one-line policy flip.
- **Scope when picked up:** decide what "authorized" means for the Scheduler (piggyback on B406's team auth? a simpler shared secret? per-user rows?), rewrite the `planar_*` RLS policies to match, and repoint `public/sequence/index.html`'s client accordingly.

### B776 тАФ Special-district layers: ESD, TIRZ (+ audit LID/FWSD coverage of the TCEQ row) `[Site Planner / GIS]` (feature) #site-planner #gis  *(owner review 2026-07-11 as "NEW-6"; ┬зB2. - Verify: live тАФ Origin: filed 2026-07-11 from chat (owner NEW-6). Not a duplicate of B177/B178 (tax rate/choropleth) тАФ this adds the boundary substrate those need.

### B777 тАФ Subsidence district boundaries (HGSD + Fort Bend SD) `[Site Planner / GIS]` (feature) #site-planner #gis  *(owner review 2026-07-11 as "NEW-7"; ┬зB3. RENUMBERED B766тЖТ**B777** on merge-in of `origin/main` (concurrent floodplain/detention session took B763тАУB773). **LIVE sources found + verified this session тАФ implementation-ready (no static-geometry fallback needed).**)*
`[ ]` Harris-Galveston and Fort Bend Subsidence District regulatory areas as a small Jurisdictions overlay ("Subsidence districts") тАФ they govern groundwater-well permitting/fees, which matters whenever MUD/city service is in doubt. **Sources verified live via the sandbox proxy this session (the official HGSD AGOL org, `services8.arcgis.com/7yRcAUzp7kyx5Z0i`), both CORS `*`:**
- **HGSD:** `HGRegAreas/FeatureServer` тАФ the regulatory areas, but as **3 separate layers** (0/1/2 = HG_Area1/Area2/Area3), field `District`. The multi-layer shape needs a small vector-tier enhancement (query + union layers 0тАУ2) OR three rows; the district OUTLINE = their union (Harris + Galveston).
- **FBSD:** `Fort_Bend_Regulatory_Areas/FeatureServer/0` тАФ a **clean single layer, 6 areas** (FB_Area_AтАжF), field `NAME`. Drop-in via the standard recipe.
- Owner-approved static-geometry fallback is NOT needed (live services exist). тУШ: what they regulate (groundwater-well permitting/fees), why a developer cares, source + vintage. District outline is the requirement; the area subzones are the nice-to-have (these services already carry them). Coverage check: HGSD Area 3 over a Harris parcel.
- Verify: live тАФ Origin: filed 2026-07-11 from chat (owner NEW-7).

### B752 тАФ Pipeline layer: crisp vector rendering + commodity styling + click-identify (replace raster at working zoom) `[Site Planner / GIS]` (feature) #site-planner #gis #export  *(owner-dropped 2026-07-10 as "NEW-1"; minted **B752** = highest B# across both files (B751) + 1 on merge-in of `origin/main`, which took B751/V264 for the drainage-check feature тАФ the code/tests/commit/branch (`claude/pipeline-vector-rendering-2kfnn2`) keep the provisional **B751** label. тЖТ V265. `[ ]` The pipeline overlay rendered as a flat raster and pixelated on zoom. Repro: enable Pipelines, zoom to parcel level over a Houston-MSA site тЖТ grainy lines; zoom out тЖТ pixel blocks. Expected: crisp vector polylines at working zoom (matching the FEMA/NWI vectors), colored by commodity.
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-10 from chat (owner NEW-1)
- **Rendering path (reuse, don't reinvent):** registered pipelines as a `VECTOR_SOURCES.txrrc_pipe` row (`vectorLayers.js`) reusing the `sources.js` `pipelines` metadata (RRC `RRC_Public_Viewer_Srvs/MapServer` layer 13; fields operator/commodity/diameter/status/system/county). Real polyline geometry pulled via `/query`, drawn locally on the `gisCache.js` SWR cache + geometry-simplify tiers exactly like FEMA/NWI. `decideVectorOrImage` gates it: **vector when zoomed in (site/neighborhood level), raster when zoomed far out** (statewide density too heavy for vector). The existing `txrrc_pipe` `/export` layer was **repointed (not deleted) to `imageFallback`** for the far-out case.
- **Commodity styling (FINAL тАФ owner-approved 2026-07-10):** each centerline styled by commodity with **fixed map-symbology hex** (consistent on the aerial regardless of app theme, like the hardcoded `hifld_tx` EVIDENCE colors), NOT palette tokens. **Weight encodes hazard/consequence** (not diameter тАФ diameter surfaces in the click-identify). **Dash is a second signal** so classes survive grayscale/colorblind. Six buckets (`pipelineCommodity.js`): HVL `#E24B4A` solid w4 ┬╖ Natural gas `#EF9F27` solid w3 ┬╖ Crude oil `#7F77DD` solid w3 ┬╖ Refined products `#1D9E75` dash `10 6` w3 ┬╖ COтВВ `#378ADD` dash `9 5 2 5` w2.5 ┬╖ Unknown `#9a9992` dash `5 5` w2. Salience tracks hazard (HVL loudest).
- **Commodity crosswalk тАФ MUST be reconciled against real data at live-verify (V265).** Built a keyword crosswalk on `COMMODITY_DESCRIPTION` тЖТ the six buckets (blank/unmatched тЖТ gray unknown). The distinct-values query can't run from the sandbox (RRC host off the egress allowlist), so `gis-verify/pipeline-commodity-distinct-verify.mjs` runs it live and reports any value that lands in `unknown`. **High-hazard outliers** (hydrogen, anhydrous ammonia) are pre-routed to the **red HVL style, labeled by true commodity in the identify** (owner-approved candidate тАФ salience keeps tracking hazard, never buried in gray); confirm/adjust once the real distinct values are seen.
  - Adversarial-review hardening (same session): the crosswalk now also covers **condensate** (lease/gas condensate тЖТ **crude**, a deliberate crude-vs-HVL screening call to confirm live), **olefins/diolefins** (butadiene, butylene, isobutylene, isoprene тЖТ HVL), **NGL plurals** (pentanes/butanes/"pentanes plus"), **natural gasoline** (тЖТ HVL, not refined), and the bare **"PRODUCTS"** refined-group label тАФ real Texas commodities that previously fell to gray or the wrong bucket.
- **Free wins from going vector:** click-identify popup (operator ┬╖ commodity ┬╖ diameter ┬╖ status); six-class on-map legend (LayerPanel). The screening note ("RRC T-4 permit routes тАФ schematic, not surveyed locations") + data-age stamp stay visible so the sharper render never implies survey accuracy.
- **Dedupe/reconcile:** extends **B739**+**B745** (pipelines in the PDF/export path) тАФ the export composites the SAME vector geometry+styling in vector mode and the `imageFallback` raster in far-out mode (PDF-PARITY); and **B517** (the RRC source repoint) тАФ same authoritative statewide host, no fork.
- V265 covers: RRC host live + CORS; the zoom-dependent rasterтЖФvector switch; distinct-values crosswalk reconciliation + outlier check; click-identify fields; export parity.

### B741 тАФ Orphaned / misfit selection handles on angled elements `[Site Planner]` (bug) #site-planner #selection #ui  *(owner-dropped 2026-07-09 as "NEW-2"; provisional **B735**, renumbered **B741** тАФ concurrent `main` took B734тАУB739. - Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-09 from chat (owner NEW-2)
- Expected: exactly one clean set of handles hugging the selected element's real footprint, no leftover handles from the prior selection, rotation stem anchored to the box edge.
- Hypotheses to confirm live (likely a combo): **A тАФ stale handle layer** (previous selection's handles not cleared before the new selection draws). **B тАФ upright box around an angled shape** (handles from an axis-aligned box instead of an oriented box that follows the polygon's angle). **C тАФ rotation-stem placement** (stem "up" in screen space, not normal to the rotated box's top edge).
- **Concrete lead found in code (AUDIT-FIRST):** the SINGLE-select handle path is already OBB-correct тАФ `handleNodes`/`elSelOutline` derive corners from `elCorners`/`rot2` at the element's own `rot`. The AABB-ignores-rotation defect lived only in the **multi-select** box (`featBBox`), and that path is fixed by **B740** (per-member rotation-aware OBB outlines + single-grip suppression). So the reported *single*-select misfit needs a live repro to pin the true cause (A vs C, or a polygon-vs-rect representation issue) before touching the single-select path.
- **DEDUPE-FIRST:** related to **B740** (multi-select visuals, this batch) and **B569** (multi-select infra) тАФ distinct single-select handle bug.

### B735 тАФ AnchoredMenu portal + click-away backdrop can linger over the newly-active workspace when a menu is left open and the user navigates via browser Back/Forward `[App Shell / UI]` (bug) #ui #infra  *(self-discovered 2026-07-09 during the B734 post-merge adversarial review; **B735** = highest B# across both files (B734) + 1)*
`[ ]` Every `AnchoredMenu` consumer with LOCAL open state (the account dropdown, Site Planner rail flyouts + export/print menus, the project breadcrumb, the scheduler toolbar, the team-role menu) can be left `open` and then have its host workspace hidden by the keep-alive render (`display:none`) if the user navigates **without a click** тАФ browser **Back/Forward** or a programmatic hash change. Because the menu renders in a **portal at `document.body`**, and the click-away backdrop (`position:fixed; inset:0`) renders whenever `open===true`, the hidden instance leaves a full-screen (invisible) click-trap тАФ and, since `place()` doesn't re-run on the display flip so `pos` stays stale-truthy, the menu itself can even render at its stale position тАФ hanging over the newly-active workspace until one click / Esc dismisses it. Rare and self-recovering, but a real UX trap.
- Verify: live (timing / nav-interaction + keep-alive multi-instance class; the fix touches shared infra used by ~20 menus, so it needs a cross-consumer live pass тАФ open each menu type, hit browser Back, confirm nothing lingers and nothing else regressed).
- Origin: found 2026-07-09 during the B734 post-merge review (the B734 fix тАФ self-contained per-instance `AccountControl` тАФ surfaced it; the account dropdown itself is already handled, see below).
- **Partial fix already shipped (B734 follow-up):** `AccountControl` closes its own dropdown on `hashchange` (fires on every nav incl. Back/Forward), so the ACCOUNT menu тАФ the most-reachable instance, present in every header тАФ no longer lingers. This item covers the REMAINING consumers.
- **Correct shared fix (the real job):** in `AnchoredMenu`, make placement re-run when the anchor's box changes to zero (a `ResizeObserver`/`IntersectionObserver` on the anchor, or re-measure each render while open) **and** clear a stale position тАФ change `if (p) setPos(p)` to `setPos(p)` so a null (unmeasurable/`display:none` anchor) result HIDES the menu instead of leaving the last position; optionally gate the backdrop on `pos` (backdrop iff visible). Watch the perf cost of per-render re-measuring across the ~20 consumers (getBoundingClientRect forces layout) тАФ hence the live pass.
- **DEDUPE-FIRST:** net-new. Relatives (not dupes): B734 (the corner-anchor fix + `placeMenu`; this is a different symptom тАФ lingering-after-nav, not mis-anchored-on-open) ┬╖ B127 (built `AnchoredMenu`).

### B725 тАФ Auto-generated entitlement issues from thoroughfare-plan exposure `[Site Planner / entitlements]` (feature) #thoroughfare #entitlements #site-planner  *(filed 2026-07-08 from chat, provisional NEW-6; epic B720тАУB726)*

### B663 тАФ ONE-TIME migration: every existing project gets the standard tree + existing files move into their tree folders in Drive `[Library / storage]` (task тАФ owner-requested migration) #library #drive  *(owner 2026-07-05 тАФ "i want all the existing projects to have this folder structure, this can be a one time migration. also go ahead and place the existing files in appropriate folders"; first minted **B660**, RENUMBERED to **B663** on the same merge-in as B662; **B663** = B662 + 1; branch `claude/planyr-folder-drive-sync-0k8h0t`)*

- **Per project:** idempotent template seed (`ensureSeeded`, existing) тЖТ chunked Drive mirror (`syncFoldersToDrive`, B662) тЖТ **chunked FILE moves**: the server pages the caller's `drive_files` keys (`idStore.listByPrefix`), parses each `<uid>/project-<pid>/<discipline>/<name>` key (`parseFiledKey` тАФ the stored key already carries project + discipline, so NO review records are opened), resolves the tree target through the SAME shared resolver uploads use (now slug-tolerant: `site-plans` тЙб "02. Site Plans"), reads the file's current Drive parents (`driveClient.parentsOf`) and **re-parents in place by file id** (names, share links, read-back untouched тАФ downloads resolve by id). `migrateFilesToTree` in `server/storage/folderMirror.js`; `/api/folders action:"migrate-files"` (8 files/request); client loops (`migrateProjectFiles` / `migrateAllProjects` in `library/lib/folders.js`).
- **Safety:** idempotent end-to-end (already-in-tree files skip on a cheap parents check тЖТ safe to re-run; the once-per-account marker `planyr:treeMigrateV1:<uid>` only avoids waste); `project-unfiled/тАж` holding-area files are deliberately NOT moved (no auto-guess); a file whose tree folder isn't mirrored yet stays put (skipped, counted); per-file errors carry real text and don't stop the rest.

- **ЁЯФН Adversarially reviewed (2026-07-05, 2 dimensions ├Ч verify): 14 findings CONFIRMED (deduped to 8 root causes), all addressed same-session.** The theme: the migration must NEVER write its permanent done-marker over a false success, and one bad file must never wedge the rest. Fixed: (1-HIGH) a blipped `drive_files` page read returned `[]` = "end of list" тЖТ the walk reported COMPLETE + wrote the marker with files never moved тАФ `listByPrefix` now returns null and the chunk fails loudly; (2-HIGH) a transiently-failed/empty project list wrote the marker over "All 0 projects organized" тАФ zero projects now writes NO marker and claims nothing; (3-HIGH) one poisoned file 502'd its chunk and every retry died at the same spot тАФ per-file errors now ride along (chunk stays ok, cursor advances, final report lists them) and a dangling mapping (Drive 404) self-heals by deleting the stale row; (4) a skipped file-phase after a successful mirror no longer counts as success; (5) the per-instance run guard blocked a second ACCOUNT on the same mounted Library тАФ now per-uid; (6) the round cap could restart at 0 forever тАФ replaced with a stall guard + a 500-round backstop; (7) an account switch mid-run stops the walk and blocks the marker write (identity pinned start-to-finish); (8) the signed-out skip message no longer masquerades as "Drive isn't connected".
> **Dedup:** the execution of B662's "migrate PRE-tree uploads" follow-on + the all-projects scaffold backfill in one owner-requested pass. Reuses the B662 resolver/chunk-loop/endpoint patterns wholesale тАФ no parallel system.

### B662 тАФ Unified Library: the folder tree IS the view, and files live inside it (+ the live-502 chunked Drive sync fix) `[Library / Doc Review / storage]` (feature + bug тАФ B650 follow-on) #library #drive #persistence  *(owner-dropped 2026-07-05 with a live 502 screenshot on the first real seed тАФ "it's already breaking тАж let's wire them together тАж folders should be the primary view тАж I don't know that I even need a file view"; first minted **B659**, RENUMBERED to **B662** on merge-in of `origin/main` тАФ a concurrent session took B659 (sheet-reader revamp) + B658 (landing copy) + V212/V213; **B662** = highest real B# across both files (B661, the re-renumbered parcel item) + 1; branch `claude/planyr-folder-drive-sync-0k8h0t`)*

Errors now surface as **real text + a Retry**, never a naked status code (LOUD-FAILURE). The owner floated *"maybe the file view should just be the Review module"* тАФ resolved as: Review keeps "open one drawing + mark up"; the Library keeps browsing/filing, now tree-first. lint 0 ┬╖ 2,551 tests ┬╖ build green ┬╖ logged-out E2E smoke on the unified surface.
- **Follow-ons (small, filed not lost):** physically move a demoted (superseded) file's Drive object to `02. Archive` when it's replaced (display already correct); ~~migrate PRE-tree uploads' bytes into the tree~~ **DONE тАФ B663** (the owner asked for it same-day); drop-onto-a-selected-folder manual filing; **folder-delete тЖТ optional file-RECORD cascade** (today the modal says truthfully that entries re-shelve under Drawings and stay until deleted individually тАФ trashed Drive files remain openable by id, so nothing breaks; a real cascade needs keep-bytes-in-trash delete semantics, deliberately NOT bolted on same-session); **cross-tab sync race** (two TABS mirroring the same fresh project can still double-create empty folders тАФ the in-tab race is closed by the single-flight below; full fix = a conditional drive_id persist in the RPC that lets the loser roll back its duplicate).
- **ЁЯФН Adversarially reviewed (2026-07-05, 3 dimensions ├Ч verify): 8 findings CONFIRMED, all addressed same-session:** (1-HIGH) a blipped `project_folders` read returned `[]` тЖТ empty plan тЖТ **false "Mirrored to Google Drive"** тАФ `list()` now returns null and every consumer (sync / plan-delete / migrate) fails LOUDLY; (2) overlapping sync loops double-created Drive folders тАФ per-project **single-flight with a trailing re-run** (edits mid-pass are never lost); (3) **refile now moves the Drive bytes** to the confirmed discipline (`file-move` action + `moveKeyToTree`; failure тЖТ a visible amber notice, and the B663 migration **respects any in-tree placement** so it can't yank a refiled file back); (4) folder-delete's entry-lingering made explicit in the modal + filed as the cascade follow-on above; (5) server folder reads now carry `sort_order` so server/client resolve identical sibling order; (6) deleting the selected folder no longer strands a ghost selection (sanitize effect); (7) free-typed unicode disciplines can't crash the upload fetch (`headerSafe`); (8) folder-rail clicks exit the Needs-filing view.
> **Dedup:** B650's own follow-on (fold-in, not a new system) тАФ reuses its resolver/mirror/store end-to-end. The unified view REPLACES the B650-era Files/Folders tabs and generalizes **B496**'s Library surface; **B180**'s "folders are saved views" survives as the facet chips + cross-project browse over the same list. Auto-filing (**B312**/B299/B411) is UNCHANGED тАФ it still picks the discipline; the tree is now where its decision lands. Upload paths (**B409** resumable + B207 multipart) both target the tree.

### B650 тАФ Per-project standard folder tree, user-editable in-app, with continuous one-way sync to Google Drive `[Doc Review / Library / storage ┬╖ drive-integration / persistence]` (feature тАФ umbrella, multi-phase)  *(owner brief 2026-07-04, arrived as "NEW-1"; first filed **B645**, RENUMBERED to **B650** on merge-in of `origin/main` тАФ PR #493 took B645тАУB649 for the backlog-infra + persistence-epic batch; **B650** = highest real B# across both files (B649) + 1. The code/tests/branch keep the same feature but all self-references were bumped B645тЖТB650. Branch `claude/planyr-folder-drive-sync-0k8h0t`. Deduped against the Drive / storage-adapter / auto-filing / file-index cluster тАФ this FOLDS INTO the existing storage adapter + Supabase file-index rather than adding a parallel one; see the **Dedup** note.)*
`[ ]` Give every Planyr project a standard folder tree the user can edit in-app (**add / rename / move / delete** folders), and mirror that structure **continuously** into the user's Google Drive so the two never drift. **Planyr is the source of truth (authoritative); Drive is a live mirror that follows every structural change.**
> **тЬЕ CODE SHIPPED this session (branch `claude/planyr-folder-drive-sync-0k8h0t`) тАФ lint 0 ┬╖ 2,484 tests (53 new) ┬╖ build green ┬╖ logged-out E2E smoke passing; hardened by an adversarial code review (10 findings found + all fixed: a React remount that broke inline rename, a false-"empty" delete confirmation, a dropped move-under-a-same-pass-create, a create-persist-failure duplicate, a double-seed race, drive_* column-lock, dup-name validation). REMAINING = the signed-in + live-Drive click-through only тЖТ `VERIFICATION.md` V208 (scaffold/template/independence) + V209 (sync-in-place + delete-safety); the owner ran `project_folders.sql` 2026-07-05 (schema verified live in prod тАФ table, RLS ├Ч4, unique index, guard trigger, SECURITY DEFINER RPC all present).** **тЪа Recurrence 2026-07-05 (├Ч1, owner screenshot):** the FIRST real seed hit a live **502** тАФ the one-request mirror died mid-flight at 65/133 folders. Root-caused + FIXED same session as part of **B659** (chunked resumable sync + honest error + progress); see that item. What shipped, end-to-end:
> - **Data model:** `src/workspaces/doc-review/db/project_folders.sql` (own-row RLS; structure columns client-written, `drive_*` mirror columns server-written тАФ disjoint, no conflict).
> - **Canonical template + pure tree logic:** `src/shared/folders/folderTemplate.js` (the exact 133-folder tree) + `folderTree.js` (flatten / treeify / validate / move-cycle guard / `buildSeedRows`).
> - **Client store:** `src/workspaces/library/lib/folders.js` тАФ reads/writes the tree in Supabase (instant, authoritative), idempotent template seed, debounced Drive-sync trigger, graceful signed-out/Drive-off skips.
> - **UI:** `src/workspaces/library/components/FolderTree.jsx` (add / **inline** rename / move / delete + the **enumerated** delete-safety modal + Drive-mirror status), mounted behind a Files/**Folders** tab in `Library.jsx`.
> - **Server mirror (one-way, by stored Drive id):** pure planner `server/storage/folderReconcile.js` + executor `server/storage/folderMirror.js` + REST store `server/storage/folderStoreSupabase.js` + route `functions/api/folders.js`; new `driveClient.createSubfolder` (eager empty folders) + `trash` (recoverable delete). Gated 503 when Drive is off (tree still lives in Supabase тАФ no regression).
> - **Scaffolding hook:** `SitePlannerApp.newSiteFromMap` seeds + syncs on project creation (dynamic import, off the planner chunk); the Folders tab also lazy-seeds on first open (covers blank-then-edited projects).
> - **Delete safety:** non-empty delete тЖТ `plan-delete` enumerates the exact Drive folders + files тЖТ confirm тЖТ soft-delete rows тЖТ mirror moves them to **Drive trash** (recoverable ~30 days), never a silent/permanent wipe.
- **Model тАФ Supabase authoritative, Drive mirrors (REUSE, don't parallelize):**
  - Each project's folder tree lives in **Supabase Postgres as the project's folder index** тАФ the SAME index auto-filing queries against for file facts. Scaffolding, file-drop routing, and structure sync share this one model. Attach it to the existing library index (`doc-review/db/project_library.sql` / `file_facts.sql`), keyed on the project = the Site Planner site-group (`project_id` = `sites.group_id`); a new `project_folders` table (own-row RLS, same pattern as `drive_files.sql`) holds one row per folder with its parent, name, order, and **Drive folder id**. Do NOT spin up a parallel structure.
  - Drive holds a **mirror** of that structure. **Reject the lazy/virtual-only approach** where Drive folders materialize only when a file first lands in them: an empty folder created in Planyr must appear as an **empty folder in Drive, immediately.** тЪа This is a real CHANGE to today's Drive backend, which is **path-keyed + lazy** тАФ `server/storage/backends/driveBackend.js` / `driveClient.js` currently ensure a folder only when a file is put into it, via `client.folderId(folderPath)`. The new work adds **eager folder creation** + **id-keyed reconcile** on top of that same client (below).
  - Sync direction is **one-way, Planyr тЖТ Drive.** Watching Drive for external changes and pulling them back is **out of scope.**
- **Scaffolding on project creation:** when a user creates a project, seed it from **one canonical default template** (below) тАФ auto-create the full empty folder skeleton. Each new project is an **independent copy**: editing it later never touches the template or any other project. Editing the template itself applies to **new projects only** and must **never retroactively restructure existing projects** (same non-silent-mutation discipline used elsewhere тАФ a template edit silently rearranging live projects is the exact failure to avoid).
- **Continuous sync тАФ every structural change reconciles to Drive:** create, rename, move/reparent, and delete of any folder propagates to the Drive mirror.
  - **Store each folder's Drive folder id in the Supabase index and reconcile BY ID, never by path/name.** Rename and move must act on the **existing Drive folder in place** (`driveClient.update(fileId, { addParents, removeParents, name })` тАФ the Drive client already exposes exactly this). тЪа Path-matching creates a NEW folder and orphans the old one on every rename тАФ **do not do this.**
  - All mirrored folders are **app-created**, so this stays within the existing **`drive.file` OAuth scope** (Planyr can only see/touch the files+folders it created тАФ confirmed in `server/storage/README.md`: "the app makes its own `Planyr/тАж` folder tree"). No broader Drive permission is needed.
- **Delete safety (decision made тАФ crash-severity leg):** deleting a Planyr folder that already has synced files removes **real user documents from Drive** тАФ a silent-data-loss risk, the highest-severity bug class. Required behavior:
  - Non-empty deletes are allowed, but only behind a **loud, explicit confirmation that enumerates exactly what will be removed from Drive** тАФ list the files and subfolders that will disappear, so the user never blindly confirms. **Never mirror a destructive delete silently.**
  - **Recommended extra guard (owner to confirm):** mirror the delete as a **move to Drive's trash** (recoverable ~30 days) rather than a permanent delete, so a mistaken confirmation is still recoverable. Confirm **trash vs. hard-delete** with the owner before shipping the delete path.
- **Default template content (finalized тАФ ship EXACTLY this):**
  - Top level, **12 categories** numbered `01.`тАУ`12.`: `01. Hillwood` / `02. Design` / `03. Sustainability` / `04. Governmental` / `05. General Contractor` / `06. Insurance` / `07. Financing` / `08. Land` / `09. Testing Contractor` / `10. Utilities` / `11. Close-Out` / `12. Bldg Acq`.
  - **Subfolders:**
    - **01. Hillwood:** `01. Correspondence` / `02. Project Directory & Invoices` / `03. Development Schedule` / `04. Outline Specifications` / `05. Pursuit Budgets` / `06. Development Budgets` / `07. Financial Models` / `08. Media` / `09. Development Checklist` / `10. DPO - Investment Summary` / `11. Purchase & Sale Agreements` / `12. Ground Lease` / `13. Entity Docs - SPE` / `14. Joint Venture` / `15. Photos` / `16. Legal` / `17. Market Research` / `18. Marketing` / `19. Approvals` / `20. Financing`
    - **02. Design:** `01. Drawings` / `02. Specifications` / `03. Contracts` / `04. Reports & Studies` / `05. Correspondence` / `06. Invoices`
      - **02. Design тЖТ 01. Drawings** holds **9 discipline subfolders:** `01. Exhibits` / `02. Site Plans` / `03. Architectural` / `04. Structural` / `05. Civil` / `06. Landscape` / `07. Mechanical` / `08. Electrical` / `09. Plumbing`. **Each of the 9 contains `01. Current` and `02. Archive`.** (`02. Specifications` is a **sibling** of `01. Drawings`, NOT nested inside it.)
    - **03. Sustainability:** `01. Correspondence` / `02. Contracts` / `03. Scorecards & Budgets` / `04. LEED`
    - **04. Governmental:** `01. Correspondence` / `02. Permits` / `03. Zoning` / `04. DRC Meeting` / `05. Economic Development` / `06. Impact Fees` / `07. Ordinances` / `08. Development Agreement` / `09. Energy Code - COMcheck` / `10. Fire Department` / `11. OpEx` / `12. Taxes - Incentives`
    - **05. General Contractor:** `01. Correspondence` / `02. Preliminary Pricing` / `03. Bids` / `04. Contracts & Change Orders` / `05. Pay Apps & Invoices` / `06. Meeting Minutes` / `07. Schedules` / `08. Safety` / `09. Submittals` / `10. Monthly Reports` / `11. Weather Logs`
    - **06. Insurance:** `01. Builders Risk` / `02. Certs of Insurance` / `03. Factory Mutual`
    - **07. Financing:** `01. Correspondence` / `02. Lender's Inspector` / `03. Draw Requests` / `04. Tax Certs` / `05. Appraisals` / `06. Loan Closing Checklist` / `07. Alternative Financing`
    - **08. Land:** `01. Seller Due Diligence` / `02. CCRs - Park Assoc` / `03. Closing Stmts` / `04. Geotech Rpt` / `05. Environmental` / `06. Wetland - Stream` / `07. Flood Plain - FEMA` / `08. Survey & Legal Descriptions` / `09. Plat & Easements` / `10. Special Warranty Deed` / `11. Title Rev - Commitment` / `12. Ag Lease` / `13. Labor Study`
    - **09. Testing Contractor:** `01. Contract` / `02. Reports`

    - **12. Bldg Acq:** ship as an **empty top-level category** (no subfolders defined).
- **Naming conventions (every level):**
  - **Zero-padded two-digit prefix + period + space** (`01. ` тАж `20. `). Padding is **required, not cosmetic:** clients that sort names as plain text (Drive web, mobile) would otherwise order them `1, 10, 11, тАж 2, 3`. Padding keeps numeric order correct everywhere.
  - **`01. Current` / `02. Archive`** тАФ deliberately NOT "superseded" ("superseded" is the AEC term for a drawing replaced by a newer revision; too much jargon for general users). Numbered so **Current sorts above Archive.**
- **Ship scope / known gaps тАФ do NOT block on these:** ship exactly the folders above. Three categories were only partly visible in source and ship **intentionally short, left user-extensible:** **Land** (14тАУ18 unknown тЖТ ship 01тАУ13), **Close-Out** (11 unknown тЖТ ship 01тАУ10), **Bldg Acq** (contents unknown тЖТ ship empty).
- **Verification (two paths тАФ auth-only/live-Drive, so NOT sandbox-verifiable тЖТ own `V###` entries):**
  1. **Scaffolding + template + per-project independence:** create a project тЖТ confirm the full tree materializes in **both** Planyr and Drive; edit one project's tree тЖТ confirm the template and other projects stay untouched.
  2. **Continuous sync + delete safety:** rename / move / delete folders in Planyr тЖТ confirm Drive mirrors each **in place** (renames don't orphan or duplicate); confirm a non-empty delete triggers the **enumerated confirmation** and (if adopted) lands in **Drive trash.** Live-Drive behavior тАФ verify against a **real connected Drive account**, not the sandbox.
- **Dependencies:** builds on the in-progress Google Drive storage-adapter + Supabase file-index work. **Locate and REUSE the existing storage adapter rather than adding a parallel one.**

### B629 тАФ Drive-backed county PARCEL snapshot cache so outages stop breaking the map `[Site Planner / GIS]` (feature тАФ multi-phase) #site-planner #gis #drive  *(owner-requested 2026-07-03 тАФ "I keep having this [Chambers GIS down] issue тАж cache a copy of the entire Chambers County CAD and just update it тАж same for Fort Bend тАж we've got a Google Drive with 32 gigs"; scope refined to "all except Harris" тЖТ Chambers + Waller + Fort Bend. Minted **B629** = highest real B# across both files (B628) + 1; plan `/root/.claude/plans/okay-um-i-mean-elegant-haven.md`; branch `claude/chambers-county-gis-down-ttqfnv`.)*
`[ ]` **Phase 1 TURNED ON тАФ all three snapshots built, uploaded to Drive, and served by `/api/parcel-cache`.** Only the **V199 live click-through** (real browser on planyr.io) remains before this moves to Done. A lot draws + selects from Planyr's saved copy even with the county server 100% down.
- **UPDATE 2026-07-04 (turn-on + Waller pagination fix):** triggered the nightly builder (`workflow_dispatch`) тАФ Fort Bend **385,212** ┬╖ Chambers **38,293** ┬╖ Waller **48,740** now live on the endpoint (`/api/parcel-cache/svc/<county>?meta=1` тЖТ `cached:true`). Fixing a Waller undercount (26k vs the true ~48.7k) exposed a real paging bug in the county-poly POST leg: the loop broke on the first `batch.length < PAGE` short page, so a transient mid-pull page under 2000 rows ended the pull early and dropped ~half the county. `pageProvider` now pages by the server's OWN `exceededTransferLimit` flag and advances the offset by the rows **actually** returned тАФ so a short page no longer stops it. +3 regression tests (`parcelSnapshotBuilder.test.js`) replaying the exact short-page scenario; full Waller dry-run confirms 48,740. (`pageProvider` made fetch-injectable for the test.)
- **UPDATE 2026-07-04 (B661 тАФ first labeled B650, then B658, renumbered on collisions):** the Chambers/Waller source is fixed. The state parcel `/query` went dark on BOTH hosts (feature.tnris.org 503 ┬╖ feature.geographic.texas.gov 400 "operation not supported" тАФ the B627 outage), so the builder now pulls from the **AGO-hosted StratMap 2025 FeatureServer** (query-enabled, independent host), scoped by the **county polygon** (that layer has no county field). Verified live: Chambers 38,293 ┬╖ Waller 48,741 ┬╖ Fort Bend on FBCAD unchanged. Source-resilient (ordered candidate list + keep-last-good); TxGIO /query kept as a preferred-when-healthy fallback.
- **Why:** Chambers + Waller ride the flaky State/TxGIO service (its `/query` keeps going down тАФ B627); Fort Bend is reliable-source insurance. Measured sizes (compressed): Chambers ~5тАУ10 MB ┬╖ Waller ~5 MB ┬╖ Fort Bend ~76 MB тЖТ ~0.3% of the 32 GB Drive. Harris (1.55 M parcels / ~600 MB) is EXCLUDED (too big for the browser).
- **Architecture (reuses, not parallel systems):** a nightly builder writes a per-county snapshot to a shared `Planyr/parcelcache` Drive folder (same creds + shared-folder pattern as the B445 imagery cache; no new secret, no per-user auth); a read-through Pages Function `functions/api/parcel-cache` serves it (404-on-miss тЖТ client falls back to live); the client loads it into IndexedDB (B474) and feeds it into the EXISTING `optimisticHitAt`/`outerRingsLngLat` click path + a magenta `L.geoJSON` display layer, so no new click logic. Small counties (Chambers/Waller) load whole; Fort Bend is tiled (**Phase 2**, not yet wired).
- **Shipped + verified this session (Phase 1a):** `functions/api/parcel-cache/{[[path]],_handler}.js` (serve; 14 tests) ┬╖ `lib/parcelSnapshot.js` (client loader + IndexedDB SWR; 13 tests) ┬╖ `shared/gis/parcelSnapshotBuild.js` (pure strip+quantize transform; 7 tests) ┬╖ `lib/parcelDisplay.js` `makeSnapshotLayer` ┬╖ `MapFinder.jsx` wiring (warm on select-mode, snapshot display layer, promote-a-cached-hit when live returns nothing, "Cached copy ┬╖ as of <date>" badge + banner) ┬╖ `counties.js` (new **Waller** entry + `SNAPSHOT_COUNTIES`) ┬╖ `scripts/build-parcel-snapshot.mjs` (builder тАФ **dry-run proven against LIVE FBCAD**: 2000 parcels тЖТ strip/quantize тЖТ 0.3 MB gz) ┬╖ `.github/workflows/parcel-snapshot.yml` (nightly cron + @claude-issue-on-failure). lint 0 ┬╖ 2275 tests ┬╖ build green. Safe/inert: `ensureSnapshot` just 404s until a snapshot exists тЖТ identical to today.

Default = leave as-is (numbers already correct).

### B499 тАФ Harden the LOAD-time self-heal for the OTHER bonded children (sidewalk / dock-zone stack / side-parking) `[Site Planner / Site Model]` (task тАФ hardening) #site-planner #persistence  *(spun out of the B498 sweep 2026-06-27; minted **B499**)*
`[ ]` B498 made `createSiteModel` re-flush `dogEar` children to the host's current edge on load. The same stale-edge class could in principle affect the other bonded children if a host is ever resized by a path that skips the live `refitChildren` re-anchor тАФ but **no stale record has been observed** for these (the Jacintoport truck court re-anchored correctly), so this is hardening, not a confirmed live bug.
- **Why deferred (real blocker тАФ would risk load-time churn on CORRECT records):** unlike dog-ears (whose `dogEarGeom` IS the placement fn, so re-deriving a correct bump yields itself тЖТ provably idempotent), the others aren't placed by a single pure function. A sidewalk's stored box is the product of `fitKid` ratio-scaling + sibling pushes + `perpGap` + `sidewalkFullRunPatch`; a dock-zone's of `layoutZoneByKind` + stored `zd` depths + `courtOpts`. Re-running only the pure helper on load could rewrite a correctly-placed element (sub-foot churn тЖТ dirty flag, cloud re-saves, possible visible shift) on every load. Shipping safely needs an idempotency proof across the existing record corpus. **Side-parking** is worse: its live `fitKid` ratio-scales from an OLD-host snapshot that doesn't exist on disk, and there's no pure full-run helper тАФ a model-layer re-anchor would mean porting the stateful wall-kid + rotated-stall layout. Too large to land safely this run.
- **Plan when picked up:** lift `sidewalkFullRunPatch`+`sidewalkSpanForBumps` and `dockZones.layoutZoneByKind`/`relayoutSide` into pure modules the model imports (like `dogEar.js`); add a wall-strip + `normalizeDockZones` pass after the dog-ear re-flush; write idempotency tests that widen a host on-disk-only and assert each child re-flushes flush AND that a correct record returns unchanged (object identity). Add a pure `parkingRowFullRunPatch` (mirror of `sidewalkFullRunPatch`) to fold side-parking into the same pass.

### B495 тАФ Schedule module: instant first paint (stale-while-revalidate local cache) `[Scheduler / perf]` (enhancement, follow-on to B494) #scheduler #perf #persistence  *(surfaced fixing B494 2026-06-27; minted **B495** тАФ renumbered from a provisional B494 after a concurrent `main` took B493 for the cross-module-link feature)*
`[ ]` The embedded scheduler's boot does `await window.storage.get("hs-v1")` тАФ a pure Supabase round-trip with NO local cache (`public/sequence/index.html`) тАФ and `data` stays null (so the shell loader shows) until it resolves. B494 made the loader's READY signal reliable + bounded, but the genuine first-load still waits on that network call. Stale-while-revalidate would make repeat loads near-instant: cache the last-loaded `hs-v1` in localStorage (write it on every successful `get`/`set`), paint from it synchronously on boot so `data` is available immediately, then reconcile against the authoritative cloud read. **Care required (why deferred):** the scheduler has load-bearing concurrency/version guards (`__rev`/`knownRev`/stale-block) and a documented two-tab-fight sensitivity, and it's under active concurrent development тАФ only replace the local view with the cloud read when the user hasn't edited yet (guard the reconcile), and verify it can't lose an in-progress edit or confuse the save guard. Own focused pass.

### B483 тАФ A 100%-full localStorage boots the app signed-out (auth-token refresh write fails) `[Auth / Storage]` (bug тАФ hardening; low real-world risk post-B474) #auth #persistence  *(Cowork signed-in verification 2026-06-26, "NEW-4"; minted **B483** = highest real B# (B482) + 1)*
`[ ]` **Repro:** fill localStorage to a literal ~100% (Cowork's snippet B + a fine-grained top-up), then reload тЖТ the app boots **signed-out** (header "Sign in", empty site list) because Supabase's session-token refresh can't write to a full localStorage. Self-heals once space is freed; data intact.
- **Why low real-world risk now:** B474 moved the heavy rasters off localStorage into IndexedDB, so in real use localStorage sits ~700 KB even with big images тАФ a literal 100%-full localStorage is essentially only reachable by an artificial fill. B473's amber "saved to your account" path itself behaved correctly throughout.
- **Fix (when picked up):** ensure a device-full condition can't drop the auth session тАФ e.g. proactively evict our own large caches (gis cache / history mirror) on a QuotaExceededError to keep headroom for the Supabase auth write, or keep the session in memory so a failed localStorage refresh-write doesn't sign the user out. Deferred (edge + self-healing + low real-world likelihood post-B474); filed for the record.

### B484 тАФ Renderer freezes (~30 s main-thread stalls): PDF title-block reading, heavy map/parcel ops, and panel/rail scrolling (├Ч2) `[Doc Review + Site Planner / perf]` (task тАФ perf) #doc-review #site-planner #perf  *(Cowork signed-in verification 2026-06-26, "NEW-5"; minted **B484**)*
`[ ]` **Observed:** repeated multi-second tab-unresponsive stalls while the Review module reads a dropped PDF's title block on import, and during statewide-parcel selection / map zoom over a new area. Didn't fail a test, but it's a real responsiveness issue (and slowed the signed-in pass).
- Verify: live
- Recurrence: 2026-07-05 тАФ owner repro (chat "NEW-7", DEDUPE-FIRST fold тАФ same ~30 s unpaintable-page symptom, same module): on a **nearly empty plan**, repeatedly scrolling the left panel or right rail intermittently blocks the renderer (page unpaintable 30 s+, DOM still responsive) тАФ hit ~3├Ч in 20 min in Chrome. **New trigger class:** no PDF intake or heavy parcel op in flight, so this points at **scroll-tied paint/layout work (scroll handlers)** тАФ profile that path specifically; it may be a distinct cause sharing the symptom (keep under this ID unless profiling proves otherwise, then spin off with a cross-ref).
- **Cause:** the vector title-block read (pdf.js `extractPageText`/`extractPageItems` + the pure parsers) runs on the MAIN thread on import (OCR for scanned sheets is already in a worker тАФ B352 тАФ but the vector-text path isn't); heavy parcel geometry/render also blocks.
- **Fix (when picked up):** move the PDF title-block read + heavy geometry off the main thread (Web Worker / chunked yielding) per the CLAUDE.md "heavy work off the main thread" rule, so the tab stays responsive during PDF intake and parcel loads. Larger task тАФ deferred, filed.
- **Partial mitigation shipped (B664, 2026-07-05):** the Review rail's sheet scan now reads the ON-SCREEN page first then spirals outward (the label you're looking at fills in immediately on a 50-page set) and yields a macrotask between pages (no long main-thread hog during intake). Remaining when picked up: the Worker offload above + pre-rasterising ADJACENT sheets so a rail jump swaps instantly (the owner's "improve overall speed" ask, 2026-07-05 тАФ the switch currently shows the dimmed previous sheet + an "OpeningтАж" chip until the new raster lands, B660).

### B474 тАФ Move the Site Planner on-device cache off the 5 MB localStorage cap onto IndexedDB `[Site Planner / Persistence]` (enhancement) #site-planner #persistence  *(spun out of B473 Shipment 2, 2026-06-25; owner: "do the best long-term solution now")*
`[~]` Give the on-device cache **gigabytes (IndexedDB)** instead of localStorage's hard ~5 MB. Data-safety is already fixed (B473 Shipment 1: cloud authoritative + dead-store purge + history byte-cap + raster-shed), so this is future-proofing тАФ done carefully, NOT a drop-in swap.
- **`[x]` Stage A (SHIPPED) тАФ version-history ring тЖТ IndexedDB.** The biggest local store (~1.6 MB) and the SAFE one (a one-way backup, never read for cross-tab coordination). New `lib/localDb.js` (promisified IndexedDB kv; no-ops when IndexedDB is unavailable). In `storage.js` the ring is an in-memory cache (`historyMem`, the synchronous source of truth) written through to IndexedDB (uncapped тЖТ undo depth no longer byte-throttled) + a byte-capped localStorage fallback; `initHistoryStore()` (called from `SitePlannerApp`) hydrates + merges + one-time-migrates the old localStorage ring. Public API unchanged + synchronous (`snapshotVersion`/`listVersions`/`getVersion`/`backupNow`). IndexedDB-ABSENT path is byte-for-byte the old behavior тАФ the 1565 existing tests prove it. +6 unit tests (`test/historyIdb.test.js`, fake-indexeddb) ┬╖ lint 0 ┬╖ **1571 tests** ┬╖ build green ┬╖ headless **V139** (`ui-audit/verify-b474-history-idb.mjs`, 7/7: ring lands in IndexedDB + survives reload).
- **`[~]` Stage B тАФ heavy RASTERS тЖТ IndexedDB (the actual cap pressure), NOT the cross-tab-coordinated map.** Investigation (2026-06-26) found the literal sites map is tiny (geometry, kilobytes) and bound to the two-window guard; the thing that fills the cap is the attached IMAGES. So the safe path moves rasters to IndexedDB and leaves the small map + its guard untouched.
  - **`[x]` Underlay raster тЖТ IndexedDB (SHIPPED).** Stashed on drop (`idbPut("raster:<siteId>:underlay", тАж)` in `onUnderlayFile`); the persisted record drops the heavy data-URL `src` via `dropIdbBackedSrc` in `writeSites` (proactive off-cap, conditional on an `idbKey` so non-backed rasters keep `src` тАФ safe), rehydrated on load by a new effect in `SitePlanner.jsx`. Fixes the ONE raster with no recovery path (it used to need a re-drop after a strip). +2 unit tests (`saveFallbackCloud.test.js`) ┬╖ lint 0 ┬╖ **1573 tests** ┬╖ build green ┬╖ headless **V141** (`ui-audit/verify-b474-underlay-idb.mjs`, 7/7: stash тЖТ off-cap record тЖТ rehydrate after reload).
  - **`[x]` sheetOverlays / parcelDrawings тЖТ IndexedDB (SHIPPED).** Stashed on creation (`addOverlayFile` / `addDrawingFromRaster`, keyed `raster:<siteId>:overlay|drawing:<id>`); the rehydrate effects now try **IndexedDB first** (fast, offline) and fall back to cloud Storage (cross-device); `dropIdbBackedSrc` slims them off the cap on persist. +1 unit test; headless **V142** (`ui-audit/verify-b474-overlay-idb.mjs`, 7/7 тАФ overlay stash тЖТ off-cap record тЖТ rehydrate after reload). Drawings share the identical pattern (storage unit-tested; same rehydrate code, parcel-attach path).
  - **`[ ]` The live sites-MAP itself stays on localStorage (deferred).** Its two-window guard (B127/B314) needs synchronous cross-tab visibility + the `storage`-event merge; moving it = a BroadcastChannel rebuild (`src/shared/presence/` тАФ the editor lock already serializes editing) + two-window/signed-in testing. Not worth the risk now that the cap is non-binding тАФ **owner agreed**. Cloud (Supabase) stays the single source of truth.

### B479 тАФ Persistence "state-of-the-art" perf refactors (the deferred tail of the B485 review) `[Site Planner / Persistence]` (enhancement/perf) #site-planner #persistence #perf  *(spun out of the B485 adversarial review, 2026-06-26; renumbered **B478тЖТB479** on merge тАФ a concurrent `main` (#368) took B478 for the resume-into-planner fix; these are the findings the verifiers marked fixNow=false тАФ real but larger/riskier than a same-session patch, NOT data-loss. B485 shipped all the data-loss + honesty fixes.)*
`[ ]` Quality/perf upgrades to the IndexedDB persistence layer. None is a correctness bug; each is a worthwhile optimization once it can be done carefully (its own branch + verification).
- **`[ ]` Per-site IndexedDB history keys, not one full-ring blob (#25/#28).** `writeHistoryAll` JSON-serializes the ENTIRE multi-site version ring to a single IndexedDB key on every snapshot (O(all history) per save). Move to per-site keys (`history:<siteId>`) so each write is O(one site). Medium risk (touches the hydrate/merge/migrate path); needs the fake-indexeddb suite extended.
- **`[ ]` Store rasters as native Blobs, not base64 data-URL strings (#27).** ~33% size + memory overhead + structured-clone cost; Blobs are the idiomatic IndexedDB image store. Requires object-URL lifecycle management (create on read, `revokeObjectURL` on unmount/replace) in the rehydrate effects тАФ the reason it's deferred.
- **`[ ]` Don't let raster rehydration re-fire the autosave/cloud-push (#29).** On reload, `setUnderlay`/`setSheetOverlays` adding `src` back triggers the autosave effect тЖТ a redundant local write (B460's contentSig already suppresses the cloud RE-push, so this is local churn, not loss). Guard rehydrate-driven setState from the edit-driven path.
- **`[ ]` Honest "space left" UI via `StorageManager.estimate()` (#34) + amber self-clear after space is freed (#33).** Today "device full" is only learned by catching QuotaExceededError after a write fails; `navigator.storage.estimate()` could show usage proactively, and the amber "saved to your account" banner could self-clear once space returns instead of waiting for the next edit/Retry.
- **`[ ]` `mergeHistory` dedup by `at`+`sig`, not `at` alone (#32/#35).** Two genuinely-different snapshots sharing one millisecond collapse to one on merge. Tiny, but doing it right also needs `getVersion` to disambiguate same-`at` rows (it currently keys on `at` only) тАФ so it's a small paired change, not a one-liner.
- **`[ ]` In-memory parsed-store cache to kill the per-save `readSites()` re-parse churn (chat 2026-07-11 "NEW-1", DEDUPE folded here тАФ perf, not a bug).** One debounced autosave currently does ~4 full-store `JSON.parse` (`readSites` in `saveSite` + the `loadSite` read-back + a second `saveSite` on the settle tick + `pushSiteToCloud`'s `loadSite`) + 2 full-store stringify, all synchronous, every ~400 ms; the cost scales with total account size, not the edit. (The history-ring **parse** half is already gone тАФ B474's `historyMem` cache; the ring **stringify** on each snapshot remains.) Fix: a parsed-store cache per `sitesKey()` namespace тАФ the writer tab updates it on its own writes and invalidates on `storage` events for the sites keys (events never fire in the writing tab, so the writer's cache stays authoritative тЖТ the B127 stale-write fold is preserved), cleared in `setActiveUser` on user switch. Removes the triple parse with zero format change. Follow-on: per-site keys so a write is O(one site) (couples to the #25/#28 history-key change above). Verify: the B127 fold still triggers when another tab advanced the store (unit).

### B422 тАФ Named markup Layers (show / hide / lock / rename / reorder) `[Doc Review / Markup]` (feature) тАФ ROADMAP STUB, design pass required before build #doc-review #markup  *(owner-dropped 2026-06-23 as "NEW-2"; minted **B422**)*
`[ ]` **PARKED тАФ file only, do NOT build yet (a design pass must land first).** CAD-/Bluebeam-style named layers for the markup surface: group markups into named layers ("Existing", "Demo", "My redlines", "GC's markups"), each with show/hide, lock, rename, delete, and reorder. Distinct from & complementary to the Arrange z-order ops (**B421**, shipped): Arrange controls draw order **within** a layer; Layers organize the whole sheet. Strategic value is organizational тАФ isolate one reviewer's markups, lock an as-built, separate civil from architectural тАФ which maps onto the multi-reviewer / multi-customer direction.
- **Why it can't be a quick handoff (the open design questions):**
  - **Data-model change + migration.** Each markup gains a `layerId`; the review gains a `layers` collection (`id, name, visible, locked, order`). Old saved reviews migrate on load тАФ markups with no `layerId` fold into a default "Markup" layer. Use the existing version-bump + `migrate` discipline (same pattern as the Site Model `SITE_MODEL_VERSION` migrations), not an ad-hoc reshape.
  - **Active-layer concept.** New markups land on the active layer тЖТ needs a clear, always-visible indicator of which that is.
  - **Render + hit-testing.** The render path filters out hidden layers; `hitTest` (B33) must skip markups on hidden OR locked layers so you can't grab what you can't edit.
  - **Arrange interplay.** B421's four reorder ops become "arrange **within** the active layer" тАФ reuse them, don't fork.
  - **New UI surface.** A Layers panel in the right rail (alongside Takeoff); reuse the portal-menu pattern (`AnchoredMenu`/B127) for per-layer menus.
  - **Delete-layer is a "silence is a crash" hazard.** Deleting a layer must force an explicit choice for its markups (reassign to another layer vs. delete with the layer) via a loud confirmation тАФ never silently drop markups.
- **Next step before any code:** a design pass тАФ a Layers-panel mockup **plus** a written data-model + migration proposal тАФ reviewed and approved first. Do NOT assign to a build session until that lands.

### B413 тАФ Auto-stitch scanned, scale-less survey sheets that carry NO match-line text `[Doc Review / stitching]` (feature) #doc-review #stitching  *(owner-dropped 2026-06-23 with a real upload "get it to stitch these together correctly"; owner picked approach (A) "build the real OCR auto-stitch"; minted **B413** = highest B# (B412) + 1; IN PROGRESS)*
`[ ]` **Phase 1 (foundation) BUILT + unit-tested (`src/shared/files/ocrMatchLines.js`, 8 tests); NOT yet wired into the live stitch тАФ see remaining blockers below. Do NOT present a topology-only placement as "aligned" (a wrong stitch is worse than an unstitched one).** The owner's GPL topo slice (C-2/C-3/C-4, "TOPO SURVEY I/II/III", NOT TO SCALE, FOR REFERENCE ONLY, 9-item text layer) carries its "MATCH LINE тАж SHEET N" labels only in the RASTER тАФ so `autoPlaceGroup` (B337) gets nothing.
- **DONE тАФ OCR match-line recovery design, proven on the real pages.** `recoverMatchLines(passes, dims)` runs `parseMatchLines` in EACH orientation pass's own upright frame, then maps the label centre back to page space to pick the edge (`framePointToPage`). Verified against real Tesseract reads: C-2's bottom "MATCH LINE ~ SHEET 2" тЖТ side bottom; C-4's left (rotated 90┬░) "MATCH LINE ~ SHEET 2" тЖТ side left. Adjacency for the L-layout (C-2 over C-3, C-4 right of C-3) is fully recoverable.
- **тЬЕ DONE (2026-06-23) тАФ blocker #3, the hard CV tail: pixel-precise seam alignment. BUILT, tested, wired, proven seamless on the owner's real C-2/C-3 scans.** New pure module `src/shared/files/matchLineFit.js` (1-D horizontal CLOSE bridges the dashes тЖТ OPEN drops text/crossing strokes тЖТ RANSAC fits the line over the full width, with a span guard so a short horizontal note can't masquerade as the seam) + browser glue `doc-review/lib/matchLineRefine.js` (`refineGroupPlacements`: BFS the seam graph, re-derive each neighbor's matrix from the REAL match line via `solveM`, then `slideRefine` connects the crossing linework). Handles the ~1┬░ inter-sheet skew (recovered тИТ0.938┬░ on the real pair, matching a Python reference exactly) and the inset/dashed line. Wired into `Stitcher.jsx` (`renderPageToImageData` тЖТ binarize тЖТ refine) as a **best-effort, fail-safe** pass: any sheet it can't fit confidently тАФ or whose correction isn't a plausible nudge (`plausibleRefine`) тАФ keeps its label-based placement, so it only ever improves a seam, never breaks one. 24 unit tests; verified end-to-end through the real exported functions on the actual sheets (seamless composite). Removes the old "topology-only тЗТ keep aligned:false" limitation for any set that reaches the refiner.
- **REMAINING blockers (only the RECOGNITION layer that feeds the now-working aligner; needed for fully-automatic on these specific compressed scans):**
  1. **OCR reliability/perf.** Tesseract on these COMPRESSED scans is inconsistent across scale/orientation/PSM (a label read at one render setting is missed at another) and OCR-ing every sparse page at 3 orientations is slow. Needs tuning (edge-band crops at a fixed legible scale, per-orientation PSM) + a conservative trigger (only a sparse-text drawing with no text match-lines) and likely a worker budget. Until labels are read, `autoPlaceGroup` builds no adjacency тЖТ the aligner isn't invoked тЖТ sheet stays manual-Align.
  2. **Sequence-target resolution.** Labels reference by SEQUENCE ("SHEET 2" = the 2nd sheet = C-3), not the "C-3" code тАФ `autoStitch.buildAdjacency` keys on `sheetNumber`, so a numeric target must resolve to the Nth group member (prototyped, not yet in code).
- **Honest note for the owner:** the seamless-join ENGINE is done and proven on your sheets. For it to run hands-free on these "FOR REFERENCE ONLY / NOT TO SCALE" compressed scans, the app must also reliably recognize which scanned sheet neighbors which (blockers #1тАУ#2 above). A vector CAD set (or sheets whose match-line text + numbers read cleanly) auto-stitches AND now gets the pixel-perfect seam today.

### B411 тАФ Auto-filing residual gaps after the multi-discipline split (B410) `[Doc Review / auto-filing]` (bug/task) #doc-review #filing  *(spun off from B410, 2026-06-23; minted **B411** = B410 + 1)*
`[ ]` Three honest gaps surfaced while testing real Drive files against the new splitter (B410, shipped) тАФ none blocks the shipped feature, but each is a real recognition weakness:
- **(a) Scanned/image-only sets read as nothing in FILING.** A no-text-layer drawing (e.g. "2023.11.06 Mesa - Electrical B1.pdf") has no embedded text, so the local read returns nothing and the file lands in the holding tray. OCR already exists in the STITCHER (B352, `doc-review/lib/ocr.js`, Tesseract); wire that same OCR into the filing read (`localRead.js`) so scanned sheets classify too. Bigger lift (renders pages to canvas), so it's its own item.
- **(b) Date sometimes grabs an old BASE date over the issue/revision date.** "Mesa - Site Plan 2025.09.17.pdf" filed with `2023-04-07`; the latest-date picker isn't preferring the issue/rev date in the title block. Tighten the date selection (prefer a date adjacent to "ISSUED/REV/IFC", and weight the title-block zone).
- **(c) Big combined sets weren't validated here тАФ Drive connector caps downloads at 10 MB.** The richest split cases (GPL Civil IFP 125 MB, Jacintoport MEP 13.6 MB, full Mesa COH sets) couldn't be pulled in-session. Needs a signed-in spot-check on planyr.io (drop a big combined set тЖТ expect separate per-discipline PDFs) or a higher-limit fetch path.

### B406 тАФ Shared team workspaces: invite by email, share a project with a team `[Site Planner + Doc Review]` (feature) #site-planner #doc-review #infra  *(2026-06-22; "B-TEAM" in the cowork handoff. Filed B365 in-session, but a concurrent `main` had taken B365тАУB405 тАФ renumbered to the real next free B#406. PR #305 title still says B365.)*
`[ ]` **Shipping тАФ code merged via PR #305; DB phase-2 migrated + verified in PRODUCTION (`lyeqzkuiwngunutlkkmi`); remaining owner step: run `team_storage.sql` (phase 3) for shared-PDF reads.**
Lets a team share a workspace: invite people by email (activates on signup/sign-in even if they had no account yet), admins vs members, and a project stays **private until deliberately shared** (and can revert to private). Additive + private-by-default preserved тАФ a row with `team_id IS NULL` behaves exactly as before.
- **DB (done + verified in prod):** `db/profiles.sql` (email mirror), `db/teams.sql` (teams/team_members/team_invites + `is_team_member`/`is_team_admin` SECURITY-DEFINER helpers + `claim_team_invites`/`list_team_members` RPCs + signup auto-claim), `db/team_sharing.sql` (`team_id` on sites/doc_reviews/file_facts; PK `(user_id,id)`тЖТ`(id)`; RLS rewritten to "own OR shared-with-my-team", delete = owner-or-team-admin). Verified end-state: 3 `team_id` cols, `sites` PK = `id`, 12 RLS policies, both helpers present. Pre-flight done (snapshot tables `backup_*_20260622`; 0 dup ids) тАФ **drop the backup tables once confirmed good.**
- **DB (still to run):** `doc-review/db/team_storage.sql` (phase 3) тАФ extra Storage SELECT policy so teammates can open each other's **shared review PDFs**. Until run, that one sub-path is inert (graceful); everything else works.
- **Client:** `optimisticUpsert.casUpsert` updates by `(id,version)` only + stamps `user_id` on INSERT only (creator never re-stamped on a teammate edit); `cloudSync`/`reviewStore` carry `team_id`, delete by id (RLS scopes), team_id-missing graceful degrade; `siteModel` `teamId`/`ownerId` + `teamShareOf` (SITE_MODEL_VERSIONтЖТ8); `storage.mergePulledSites` doesn't re-push teammates' rows; `lib/teams.js` + `lib/sharing.js`; `SitePlannerApp` claims invites on sign-in; **UI** = Team tab (`TeamPanel`) + account-menu entry, Share-with-team control in the Project Files drawer.
