### B790 тАФ FEMA flood zones showed a healthy "loaded" (blue) dot over a BLANK map during a source slowdown тАФ honest per-layer "source slow / data may be missing" status `[Site Planner / layers panel]` (bug/feature) #site-planner #gis #ui #floodplain  *(coworker live-diagnosis handoff 2026-07-12 as "NEW-3"; late-bound to **B790 / V290** via `npm run next-id -- --against-main`. Origin: filed 2026-07-12 from chat. Branch `claude/nfhl-service-degradation-uy5fi1`. Implemented + sandbox-verified same session per STANDING RULE #1; parked here for the live "row goes amber on a real stall" check.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED тАФ a toggled-on raster overlay no longer reports "loaded" (blue) the instant it's added; it stays "loading" until the server-rendered image ACTUALLY lands, and flips to amber "source slow or unavailable тАФ the map may be missing data" if the export never arrives.** This is the owner's exact complaint from the 2026-07-11 NFHL slowdown ("FEMA showing blue as if it's working, but nothing paints"). AUDIT-FIRST root cause found in the live code: `syncOverlayLayers` (`lib/layers.js`) called `onStatus(k, "loaded")` **optimistically on `addTo(map)`**, before the export `<img>` resolved тАФ and esri-leaflet fires NO error for a silent hang, so a degraded agency (FEMA held/killed exports 20тАУ30 s) left the row on a false blue forever.
- **Fix:** extracted the status machine into a pure, unit-testable `wireRasterStatus` (`lib/layerRequest.js`, leaflet-free): status starts at "loading"; only a real `'load'` event тЖТ "loaded"; a **stall watchdog** (`RASTER_STALL_MS = 15 s`) flips to a NEW amber `"slow"` state when no `'load'` lands in time; a real error event тЖТ "failed" (or one proxyтЖТdirect fallback first, which no longer claims a premature "loaded"); a later `'load'` clears "slow" back to "loaded" (recovery on a pan). `layers.js` now wires through it and reports "loading" (not "loaded") on add.
- **Amber, not red (KEY DECISIONS palette rule):** RED (`--danger`) is reserved for a genuine error; a stall is "too slow, data may be missing," which is retryable тАФ so `LayerPanel` renders `"slow"` on `--warn-text` amber with an inline reason, and `combineLayerStatus` ranks it just under "failed".
- Verify: live (GIS-endpoint-behavior + zoom/data-density rendering class тАФ the sandbox has no egress to `hazards.fema.gov` (HTTP 000), so a REAL stalled export flipping the actual on-map row to amber can only be seen on planyr.io) тЖТ **V290**.
- **DEDUPE-FIRST:** the map-panel counterpart to **B366** (Done тАФ the Site Analysis *screen's* UNAVAILABLE state); no existing item makes the *layers-panel* raster status honest. Relates to but does not duplicate **B717** (panel layout/floating) тАФ that's chrome, this is status truth. Not **B739** (Done/Verify тАФ export composite; its loud drop is correct and untouched).
- Sandbox: 12 new `wireRasterStatus` unit cases in `test/layerRequest.test.js` (no optimistic "loaded"; watchdogтЖТslow; load clears it; proxy fallback once; onRemove/isActive gating; recovery) + `layerPanelInfo` "slow" precedence. Full suite **3,620 green** ┬╖ lint 0 errors ┬╖ build green ┬╖ MAP.md regenerated (new `wireRasterStatus`/`RASTER_STALL_MS` exports).

### B789 тАФ Per-source `timeoutMs` override in the GIS screening-fetch registry (FEMA flood answered at ~9.5 s, past the 9 s default) `[Site Planner / GIS]` (feature) #site-planner #gis #floodplain  *(coworker live-diagnosis handoff 2026-07-12 as "NEW-2"; late-bound to **B789 / V289** via `npm run next-id -- --against-main`. Origin: filed 2026-07-12 from chat. Same branch as B790. Implemented + sandbox-verified same session.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED тАФ a GIS source row can now set its own `timeoutMs` to override the shared 9 s screening-fetch default (`GIS_FETCH_TIMEOUT_MS`); `GIS_SOURCES.flood` sets 20 s.** During the 2026-07-11 slowdown FEMA's NFHL answered the flood `/query` in ~9.5 s, so all three retry attempts aborted ~0.5 s too early and the Site Analysis floodplain row went unavailable even though FEMA would have answered. The override lets flood wait ~20 s (flood data changes slowly, so a longer wait is cheap) while every other source keeps the 9 s default.
- **Plumbing:** `reg()` (`siteAnalysis.js`) carries `s.timeoutMs` onto the endpoint; `queryLayer`/`countLayer` forward `{ timeoutMs }` into `fetchArcgisJson`, which already honored `opts.timeoutMs ?? GIS_FETCH_TIMEOUT_MS` тАФ zero change to the fetch core.
- **AUDIT-FIRST correction to the handoff:** the handoff said the *vector* engine rides "the same 9 s substrate." It does not тАФ `vectorLayers.js` `defaultFetchJson` is a **bare `fetch` with NO timeout**, so the 9 s near-miss is the **screening path only**. The vector flood pull isn't aborted at 9 s (it has its own long TTL cache); this override targets the path that actually lost the race.
- **Caveat (live evidence, do not oversell):** FEMA's own gateway still dropped some responses at ~10 s during the worst of it, so 20 s only rescues the *marginal-slow* case тАФ the durable fix is the SWR cache proxy (**B788**), not this alone.
- Verify: live (GIS-endpoint timing class тАФ confirming the flood screening survives a genuinely slow (~9тАУ10 s) FEMA answer needs the live degraded endpoint; the sandbox can't reach `hazards.fema.gov`) тЖТ **V289**.
- **DEDUPE-FIRST:** a direct follow-on to **B366** (Done тАФ the shared resilient fetch + the 9 s cap it introduced); B366 added no per-source override. Distinct from **B367**/**B371** (the screening cache tiers).
- Sandbox: 2 new `test/siteAnalysis.test.js` cases (flood forwards `timeoutMs: 20000` to the fetch layer; a source without it passes no override тЖТ the default applies) + `test/gisSources.test.js` still green (the field is additive, unguarded). Full suite green ┬╖ lint 0 ┬╖ build green.

### B788 тАФ Route FEMA flood + other rasters through the same-origin cache proxy with a BOUNDED upstream timeout so a degraded source fails open fast, never blank `[Site Planner / GIS]` (feature) #site-planner #gis #infra #floodplain  *(coworker live-diagnosis handoff 2026-07-12 as "NEW-1"; late-bound to **B788 / V288** via `npm run next-id -- --against-main`. Origin: filed 2026-07-12 from chat. Same branch as B790. AUDIT-FIRST: the durable half was already built тАФ see below. Implemented + sandbox-verified same session.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED (the missing guardrail) тАФ the server-side GIS cache proxy now bounds every upstream agency fetch (`UPSTREAM_TIMEOUT_MS = 25 s`), so a degraded source (FEMA held/killed exports 20тАУ30 s on 2026-07-11) can't hang the Function to the platform subrequest ceiling; it fails OPEN fast instead.** AUDIT-FIRST finding that reshaped this item: the handoff's open question ("does the FEMA export already route through `/api/gis-cache`?") is **YES** тАФ `syncOverlayLayers` routes rasters through the B445 proxy by default (`gisProxyEnabled()`), and the proxy ALREADY serves the last-good Drive copy instantly on a cache HIT and refreshes in the background (the stale-while-revalidate "never blank a previously-seen area" behavior NEW-1 asked for **already exists**). So the durable win was present; the only real gap was an unbounded server fetch on the FIRST-EVER (uncached) view of an area during an outage.
- **Fix:** a shared `fetchUpstream(fetchImpl, url, timeoutMs)` helper (`functions/api/gis-cache/_handler.js`) wraps both upstream fetches (cache-miss + background refresh) in an `AbortController` timeout; `handleGisCache` takes an injectable `upstreamTimeoutMs`. On timeout the existing fail-open path runs (cache-miss тЖТ 302 to the real agency; refresh тЖТ keep the copy already served). The cache-HIT serve-last-good path is untouched тАФ the 25 s cap only ever affects the uncached first view.
- **Honest residual limit (documented, not hidden):** the truly-first-ever view of an area during an outage still can't paint (there is no last-good copy to serve, and no client/proxy trick invents one) тАФ it now fails open *promptly* instead of hanging. Every previously-viewed area is immune.
- Verify: live (server-side proxy behavior against a degraded source тАФ can only be confirmed with the live edge + a real slow/again-degraded FEMA; the sandbox can't reach the agency or the deployed Function) тЖТ **V288**.
- **DEDUPE-FIRST:** hardens **B445** (Done тАФ the cache proxy itself) and is the map-overlay sibling of **B367** (Done тАФ the *screening* SWR cache). Not **B371** (Later тАФ regional pre-cache snapshot).
- Sandbox: 2 new `test/gisCacheHandler.test.js` cases (a hanging agency + a tiny cap тЖТ 302 fail-open; the upstream fetch carries an `AbortSignal`) + the existing 13 handler cases green (the UA-header test unaffected). Full suite green ┬╖ lint 0 ┬╖ build green.

### B409 (├Ч2) тАФ Unlimited-size file uploads: chunked Drive upload through the Worker proxy (replaces the CORS-dead browser-direct path) `[Doc Review / storage]` (bug) #doc-review #drive  *(owner-dropped 2026-06-23 as "NEW-1"; minted **B409**. REWORKED 2026-07-11 per the ownerтАЩs unlimited-uploads handoff, branch `claude/unlimited-file-uploads-04zkc9`; тЖТ V282 (minted V280, renumbered on merge-in of `origin/main` тАФ the concurrent jurisdiction-badge/ISD session took V280/V281).)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED (rework) тАФ any-size uploads as ~16 MB chunks relayed through new `/api/uploads/*`; the streaming/Range download half fixes "won't open"; parked here for the live 125 MB round-trip тЖТ V282.**
- Recurrence: 2026-07-11 (├Ч2) тАФ the owner's 125 MB "GPL - Civil IFP 2026.06.19.pdf" still can't save. The first fix (browser PUTs bytes DIRECTLY to Google) is **CORS-dead by design and could never pass its live gate**: Fetch-over-CORS hides the `Location` header of the session-init response, and Google's upload endpoint answers preflights with no `Access-Control-Allow-Origin`. Re-opens the ORIGINAL B# (DEDUPE-FIRST) тАФ do not re-attempt browser-direct-to-Drive.
- **Rework (all same-origin, so CORS never applies; owner decision: Drive + chunked-through-the-Worker, not R2/Supabase):** the browser slices the file (`File.slice`, never a whole-file read) into 16 MiB chunks (64 ├Ч Google's 256 KiB granule) тЖТ `PUT /api/uploads/<id>/chunk` тЖТ the Worker relays each chunk to the Drive resumable session it minted in `POST /api/uploads/start`. The capability session URI persists in new **`public.upload_sessions`** (`server/storage/db/upload_sessions.sql`, own-rows RLS, **migrated to production this session via MCP**) and is never returned to the browser. `GET тАж/status` probes Drive (`bytes */total`) for resume-from-offset; `POST тАж/complete` records the `drive_files` mapping (keeps the NEW-4 rollback: mapping-write failure deletes the Drive file + fails honestly тАФ the V191 guard moved here). No single request is ever large тЖТ the Worker's ~100 MB body cap, its 128 MB memory, and Supabase's 50 MB cap all stop mattering, at any total size. Client loop (`src/shared/files/chunkedUpload.js`): sequential chunks, 5├Ч exponential backoff, resume via /status after a drop, `storageQuotaExceeded` тЖТ plain-English "Drive is full" without futile retries; Library tray shows an honest per-file **progress bar** (server-confirmed bytes).
- **Download half (this is what "the big file won't open" was): `GET /api/files` now STREAMS** тАФ the Drive body passes through as a ReadableStream (the old handler buffered `arrayBuffer()` in the Worker, blowing the 128 MB memory cap on a 125 MB PDF) тАФ **and forwards the client's `Range` тЖТ 206 Partial Content** (`adapter.fetchStream` / `driveBackend.getStream` / `driveClient.mediaStream`). Drive-stored PDFs > 50 MB open BY URL (`driveStreamSource` + URL-source `loadPdf`), so pdf.js range-streams them progressively; the buffered path stays the fallback and for everything else.
- **Removed (per the handoff ┬з9):** the whole-file `POST /api/files` route, `functions/api/files/resumable.js` (browser-direct), `reviewStore.uploadLargeToDrive` + `uploadSource`, and the **Supabase Storage upload fallback** in `storeSource` (the 50 MB fallback IS what produced the silent "oversize" dead end; Supabase Storage reads remain for pre-cutover files). ALL uploads тАФ any size тАФ now take the one chunked path; `sourceState`'s `oversize`/`too-large` states remain only to classify legacy never-stored records.
- **Post-review hardening (same session тАФ a 5-lens adversarial review over the diff; 2 findings double-confirmed, 15 triaged):** the chunk endpoint no longer order-checks against its own best-effort bookkeeping (a missed progress write could 400 a healthy upload; Drive arbitrates offsets authoritatively); `/complete` is **idempotent** (the row is marked `recorded` and kept until expiry, so a retry after a lost response succeeds instead of 404ing a fully-successful upload тАФ status CHECK extended via a second production migration) and a rolled-back session answers a distinct 410 + `sessionLost`; the client **short-circuits `sessionLost`** (no futile retry burn), **re-reads the auth token per request** via a getter (an upload outliving the ~1 h JWT no longer dies mid-flight), resets its retry budget when the /status probe shows progress (bodies landing while responses drop), validates the server's chunkSize granularity, and maps a quota failure at session-mint too; the **real failure cause** (e.g. "Google Drive is out of storage space") now reaches all three surfaces тАФ the Library tray (`fileWarn`), the DocReview banner, and a NEW Stitcher store-failure banner (the Stitcher previously lost a failed store silently); split uploads share one continuous progress bar. **Known residuals (accepted, minor):** pdf.js range reads pin the open-time token, so a page first fetched >1 h after opening can 401 (re-open recovers); a tab closed in the seconds between the final chunk and `/complete` can orphan one Drive file (the 7-day purge removes only the row).
- Verify: live (concurrency/timing + real-project-data + range/parity тАФ mandatory LIVE-VERIFY classes) тЖТ **V282**: signed-in тЙе100 MB upload completes with a moving progress bar + lands in Drive; opens in the viewer with `206` responses in the network tab; killing the network mid-upload resumes (not restarts).
- Sandbox: full suite green (new `test/chunkedUpload.test.js` ┬╖ `resumableProxy.test.js` ┬╖ `uploadEndpoints.test.js` ┬╖ `filesStream.test.js` тАФ chunk math incl. final-short-chunk / exact-multiple / 256 KiB granularity, **308-as-success**, resume-from-offset, retry cap, quota short-circuit, foreign-uploadId тЖТ 404 before Drive is touched (B491), session-URI-never-in-a-response, initтЖТ308sтЖТ200 integration, RangeтЖТ206 passthrough + the V150 two-account no-bytes regression) ┬╖ lint 0 ┬╖ build green + lazy chunks intact.

### B812 тАФ The single-tab false "another window" toast BURST on a building resize (survived B759├Ч2 + B811) тАФ own-echo-by-rev `[Site Planner / persistence]` (bug) #site-planner #persistence #infra  *(owner-reported 2026-07-13 from chat тАФ "itsstill doing it" with fresh screenshots of a BURST of "you (another window) changed a paving area / sidewalk / parking field you just edited тАФ their version is showing", all one tab, mid building resize; owner confirmed he had already hard-reloaded, ruling out deploy lag. Branch `claude/site-debugging-y82heo`. Minted **B812** via `npm run next-id -- --against-main`. тЖТ V304. Third mechanism in the B759/B811 stale-refetch self-echo family; hunted + fixed via a 6-hypothesis reproduction workflow + THREE adversarial red-team rounds.)*
`[x]` **FIXED this session тАФ the burst mechanism reproduced against the real engine, a bulletproof rev-based fix landed, and THREE red-team rounds drove out four residuals (the burst itself + delete-resurrection + serialization-drift + a >15s aged-echo edge); full suite 3728 green, `eslint` 0 errors, build green. The signed-in realtime end-to-end parks in тП│ Verify тЖТ V304.**
- Verify: live тАФ signed-in, **timing/race + concurrency/multi-writer** class (mandatory LIVE-VERIFY); the burst only manifests with a real Supabase realtime reconnect/tab-wake echoing real commits, which the logged-out sandbox can't exercise. Owed on V304.
- Origin: owner-reported 2026-07-13 (false-toast burst still firing after B759├Ч2 + B811).
- **AUDIT-FIRST тАФ root cause: a stale refetch that OMITS a just-committed element evicts it from the shadow, so its own echoes look foreign.** A resize re-commits a building's bonded children (sidewalk/paving/parking) several times fast. On a socket reconnect / tab-wake, `refetchReplace`'s fetch snapshot can OMIT a just-committed child (read-replica lag / the fetch predating the commit burst). `reconcileSeedRows` (B811) can only substitute into rows the fetch still CONTAINS тАФ it cannot re-insert a dropped row тАФ so `eng.seed()` evicts the child from the shadow. The child's own realtime echoes of earlier revs then arrive with no shadow entry (the rev guard can't catch them), no pending entry, and the single-slot `recentSent` held only the latest version тЖТ `sentMatches` missed the intermediate revs тЖТ a false `remote-upsert(authoredRecently)` per pre-final commit = the burst. B759├Ч2 (data-match suppression) and B811 (present-but-stale reconcile) both left the OMITTED-element path open.
- **The fix (client-only, `lib/elementSync.js` + `lib/elementRows.js`), four layers, each closing a residual a red-team confirmed:**
  1. **`ownRevs` + `maxOwnRev` high-water (own-echo-by-rev).** Record EVERY server rev this tab's commits produce (ok / restore-self-dup / conflict-self-dup), plus a NEVER-time-pruned per-key high-water. `applyRemoteRow` ignores any non-tombstone echo where `isOwnRev(rev)` OR `rev <= maxOwnRev[key]`, before the pending branch тАФ so it kills the `remote-upsert` AND `remote-while-dirty` variants. Server revs are monotonic per element, so anything at/below our high-water is definitively ours (or a foreign write we already superseded); a live foreign edit always lands strictly ABOVE it тЖТ still surfaces. The high-water (never pruned) closes the round-2 Angle-4 edge where a >15s-old own echo outlived the 15s `ownRevs`/`recentSent` windows.
  2. **`recentSent` тЖТ all-versions** (`Map<key,Map<json,at>>`): covers the pre-RPC / transport-failure window where no rev was learned, for every version put on the wire.
  3. **`stableStringify` тЖТ exact JSON wire semantics** (drop undefined-valued keys / functions / symbols, holes+undefined тЖТ `null`, Date via toJSON): the old `undefined` token made any element with an undefined property serialize DIFFERENTLY from its post-jsonb echo, permanently defeating every self-echo byte-compare AND producing phantom no-op diffs (red-team Angle 2). Floats were confirmed byte-stable тАФ not a source of drift.
  4. **`reconcileSeedRows` tombstone-aware** (new 3rd arg `tombstonedSnapshot()`): a delete clears the shadow entry, so a stale-alive refetch would adopt the row verbatim and RESURRECT a just-deleted element (a TOMBSTONE-DELETES violation) + later mis-fire "was deleted by you (another window)" (red-team Angle 1). A fetched-alive row whose (kind,id) this tab tombstoned within the window at a rev тЙд our delete is kept deleted; a genuine re-create ABOVE the delete rev passes through alive.
- **Named rules:** LIVE-VERIFY (signed-in realtime тЖТ V304); AUDIT-FIRST (6-hypothesis repro workflow located the omitted-element eviction; reconciled against B759├Ч2/B811's "sufficient" claims and found the open path); TOMBSTONE-DELETES (reconcileSeedRows now honours the delete floor тАФ no resurrection); LOUD-FAILURE (own echoes suppressed only by rev identity / delete floor тАФ every genuine foreign write/delete still surfaces, pinned by guard tests). No `MAP.md` change (no export add/remove; `reconcileSeedRows` gained a param but was already exported).
- **Verified (sandbox):** independent node repros of the burst (child dropped тЖТ 0 toasts), the resurrection (stays deleted; foreign re-create above delete stays alive), the undefined-prop echo (recognized; no phantom commit), and the >15s aged echo (recognized via high-water). `test/elementSync.test.js` +8 (burst; pending re-create; two genuine-foreign GUARDs; per-element rev keying; high-water aged echo; Angle-4; wire-semantics + no-phantom-diff for stableStringify) and `test/elementRows.test.js` +3 (no-resurrection; foreign-recreate-alive; no-tombstone back-compat). Full suite **3728** green; build green; lint 0. THREE red-team rounds: round 1 found delete-resurrection + serialization-drift; round 2 confirmed those closed + found the >15s aged-echo edge; **round 3 (final) тАФ CLEAN, 0 breaks**: proved the high-water floor cannot over-suppress a foreign edit (server per-element rev monotonicity тЖТ any rev тЙд our high-water is superseded by our own write; a live foreign edit is always strictly above it; foreign deletes are exempt via the `!row.deleted_at` gate) + a 48-permutation full-flow integration (mixed edit/delete/create burst ├Ч stale-omit/rollback/show-alive ├Ч echo orderings ├Ч journal ├Ч transport-failure) all clean.
- **DEDUPE-FIRST:** same stale-refetch self-echo family as **B759** (the toast) and **B811** (the canvas-revert), but a DISTINCT mechanism (omitted-element shadow eviction, not present-but-stale) and a DISTINCT fix (rev-identity own-echo, not data-match), so filed as its own B# cross-referencing both тАФ mirrors how B811 was filed alongside B759. Two round-2 latent gaps (foldJournal not recognizing the local-tombstone sentinel; boxed-primitive/BigInt in stableStringify) were proven UNREACHABLE in Planyr's element model (no journal survives the delete idle transition; elements never carry wrapper objects or BigInt) тАФ noted, not fixed.
- **Documented KNOWN EDGES:** (1) **>15s stale-alive delete resurrection тАФ the WITHIN-SESSION half is now CLOSED (round-4, owner "close all loose ends").** The floor `reconcileSeedRows` consults is now a NEVER-pruned per-key high-water (`maxDeleteRev`, session-long, mirrors `maxOwnRev`), cleared only when the element is genuinely re-created/restored тАФ so an in-session reconnect ARBITRARILY LATER than a delete keeps it deleted. SAFE by monotonicity: the floor can only ever keep-deleted a fetched row at a rev тЙд the delete (already superseded); a genuine re-create always lands ABOVE it, so no legitimate element can be hidden even if the floor lingered (the same invariant red-teamed clean for `maxOwnRev`). The realtime-echo twin is already covered beyond 15s by `maxOwnRev` (the delete's rev is recorded, so a pre-delete echo is тЙд high-water тЖТ suppressed). **Residual (still open):** the cross-**RELOAD** variant тАФ delete, then reload the page, and the post-reload fresh fetch hits a routed read-replica still lagged past the delete. In-memory floors don't survive a reload; fully closing it needs a DURABLE per-element delete tombstone (like B757's plan-level `deltomb`) with clear-on-restore. Config-dependent (Supabase PostgREST reads the primary by default тЖТ no lag тЖТ no resurrection unless read-replicas are explicitly routed) and SELF-CORRECTING (next edit тЖТ `edit-vs-deleted` тЖТ drops again). Deferred as higher-risk (persistence in the data-integrity path) than the edge is worth тАФ owner-visible trade-off, revisit on request. (2) **Redundant re-create round-trip.** When a stale fetch OMITS an element this tab already synced, `foldNeverSyncedLocal` folds it back and `reconcile` re-enqueues a create; the server answers `exists` тЖТ adopted as an update (one extra rev + a redundant identical write). No toast, no data loss тАФ a benign wasted round-trip, later suppressed by the high-water floor.

### B811 тАФ A resized building's bonded sidewalk / paving "separates" (snaps back) when a stale refetch re-seeds the shadow `[Site Planner / persistence]` (bug) #site-planner #persistence #infra  *(owner-reported 2026-07-13 from chat тАФ "it's separating the sidewalk and paving and building when i change the building size"; a screenshot showed a "you (another window) changed a parking field you just edited тАФ their version is showing" toast during the resize. Owner confirmed it stopped after reloading onto the B759 (├Ч2) build. Branch `claude/site-debugging-y82heo`. Minted **B811** via `npm run next-id -- --against-main`. тЖТ V303. The CANVAS-REVERT twin of B759 (same stale-seed root cause, different symptom).)*
`[x]` **FIXED this session тАФ sandbox verified (a node repro against the real engine + 8 new unit tests; full suite 3717 green, `eslint` 0 errors, build green); the signed-in realtime end-to-end parks in тП│ Verify тЖТ V303.** A building's sidewalk/paving/parking are separate elements bonded to it (`attachedTo`) and DO reflow flush on resize (`refitChildren`/`fitKid`), so the "separation" wasn't a geometry bug тАФ it was a stale copy of a just-committed piece getting shoved back onto the canvas.
- Verify: live тАФ signed-in, **timing/race + concurrency/multi-writer** class (mandatory LIVE-VERIFY); the revert only manifests with a real Supabase realtime reconnect/tab-wake landing a stale fetch, which the logged-out sandbox can't exercise. Owed on V303.
- Origin: owner-reported 2026-07-13 (bonded pieces separating on building resize).
- **AUDIT-FIRST тАФ NOT a `refitChildren` bug; it's `refetchReplace` re-seeding from a STALE fetch.** An Explore pass confirmed bonded RECTANGULAR children (sidewalk/paving/parking/dock stack) already track a resize via `refitChildren`тЖТ`fitKid`/`relayoutSide`. The real cause is the same stale-seed root as B759: `refetchReplace` (SitePlanner.jsx, fires on every socket (re)join / tab-wake / 4s fallback) `await`s `fetchElements` then `eng.seed(rows)` + `replace(setEls, merged)`. When that fetch's snapshot PREDATES a batch this tab just committed (resize тЖТ the building AND its bonded children commit as one batch), the seed rolls the shadow's revs BACKWARD and the rebuild puts the PRE-resize child positions back on the canvas тАФ the building keeps its new size (already on canvas) but a bonded piece snaps back = "separating". `foldNeverSyncedLocal` only covers ZERO-row elements and `foldJournal` is cleared once a commit succeeds, so a committed-then-refetched element was protected by neither. - **The fix (new pure `reconcileSeedRows` in `lib/elementRows.js` + 3-line wiring in `refetchReplace`):** before seeding, replace any fetched row THIS tab's shadow holds a STRICTLY NEWER rev for with our committed data+rev+z (read `eng.shadowSnapshot()` BEFORE `seed` clears it; feed the SAME reconciled rows to `seed` AND `rowsToModel` so shadow and canvas stay in lockstep). Everything else passes through: a foreign-advanced or caught-up row stays canonical (a genuinely stale reconnecting tab has LOWER shadow revs than the server тЖТ adopts the server rows тЖТ V229 #5 stale-tab clobber guard holds), and a tombstone row is never overridden (TOMBSTONE-DELETES тАФ no resurrection; edit-vs-delete still resolves via the conflict matrix).
- **Named rules:** LIVE-VERIFY (signed-in realtime timing/race тЖТ V303); AUDIT-FIRST (Explore-confirmed the geometry reflow is correct, traced the revert to `refetchReplace`'s stale seed); TOMBSTONE-DELETES (tombstone rows are never overridden by a live shadow entry); LOUD-FAILURE (no silent clobber тАФ a foreign-newer row is always adopted, never masked). Docs: `MAP.md` regenerated (new `reconcileSeedRows` export).
- **Verified (sandbox):** a standalone node repro (`seed(fresh) тЖТ commit a child move тЖТ reconcileSeedRows(staleRows, shadow) тЖТ rowsToModel`) reverted to the old position WITHOUT the fix and stayed at the new position WITH it, while a foreign rev-9 row was still adopted (V229). `test/elementRows.test.js` +8 (replace-stale; keep-when-equal; keep-foreign-advanced/V229; never-override-tombstone; leave-unknown-row; malformed-json-safe; empty/non-Map inputs; input-immutability). Full suite 3717 green; build green; lint 0 errors.
- **DEDUPE-FIRST:** same stale-seed root-cause family as **B759** (reopened ├Ч2 for the toast) but a DISTINCT symptom (a canvas REVERT, not a false toast) and a DISTINCT code path (`refetchReplace`/`reconcileSeedRows` vs `applyRemoteRow`), so filed as its own B# cross-referencing B759 rather than a B759 leg. Related folds it complements: `foldNeverSyncedLocal` (B756, zero-row elements) and `foldJournal` (NEW-F4, journaled failed commits) тАФ `reconcileSeedRows` closes the third gap (successfully-committed elements a stale fetch predates).

### B759 тАФ False "someone else edited this in another tab" pop-up while actively editing in ONE tab (├Ч2) `[Site Planner / persistence]` (bug) #site-planner #persistence #infra  *(owner-reported 2026-07-11 from chat тАФ "While I was editing this building [Building 3, splitting a truck court off], I got a notification that someone else, or me in another tab, split it off тАФ which can't be true, I'm only working in one tab. Figure out how that even happens." Branch `claude/concurrent-edit-notification-10br1m`. Minted **B757** via `npm run next-id`; RENUMBERED to **B759** = highest B# across both files (B758) + 1 on merge-in of `origin/main`, which took B757 (deleted-plan-resurrect) + B758 (bundle-404 white-screen) + V271/V272 тАФ the code/tests/commit/branch keep the provisional **B757** label. тЖТ V273. **RECURRENCE 2026-07-13** (owner screenshot: a BURST of "you (another window) changed a paving area / trailer court you just edited тАФ their version is showing", +2 more, all one tab) тЖТ **V301**; branch `claude/site-debugging-y82heo`.)*
`[x]` **FIXED this session тАФ an adversarial 4-lens hunt + a red-team of the fix found FIVE single-tab self-echo false positives (3 realtime-read + 2 write-result timeout paths), each REPRODUCED live against the real `createElementSync` engine; all five fixed, 9 new regression tests + full suite green (3394) + `eslint` clean + build green. Red-team verdict on the fix: APPROVE-WITH-ADDITIONS (all additions folded in). The signed-in realtime end-to-end parks in тП│ Verify тЖТ V273.**
- **Recurrence (├Ч2, 2026-07-13) тАФ the SIXTH self-echo path, in the no-pending READ branch the original fix's "read-path guards are SUFFICIENT" claim left open. FIXED this session** (repro'd against the real engine pre-fix; 4 new regression tests + guards; full suite **3696** green, `eslint` 0 errors, build green). Parks in тП│ Verify тЖТ **V301** (same signed-in realtime class as V273).
  - **AUDIT-FIRST тАФ root cause = `refetchReplace` re-seeds the shadow BACKWARD, then our own batch's echoes look foreign.** `SitePlanner.jsx refetchReplace` runs on EVERY socket (re)join, tab-wake, and the 4s fallback; it `await fetchElements(...)` at the top, then `eng.seed(rows)` (which `shadow.clear()`s and rebuilds). If that fetch's snapshot PREDATES a batch this tab just committed (fetch issued mid-edit-stream, seed runs after the commit lands), the seed rolls the shadow's revs BACKWARD. The just-committed batch's realtime echoes then arrive at a rev ABOVE the stale shadow with **no pending entry left** (dirty+inflight cleared on commit) тЖТ `applyRemoteRow`'s no-pending `remote-upsert` branch fires, and because we authored each element within the 15s window it stamps `authoredRecently:true` тЖТ one false "you (another window) changed X you just edited" per element = the owner's burst (a 6-element paving/trailer-court group edit тЖТ 6 toasts). B757's five fixes ALL live in the `if (pend)` branch + `processResults`; this branch had no own-echo guard. (The delete twin fires "тАжwas deleted by you (another window)" the same way after a stale seed re-adds the row alive.)
  - **The fix (`lib/elementSync.js applyRemoteRow`, client-only, no schema change):** extend the SAME own-echo recognition B757 built into the pending branch to the no-pending read path. **Edit echo:** before emitting `remote-upsert`, if the incoming row's data byte-matches what THIS tab put on the wire in the last ~15s (`sentMatches`/`recentSent`), it's our own stale-seed echo тЖТ apply the canvas upsert (so a stale-seed canvas re-trues) but **suppress the conflict event** тАФ no toast. **Delete echo:** a tombstone at a rev no newer than our own delete's remembered rev (the `tombstoned` floor) is our own delete echo тЖТ drop it from the canvas but suppress the event. Gated on DATA-identity / the delete floor, never on `updated_by` alone, so a genuine foreign write (different data / a rev above our delete) still surfaces per the B673 matrix.
  - **Named rules:** LIVE-VERIFY (signed-in realtime timing/race тЖТ V301); AUDIT-FIRST (traced the code to `refetchReplace`'s stale re-seed, reconciled against B757's "read-path guards sufficient" claim and found the gap); LOUD-FAILURE (self-echoes silenced by data-identity / delete-floor only тАФ genuine conflicts stay loud, pinned by two GUARD tests). No `MAP.md` change (pure logic, no export change).
  - **Verified (sandbox):** a standalone node repro (`seed(fresh)тЖТcommit editтЖТseed(stale, older rev)тЖТecho`) fired the false `remote-upsert(authoredRecently)` pre-fix, silent post-fix. `test/elementSync.test.js` +4: stale-seed edit echo тЖТ upsert, no toast; a genuine foreign upsert of a just-edited element STILL fires `remote-upsert(authoredRecently)`; stale-seed tombstone echo of our own delete тЖТ remove, no toast; a genuine foreign delete STILL fires `remote-delete`. All 43 elementSync tests green; full suite 3696 green.
  - **DEDUPE-FIRST:** this IS the recurrence of B759/B757 (same module `elementSync.js applyRemoteRow`, same symptom, same "you (another window)" resolver, same user goal) тАФ reopened, not a new B#. The new path is the no-pending READ branch after a `refetchReplace` stale re-seed; B757 closed the pending + write-result paths only.
- Verify: live тАФ signed-in, **timing/race + concurrency/multi-writer** class (mandatory LIVE-VERIFY); the engine logic is proven by unit repros/tests, but the false toast only manifests with a real Supabase realtime socket echoing a real commit, which the logged-out sandbox can't exercise. Owed on V273 (original 5 paths) + V301 (the recurrence's no-pending path).
- Origin: owner-reported 2026-07-11 (spurious concurrent-edit notification, single tab); recurrence owner-reported 2026-07-13 (burst screenshot).
- **AUDIT-FIRST тАФ it's the NEW element-sync toast (B673), NOT the retired whole-doc "changed in another session" banner.** The wording the owner saw ("someone elseтАж or me in another tab") is the B673 conflict toast whose editor name resolves to **"you (another window)"** for the user's own uid (`lib/editorNames.js`). The legacy doc-level banner was retired by architecture (B672 тАФ slim header, no whole-doc payload to fight over), so this is a genuinely new false-positive in the per-element realtime read path.
- **Root cause (`lib/elementSync.js applyRemoteRow`): our OWN write echoing back over realtime is mis-read as a foreign edit.** Supabase realtime echoes a tab's own writes back to it; `applyRemoteRow` is the only guard, and it never checks `row.updated_by`/`deleted_by` against `selfUid` тАФ it relies on (a) rev idempotency (`rev <= shad.rev`) and (b) a data-equality proxy (`sameData`). The realtime READ path (`applyRemoteRow`) had three holes; a red-team of the first fix then found two more on the WRITE-RESULT path (`processResults`) тАФ **five** single-tab self-echo false positives, each reproduced live against the real `createElementSync` engine:
  1. **Edit-in-flight echo vs a newer queued edit (the reported one).** During active manipulation the echo of an in-flight commit (data **D1**, rev N+1) races ahead of its own RPC result, so the shadow rev is still N (< N+1) тЖТ the rev guard passes; meanwhile a **newer** edit (**D2**) queued into `dirty`, and the old code compared the echo only against the `dirty || inflight` **winner** (D2). D1 тЙа D2 тЖТ fired `remote-while-dirty` тЖТ *"you (another window) also just edited Building 3 тАФ your version is being kept."*
  2. **Delete-in-flight tombstone echo.** Our own delete's tombstone echo (before its RPC result) can never satisfy `sameData` (the `!row.deleted_at` guard forces it false) тЖТ same false toast on a single-tab delete.
  3. **Stale post-delete echo RESURRECTS the element (worst тАФ a data effect, not just a toast).** After editing then deleting an element, the delete's `shadow.delete()` removes the rev ceiling, so a delayed echo of the pre-delete UPDATE sails past every guard тЖТ `remote-upsert` puts the deleted element **back on the canvas** AND (authored within 15s) fires *"you (another window) changed тАж you just edited."*
  4. **Timed-out-but-committed EDIT (write-result path).** The 8 s `COMMIT_TIMEOUT_MS` aborts a commit that actually landed server-side; the retry re-flushes at the stale expected rev, hits OUR OWN committed row (a `conflict` whose `data` === our data), and `processResults` emitted `edit-vs-edit-lost-race` тЖТ *"was also just edited by you (another window) тАФ your version was kept."*
  5. **Timed-out-but-committed RESTORE (write-result path).** Same mechanism on the Restore action тЖТ a false `restore-conflict` toast (*"already restored or edited by you (another window)"*).
  Splitting a truck court off a building is a multi-element create/move/delete gesture, so the read-path trio (1тАУ3) can all fire at once; (4)/(5) need the rarer commit-timeout window.
- **The fix (`lib/elementSync.js`, client-only, no schema change):**
  - *(1) `applyRemoteRow` pending branch:* recognize the echo as OURS by matching the row against **either** pending serialization тАФ the in-flight batch entry **and** the dirty entry (not just the winner) тЖТ adopt silently, no event.
  - *(2) pending branch:* a pending `delete` + an incoming tombstone is our own delete echo тЖТ silent.
  - *(3) new `tombstoned` map (key тЖТ {rev, at}):* on a committed delete, remember the delete's rev; a later non-tombstone echo at a rev **no newer** than that delete is a stale pre-delete self-echo тЖТ ignored (no resurrect, no toast). A genuine re-create by another session arrives at a **higher** rev, clears the floor, and comes through.
  - *(4)/(5) `processResults` conflict branches:* before emitting `edit-vs-edit-lost-race` / `restore-conflict`, if the conflicting live row's `data` **equals our own op's data**, it's our own timed-out-but-committed write echoing back тЖТ adopt the fresh rev silently, no re-commit, no toast. **Gated on data-equality, not `updated_by === selfUid` alone**, so a genuine same-account two-window conflict carrying *different* data still surfaces per the B673 matrix.
  - *(residual) new `recentSent` map (key тЖТ {json, at}):* the last serialization this tab put on the wire тАФ it SURVIVES a transport-failure `inflight` clear, so a committed-but-unacked write's realtime echo is still recognized as ours even after `onTransportFailure` requeued a newer edit into `dirty`.
  All new memories are pruned to the 15 s window so they stay tiny. A genuine other-window write matches **neither** pending entry / carries **different** data / arrives **above** the delete floor, so real two-window conflicts still surface loudly; two writes that produce byte-identical data aren't a conflict anyway (the pre-existing `sameData`-adopt-silently semantics). No weakening of genuine multi-writer detection (a dedicated guard test pins this).
- **Why the read-path guards are SUFFICIENT on the success lifecycle:** the (1)/(2) window is exactly "echo passed `rev <= shad.rev`", true only while the commit is in flight (shadow not yet advanced). `inflightKeys` is cleared in the flush `finally` block in the SAME microtask as `processResults` advances the shadow rev тАФ so the moment inflight clears, the rev guard already suppresses late echoes; the tombstone floor (3) covers the post-delete window, and `recentSent` covers the one exception (a `ok:false` transport failure clears inflight WITHOUT advancing the rev). The windows are complementary with no gap.
- **Named rules:** LIVE-VERIFY (signed-in timing/race + concurrency class тЖТ V273); AUDIT-FIRST (traced the code, ruled out the retired whole-doc banner, reconciled against the B672/B673 claims); TOMBSTONE-DELETES (the new tombstone floor extends the delete's authority so a stale echo can't resurrect); LOUD-FAILURE (self-echoes are silenced by data-identity, never by blanket-swallowing a class of events тАФ genuine conflicts stay loud). Docs: no `MAP.md` change (no file add/remove/export change тАФ pure logic inside `elementSync.js`).
- **Verified (sandbox):** four standalone node repros confirmed the reported bug + the delete/resurrection/timeout variants pre-fix and their absence post-fix. `test/elementSync.test.js` +9 regression tests тАФ in-flight edit echo w/ newer queued edit тЖТ silent; in-flight delete tombstone echo тЖТ silent; stale post-delete edit echo тЖТ not resurrected; a genuine re-create above the delete rev still upserts; a genuine foreign edit (data тЙа inflight AND тЙа dirty) still fires `remote-while-dirty`; a timed-out-but-committed edit whose retry conflicts with our own row тЖТ silent; same for restore; a timed-out edit whose retry conflicts with DIFFERENT data still fires `edit-vs-edit`; a committed-but-unacked realtime echo after a newer edit queued during backoff тЖТ silent. All 39 elementSync tests green; full suite **3394** green; `eslint` clean; build green.
- **Note (the idempotency-key alternative):** paths (4)/(5) could alternatively be fixed with a per-op idempotency key on the `commit_elements` RPC (a live-DB change). The data-equality guard is the equivalent client-only fix (the server already returns the conflicting row's `data`), so no schema migration is needed and the whole class is closed in one branch.
- **DEDUPE-FIRST:** NOT a recurrence of B612/B455/B460/B558/B596 (those are the retired whole-doc "changed in another session" banner). First filed false-positive in the B672/B673 per-element realtime toast path. Related-but-distinct from B672's V229 #5 (a lost-UPDATE data-loss on refetch); path #3 above is a spurious RESURRECTION, #1/#2/#4/#5 are spurious notifications.

### B758 тАФ App white-screens when the MAIN bundle 404s during a deploy (no recovery exists for the entry chunk) `[App shell / infra]` (bug) #infra #ui  *(owner-reported 2026-07-11 from chat тАФ "I pressed control shift r, and I guess we had just merged to change. And now the thing isn't even loading." Console showed `Failed to load resource: тАж 404 тАж index-CgI4uzRL.js`. Branch `claude/app-not-loading-merge-t7dwnu`. тЖТ V272.)*
`[x]` **FIXED this session тАФ recovery mechanism proven headless (3-scenario browser test), build green; the real Cloudflare deploy-window race parks in тП│ Verify тЖТ V272.** A hard reload during the seconds a fresh deploy was still propagating served the current `index.html` but 404'd its entry bundle `/assets/index-<hash>.js` at the owner's edge тЖТ blank white screen. **Confirmed transient:** that exact file returned HTTP 200 minutes later, and the live entry hash rolled `CgI4uzRL тЖТ DwgvooFK` (build id `6e67849`) between two checks тАФ i.e. active deploy churn, not a broken build.
- Verify: live тАФ deploy timing/race class (mandatory LIVE-VERIFY); the recovery mechanism is proven by a headless 3-scenario browser test, the real-deploy trigger is owed on V272.
- Origin: owner-reported 2026-07-11 (app not loading after a merge).
- **AUDIT-FIRST тАФ why the existing recovery couldn't help.** `src/app/chunkReload.js` + `ErrorBoundary` already recover from stale/missing **lazy** workspace chunks (via Vite's `vite:preloadError`) and from render crashes тАФ but that code lives INSIDE the main bundle. When the ENTRY bundle itself 404s, **no app JS runs at all**, so none of that machinery exists тЖТ a permanent white screen until a manual reload. The `_headers` (index.html `no-cache`, `/assets/*` immutable) and Cloudflare's atomic deploys are correct; the one uncovered gap is the brief edge-propagation window where fresh HTML points at a not-yet-published entry chunk.
- **The fix (`index.html`, inline boot watchdog тАФ the entry-bundle analogue of B221/B239):** a small self-contained script that is part of index.html (the one file that is never content-hashed, so it never 404s and survives the failure). It catches **(A)** a definitive load error on the entry `<script>` (capture-phase `error` listener, filtered to a not-yet-mounted app + an `/assets/*.js` script so a font/CSS/image error or a late runtime throw never trips it) and **(B)** a never-mounts timeout, then shows an honest "Updating PlanyrтАж" message and does a BOUNDED, cache-busting reload (`?_r=<ts>` тАФ the same param the app already strips post-boot via `stripReloadParam`) to pick up the finished deploy. Bounded to **3** auto-reloads on a definitive load error (**1** on a bare mount-timeout, so a slow-but-fine connection isn't re-downloaded to death), then an honest "finishing an update / Try again" manual screen тАФ never an infinite loop. A successful mount **clears the retry counter** so a future, separate deploy gets a fresh budget. Bails on `navigator.webdriver` (e2e/ui-audit untouched) and the whole body is `try/catch`, so it can never itself block boot.
- **Named rules:** LOUD-FAILURE (a blank dead page becomes a visible "updating" state + bounded auto-recovery, never a silent no-op). No pure lib touched (inline HTML), so no unit test is applicable тАФ verified instead by a headless browser integration test.
- **Verified (sandbox тАФ headless Chromium against a local server that serves `dist/` and 404s the entry bundle for the first N loads, `navigator.webdriver` overridden to false + a `#`-hash deep-link so the app boots like a real user):** (1) **normal boot** тАФ 1 load, app mounts, overlay never appears, no leftover state; (2) **transient race healing after 2 failed loads** тАФ 404 тЖТ auto-reload тЖТ 404 тЖТ auto-reload тЖТ 200 тЖТ app mounts, counter cleared (the owner's exact scenario); (3) **persistent break** тАФ exactly 3 auto-reloads (4 total loads) then the honest manual-retry overlay, no loop. All three PASS. Build green.
- **Live check owed (V272):** on planyr.io after this deploys тАФ confirm normal boot is unaffected (the watchdog is invisible on success), and (DevTools тЖТ Network тЖТ block `/assets/index-*.js` тЖТ reload) confirm the "Updating PlanyrтАж" overlay appears and recovers when unblocked. A real Cloudflare deploy-race can't be forced on demand from the sandbox.

### B757 тАФ Deliberately-deleted PLAN can resurrect on reload/sign-in when its cloud delete never landed (offline / transient) тАФ no DURABLE record-delete tombstone `[Site Planner / Persistence]` (bug тАФ data-integrity) #site-planner #persistence  *(chat 2026-07-11, from an adversarial-review brief тАФ "NEW-4 (batch 2): deleted plan resurrects after a failed/unlanded cloud delete". Minted **B757** via `npm run next-id`. Branch `claude/backlog-sharing-realtime-site-ioc65x`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED this session тАФ sandbox verified (7 new unit tests, full suite 3,391 green, build green, lint 0 errors); the signed-in offline/cross-device round-trip parks in тП│ Verify тЖТ V271.** A deliberate whole-plan delete now sticks across reload / sign-in / device sync instead of coming back.
- Verify: live тАФ offline + cross-device delete durability is a mandatory LIVE-VERIFY class (concurrency / multi-writer timing). The pure suppression/retry logic is unit-proven; the real "delete offline тЖТ reload signed-in тЖТ still gone" is owed on V271.
- Origin: filed 2026-07-11 from the two-batch review brief; **most of that brief was already handled** (see the DEDUPE note below) тАФ this residual is the one genuinely-open data-integrity gap it surfaced.
- **AUDIT-FIRST тАФ the reported premises were HALF stale; the real gap is narrower and confirmed in code.** `cloudDelete` ALREADY does an affected-row check (`.delete().eq("id",id).select("id")` тЖТ typed `interpretDelete`, `cloudSync.js`), `deleteSite` ALREADY awaits it and `deleteSiteGroup` surfaces a LOUD "may reappear" on a failure / 0-row no-op (B372/B468). What was missing: the B372 guard is the **in-memory, per-tab `recentlyDeleted` Set** тАФ cleared on reload and consulted **only in `saveSite`**. It does NOT stop `pullCloud` тЖТ `mergePulledSites` from RE-ADDING a cloud row whose delete never landed. So: signed-in, go offline, delete a plan тЖТ local removal + the loud warning, but on the next reload/sign-in the surviving cloud row is re-inserted (`map[id] = local ? merge : n`) тЖТ the plan is back. B372 fixed the same-session mount-flush half; this is the cross-reload/offline half it explicitly deferred.
- **The fix (`lib/storage.js` + a tiny `onStore` filter):** durable per-user `{id: ts}` tombstones (`planarfit:sites:deltomb:v1:<uid>`, bounded to 300). `deleteSite` records one; `mergePulledSites(existing, cloud, uid, tombstones)` now (a) SUPPRESSES an **owned** cloud row still pending removal (drops it from the merge тЖТ no resurrection) and flags it for retry, (b) KEEPS a row whose cloud copy is genuinely NEWER than the delete (`updatedAt > ts` = a real later edit on another device тЖТ the delete is stale тАФ cross-device safety, mirrors B18/B511), (c) drops the tombstone for a not-ours (teammate) row or one the cloud already removed; `pullCloud` clears the honored tombstones and **RETRIES `cloudDelete`** for the pending ones, clearing each only on a confirmed removal. Nothing is dropped for a NON-tombstoned id тАФ the change is byte-identical to today whenever no tombstone applies (unit-pinned).
- **Named rules:** TOMBSTONE-DELETES (a deliberate delete records a durable tombstone for the FULL record so a merge/sync can't resurrect it); LOUD-FAILURE (the existing "may reappear" banner stays; the retry now actually makes it land); LIVE-VERIFY (offline/cross-device timing тЖТ V271).
- **Also fixed (same delete/sync-hardening theme):** (1) **Doc Review `deleteReview`** now does the SAME `.select("id")` row-count check (`reviewStore.js`) тАФ it previously reported `ok:true` on a 0-row no-op (silent survivor); it returns `removed` now, matching the sites path. (2) **`onStore` cross-tab filter** now excludes the `:history:` and `:deltomb:` sub-namespaces тАФ the `planarfit:sites:` prefix also matched the version-history ring, so every default save ran the signed-out cross-tab fold 2тАУ3├Ч per edit (harmless no-op via the B591 signature check, but wasteful); tightened to the actual store keys.
- **Verified here (sandbox):** `test/storage.test.js` +7 (suppress owned-pending; keep-on-newer-cross-device; clear-on-landed; don't-suppress-teammate; never-drop-non-tombstoned; backward-compat with no tombstones) ┬╖ full suite 3,391 green ┬╖ build green ┬╖ lint 0 errors ┬╖ `MAP.md` regenerated (new `recordSiteTombstone`/`clearSiteTombstone` exports).
- **тП│ V271 (live, signed-in):** on planyr.io тАФ delete a plan while offline (DevTools Offline), reload signed-in тЖТ the plan STAYS gone (and the cloud row is actually removed once back online); a plan legitimately edited on device B after being deleted on device A survives (cross-device exception). See VERIFICATION.md.
- **DEDUPE-FIRST тАФ the rest of the two-batch brief maps to already-shipped work (no new numbers minted for these):** batch-1 NEW-1 (share never sets team_id) + NEW-2 (realtime RLS "leak") = **B714** (тП│ V244; share DOES set team_id тАФ the bug was autosave reverting it, fixed; realtime is RLS-gated by schema, no leak); NEW-3 (cold-start `reading 'length'` crash) = **B690** (Done) + **B692** (тП│ V232 root-cause sanitize); NEW-4 (offline element lost-update, "reproduced twice") = the **B672** V229 #5 recurrence (fixed) + **B673/B674/B756**. Batch-2: NEW-2 (writeSites strips only underlay) = STALE (B473/B474 shed all three raster homes); NEW-3 (cloud push skipped on local-write fail) = **B473** (`pushModelToCloud`); NEW-5 (phantom "reload before saving" from a fold) = STALE (the B672 architecture retired that banner + the signed-in fold); NEW-6 (wire tombstones into all delete handlers) = **B556/B569/B596/B598/B612** (done). NEW-1 (autosave re-serializes the whole account тАФ a real perf enhancement, not a bug) folded into **B479** as a bullet.

### B756 тАФ DATA LOSS: a new signed-in site created from the map ("Plan N parcels тЖТ") silently loses ALL its parcels `[Site Planner / persistence]` (bug) #site-planner #persistence #infra  *(owner-reported 2026-07-10 from chat тАФ "I deleted [the Bane site], selected all the same parcels, clicked start plan, it created the plan but then all my parcels went away." Branch `claude/parcels-disappear-plan-bug-iofgka`. тЖТ V270 renumbered from V269 on merge-in of `origin/main`, which took V269 for the parcel outline-style editor.)*
`[x]` **FIXED this session тАФ sandbox + integration verified (10 new unit/integration tests, full suite green, build green); the signed-in end-to-end parks in тП│ Verify тЖТ V270.** Confirmed live in Supabase: the reported site `smrfgk3pz3ii` "27211 Hoyt LN, Katy" has 0 parcel rows, 0 tombstones, 0 `site_elements` rows total тАФ the parcels were **never committed**, then wiped. Same 0/0/0 loss on GREEN RIVER, HOLLISTER, WAYSIDE (all created after the 2026-07-06 cutover); every pre-cutover site kept its parcels.
- Verify: live тАФ signed-in, timing/race + concurrency/multi-writer class (mandatory LIVE-VERIFY); the pure fold + engine-commit wiring is proven by unit/integration tests, the real signed-in "Plan parcels тЖТ reload тЖТ rows exist" end-to-end is owed on V270.
- Origin: owner-reported 2026-07-10 (data loss on new sites planned from the map).
- **AUDIT-FIRST тАФ REGRESSION from the B672 read cutover, not the delete.** The delete-then-replan the owner described is INCIDENTAL; the causal flow is "create a new site from the map while signed in." Since B672 (commit `83411c8`, 2026-07-06, entrenched by `ec7b9fc` 2026-07-07) signed-in reads are canonical from the `site_elements` table and `slimForCloud` strips all 5 element collections out of the cloud `sites.data` header. But `newSiteFromMap` (`SitePlannerApp.jsx`) only writes the parcels to localStorage + that slim header тАФ **nothing commits a brand-new site's initial parcels to `site_elements`** (`explodeModel` has zero runtime callers; no DB trigger explodes the blob). On first planner mount, `refetchReplace` (`SitePlanner.jsx`) fetches 0 rows, rebuilds `next.parcels=[]` (rows-canonical), and `setParcels([])` **wipes the canvas BEFORE** the seed-gated write engine (`reconcile()` is a no-op until `seed()`, which runs only inside `refetchReplace`) could ever diff/commit them; the follow-on autosave then `writeMirror()`s the empty state over localStorage too. Net: 0 rows, empty header, empty mirror тЖТ every parcel gone. It's a genuine race (some new sites survived only because the user re-drew shapes after the silent wipe, which then committed).
- **The fix (`SitePlanner.jsx refetchReplace` + a pure helper in `lib/elementRows.js`):** `foldNeverSyncedLocal(next, stateRef.current, rowKeys, isHuskParcel)` folds NEVER-SYNCED local-only elements тАФ those on the pre-replace canvas whose `(kind,id)` has NO row at all (checked against LIVE **and** TOMBSTONE rows) тАФ back into `next` before the replace, so they survive AND the existing `eng.reconcile(merged)` enqueues them as creates тЖТ they finally reach `site_elements`. Bounding the fold to zero-row `(kind,id)`s is what keeps it safe: anything that already has a row is left untouched, so rows stay canonical.
- **Named rules:** LOUD-FAILURE (a silent empty-save passed the B473/B592 count/membership check because want==got==0 тАФ this closes that hole for new sites); TOMBSTONE-DELETES (a remotely-deleted element has a tombstone row тЖТ excluded from the fold тЖТ never resurrected); LIVE-VERIFY (signed-in race class тЖТ V270). Docs: `MAP.md` regenerated same commit (new `foldNeverSyncedLocal` export).
- **Verified (sandbox):** `test/elementRows.test.js` +8 (fold keeps a never-synced local parcel; adopts a live row; never resurrects a tombstone; drops husks; no dup; all 5 collections; `(kind,id)` keying vs the legacy e6327 class; input-immutability) and `test/elementSync.test.js` +2 integration (seed([]) + fold + reconcile тЖТ exactly one `create` commit; a row-backed stale local copy is NOT re-committed тАФ V229 preserved). Full suite green, build green.
- **Safety vs V229 #5 (the exact clobber the cutover added `refetchReplace` to prevent):** a reconnecting stale tab holds old geometry ONLY for elements that already have rows тЖТ those `(kind,id)`s are in `rowKeys` тЖТ excluded from the fold тЖТ row adopted, never a stale rev-guarded re-commit. The fold can only ever emit *creates* for ids the server has literally never seen.
- **DEDUPE-FIRST:** recurrence-of-CLASS of **B473** (Done тАФ "a NEW site's edits vanish on reload when signed in"), whose regression guard `ui-audit/verify-new-site-save.mjs` runs LOGGED-OUT ONLY, which is exactly why the B672 cutover reopened new-site data loss undetected. Filed as a NEW B# (not a B473 reopen) because the mechanism is entirely new (the row cutover, not the blob path). Overlaps **B692** (husk-parcel funnel тАФ same `refetchReplace` husk-filter code); the fold reuses `isHuskParcel` so a husk is never folded.
- **Owner note (recovery):** the fix stops all FUTURE loss. Already-lost sites (Katy/GREEN RIVER/HOLLISTER/WAYSIDE) have no cloud copy of their parcels; the just-planned Katy site is trivially re-created (re-select parcels тЖТ Plan). See V270 / OWNER-TODO for whether older ones held work worth recovering from a device's local version history.

### B625 тАФ Metes-and-bounds deed rotates grossly off-angle on "Align to county parcel" (├Ч2) `[Site Planner]` (bug) #site-planner #coordinates #gis  *(owner-reported 2026-07-02 on Grand Port; original fix shipped that session. RECURRENCE filed 2026-07-10 from chat (Cowork "NEW-1") тАФ the align tool now over-rotates. Reopened per DEDUPE-FIRST / recurrence rule (B636) rather than minting a new B#; branch `claude/metes-bounds-rotation-bug-x58zih`.)*
`[x]` **RE-FIXED this session (recurrence) тАФ sandbox + headless verified; the real-deed/real-parcel end-to-end parks in тП│ Verify тЖТ V197.** The B625 align feature swung a plotted deed to a gross angle (tens of degrees, "~45┬░") instead of the intended small (~1.5┬░) basis-of-bearings correction, so it didn't overlay.
- Verify: live тАФ repro cites real county-parcel project data + GIS import (mandatory LIVE-VERIFY class); the pure alignment math is proven by unit tests, the signed-in real-deed end-to-end is owed on V197.
- Recurrence: 2026-07-10 тАФ owner (Cowork, "NEW-1"): a 67.63-ac deed lands over the 67.004-ac county parcel but badly rotated; a 42.32-ac deed floats with no parcel under it and still gets rotated.
- **AUDIT-FIRST тАФ real cause (the reporter's projection / sign-flip / units leads were ruled OUT):** the bearingтЖТvector parser (`metesAndBounds.js` `bearingToAz`/`callsToPath`) is correct (azimuth CW-from-north, dx=sin, dy=тИТcos, y-down), and deed rings + county rings (`arcgis.js lngLatRingToFeet`) share the SAME y-down feet frame тАФ no sign/mirror bug. The gross rotation came from `deedAlign.js solveDeedAlignment`: it found the rotation by a **full ┬▒180┬░ sweep** minimizing a correspondence-free symmetric nearest-vertex RMS with scale locked to 1, so a near-symmetric / generalized outline snapped to a spurious 45/90/180┬░ alias (the `confident` gate checks residual only, never rotation magnitude). `bestDeedFit` (`SitePlanner.jsx`) compounded it by force-fitting to the lowest-residual parcel even when none corresponded (the floating 42-ac case).
- **The fix (two parts):** (A) `deedAlign.js` тАФ bound the rotation sweep and its clamped refine to a physically-plausible window `MAX_ALIGN_ROT_DEG = 20┬░` (covers grid convergence ~1.5┬░ + record/magnetic basis slop; excludes the aliases); a deed that only fits past the window is reported not-confident, never force-rotated (reversed winding needs no wide sweep тАФ the point-set metric handles it). (B) `SitePlanner.jsx bestDeedFit` тАФ a spatial-correspondence gate (deed must overlap the parcel by тЙе half the smaller footprint via `polyIntersectArea`, AND their areas within ~4:3) so a non-corresponding parcel can't hijack the fit; with none qualifying it falls back to the small, safe grid-convergence correction / "no parcel" message, and the post-plot banner no longer false-claims an offset.
- **Tests:** `test/deedAlign.test.js` тАФ 3 new (13 total): a near-symmetric deed rotated ~1.5┬░ recovers ~1.5┬░ not a 90┬░ alias (would FAIL under the old ┬▒180┬░ sweep тАФ the exact regression); a 45┬░-off deed clamps to тЙд20┬░ + reports not-confident; the `opts.maxRotDeg` override is honoured. Full suite **3302 green** ┬╖ lint 0 errors ┬╖ build green ┬╖ `MAP.md` regenerated (new `MAX_ALIGN_ROT_DEG` export).
- **DEDUPE-FIRST:** this IS the recurrence of B625 (same feature / module / symbols / user goal). Related, NOT dupes: `alignToParcelEdge` (element-edge snapper, bails on polygons) ┬╖ `overlayAlign.solveSimilarityLSQ` (scanned-overlay similarity fit, a separate system) ┬╖ B626 (the stale-sliver *parse*, resolved).

### B755 тАФ Floodplain mitigation reads UNKNOWN because it won't calculate a BFE тАФ auto-DERIVE one from FEMA's Base Flood Elevation lines `[Site Planner / GIS ┬╖ yield]` (feature) #site-planner #gis #yield #floodplain  *(owner-dropped 2026-07-10 with the Bain/Concept A screenshot тАФ "it's not calculating a base flood elevation, so it's not really doing anything useful for me тАж it should calculate a base flood elevation. I don't know why it's not." Owner picked "best estimate, show the conservative high too" over always-round-up. Minted this session as **B752**; RENUMBERED to **B755** = highest B# across both files (B754) + 1 on merge-in of `origin/main`, which took B752/B753 + V265/V266 for the pipeline vector-rendering/easement features and B754/V267 for a COH-ETJ detention fix тАФ the code/tests/commit/branch keep the provisional **B752** label. тЖТ V268. Branch `claude/bain-base-flood-elevation-v2ts85`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED this session тАФ sandbox+headless verified (24 new mitigation + 4 new pipeline unit tests, all green; app boots clean); the real-Bain-GIS derive + the priced volume it produces park in тП│ Verify тЖТ V268.** The mitigation engine needs a 1% BFE to price compensating storage, but FEMA leaves `STATIC_BFE` at the тИТ9999 sentinel on most AE polygons, so the readout honestly dead-ended at "no published BFE on this reach."
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-10 from chat (owner drop)
- **AUDIT-FIRST тАФ the BFE genuinely wasn't on the polygon we queried.** Confirmed against the live FEMA NFHL for the Bain reach (29.7701, тИТ95.8502): the AE zone's `STATIC_BFE` IS тИТ9999, but the BFE lives on the SEPARATE **S_BFE line layer (NFHL sublayer 16)** тАФ 24 whole-foot contour lines (133тАУ146 ft, all Feet/NAVD88) cross the site тАФ which the app never fetched. `assessHydraulicRegime`/`computeMitigation` were correct to read UNKNOWN; the gap was a missing data source, not a bug.
- **Fix (new `bfe-line-interp` provider, slotted after manual, before UNKNOWN):**
  тАв **GIS pipeline** (`vectorLayers.js`) тАФ `featuresToGeoJson` now emits LineString/MultiLineString from Esri `geometry.paths` (it silently dropped every line feature before тАФ the fabricated-empty-result trap); `simplifyGeoJson` passes non-polygons through unthinned (thinning would shift a line off the query point); new `bfeLines` (sublayer 16) + `crossSections` (14, registered-not-consumed) sources.
  тАв **Derivation** (`floodplainMitigation.js`, pure) тАФ `bfeLinesFromFeatureCollection` (feet+NAVD88 guard; тИТ9999/NGVD29/meters excluded and counted тАФ never a mixed-datum silent error) + `deriveBfeFromLines` (distance-weighted interpolation between the nearest line and the nearest DIFFERENT-elevation line тАФ "read a spot elevation between two topo contours"; degrades to nearest-line ┬▒0.5 ft, then to null тЖТ the existing honest UNKNOWN when no line is within 2500 ft).
  тАв **Wiring** (`SitePlanner.jsx`) тАФ `checkDrainage` pulls S_BFE on the same explicit click + SWR cache and derives one BFE at the fill-footprint centroid; threaded through `fmElev.derivedBfeFt`, `fmGoverningBfe` (buildability/FFE), and the mit/pond memo sigs. It NEVER writes to `settings.floodMitigation.bfeFt` (would fake a manual entry); a published static BFE, an AO zone's grade+DEPTH, and a manual entry all still outrank it.
  тАв **Honest labeling (owner option A)** тАФ priced off the central estimate with the conservative upper bracket shown alongside; Yield row tagged "BFE derived", FloodMitigationCard provider "derived (BFE lines)" + a note stating the interpolation, bracket, and "screening estimate тАФ confirm before design; type a BFE to override"; BFE input placeholder shows "~x derived"; print sheet appends "(derived BFE тАФ screening est.)".
- **Named rules:** LOUD-FAILURE (the polyline-drop trap fixed; a failed/empty/out-of-range pull тЖТ honest UNKNOWN, never a fabricated number), AUDIT-FIRST (reconciled against the existing STATIC_BFE path тАФ the тИТ9999 was real), PDF-PARITY (export mirrors the derived tag). Docs: `MAP.md` regenerated same commit (new exports).
- **Verified (sandbox):** `test/floodplainMitigation.test.js` +24 (distToPolyline, the deriveBfeFromLines edge matrix, parser datum/unit guards, provider precedence тАФ manual/static/AO all beat derived, derived-null тЖТ unchanged UNKNOWN) and `test/vectorLayers.test.js` +4 (pathsтЖТline geometry, non-polygon pass-through, the two source rows); full suite **3338 green**, build green, lint 0 errors, headless boot clean.

### B751 тАФ Detention: make the HCFCD-channel-drainage + reviewing-agency assumptions transparent AND user-overridable, and remember the last drainage check `[Site Planner / GIS ┬╖ yield]` (bug+feature) #site-planner #gis #yield #persistence  *(owner-dropped 2026-07-10 with a screenshot of the Bain/Concept A Stormwater readout тАФ "why is it unknown whether the site drains into a[n] HCFCD channel when one literally runs through the middle of the site тАж it should let me know whether it assumes this or not тАж I can click a checkbox and tell it тАж and why does it not know whether it's City of Houston or Harris County flood control district if I have an analysis tool that can detect that?" Owner picked BOTH overrides + "button, but remember it". Minted this session as **B750**; RENUMBERED to **B751** = highest B# across both files (B750) + 1 on merge-in of `origin/main`, which took B750/V263 for the properties-click feature тАФ the code/tests/commit/branch keep the provisional **B750** label. Branch `claude/site-drainage-detection-kp84y0`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED this session тАФ sandbox+headless verified (13 new unit tests + 8 new headless assertions, all green); the real-GIS channel naming on a live Harris/COH site + cross-session persistence on the SIGNED-IN app park in тП│ Verify тЖТ V264.** Two transparency+control gaps, not missing detection.
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-10 from chat (owner drop)
- **AUDIT-FIRST тАФ the detection already existed.** `resolveDrainageContext` already queries the real HCFCD channel centerline layer (`HCFCD/Channels/MapServer/0`) тЖТ `channel.near`, and resolves COH-vs-HCFCD via `identifyJurisdiction`. The panel fed `drainsToHcfcdChannel: drainCtxData?.channel?.near ?? null` with NO user override, so when the HCFCD host was unreachable (or the visible channel isn't an HCFCD unit) `near` came back `null` and the tool hedged "тАжis unknown," dead-ending the user. And the rule badge showed the governing-RATE authority (HCFCD) while the greater-of named Houston тАФ reading as indecision when it's actually Houston's own >20-ac rule.
- **Fix (both owner-chosen options):**
  тАв **Channel Auto/Yes/No control** (segmented, mirrors the pond Outfall toggle) тАФ the user confirms/denies "drains to an HCFCD channel"; the explicit answer overrides detection. State-aware plain-English copy names the detected unit ("HCFCD channel detected тАФ Unit W100-00-00 тАж assuming your detention discharges to it"), or on a failed lookup "Couldn't confirm from HCFCD's map server тАж set Yes or No," or on override the confirmed copy.
  тАв **Reviewing-agency picker** (`<select>`, Auto + every modeled authority) тАФ overrides the resolved authority when the county maps can't (overriding to COH also asserts city-limits so the >20-ac greater-of fires).
  тАв **Greater-of clarity** тАФ names the reviewing authority ("City of Houston, detected from city-limits GIS") DISTINCTLY from the governing rate ("For a tract over 20 acres, Houston applies the larger of its own rate and HCFCD's тАФ тАж so HCFCD's N ac-ft governs"), so it no longer reads as indecision.
  тАв **"Remember it"** тАФ a slim, geometry-free summary of the last check + the two override choices persist in `settings.drainage` (rides the existing settings autosave тАФ NO schema/version bump); on reload the readout shows last-known facts with a "Remembered from your last check on <date> тАФ re-check to refresh" line.
- **Pure helpers (new, unit-tested):** `effectiveChannelDischarge`, `effectiveReviewer`, `DETENTION_AUTHORITY_CHOICES`, `slimDrainageContext`/`hydrateDrainageContext` (round-trip: rule + watershed overlays re-derived, geometry dropped) in `lib/detentionRules.js`. The engine's `drainsToHcfcdChannel` true/false/null branches were already tested.
- **Deliberate boundary (not changed):** the owner/primary-source-verified rule that a >20-ac COH tract defers to HCFCD's rate even on "No" (COH IDM Table 9.5, V204) is surfaced + explained, not re-calibrated тАФ a "No drops it to Houston-rate-only" change would be a separate rule decision.
- **Named rules:** LOUD-FAILURE (a failed channel/jurisdiction lookup shows an honest hedge + the override, never a silent all-clear), AUDIT-FIRST (reconciled against the existing detection engine тАФ extend, not fork), MODULE-SCOPE-COMPONENTS (controls are inline JSX, no inner component). Docs: `MAP.md` regenerated same commit.
- **Verified (sandbox):** `test/detentionRules.test.js` +13 (effective*/choices/slim+hydrate), full suite **3307** green, build green; `ui-audit/verify-b629-detention.mjs` extended to **28/28** тАФ the channel Auto/Yes/No control + detected-unit copy + agency picker render, toggling NoтЖФYes follows the user's choice, and a second COH pass proves the >20-ac greater-of wording + the failed-channel hedge + the Yes override clearing it.

### B754 тАФ Detention: a City-of-Houston **ETJ** parcel was wrongly treated as City-of-Houston for detention criteria `[Site Planner / GIS ┬╖ yield]` (bug) #site-planner #gis #yield  *(owner-dropped 2026-07-10 on the Bain/Concept A readout тАФ "Why does it think this site goes to the city of Houston? It's not in the city of Houston тАж it's just not the city of Houston," then the domain correction: "it IS city of Houston ETJ, but in the city of Houston ETJ, that doesn't mean that city of Houston drainage criteria apply." Minted this session as **B752**; RENUMBERED to **B754** = highest B# across both files (B753) + 1 on merge-in of `origin/main`, which took B752/B753 + V265/V266 for the pipeline vector-rendering feature тАФ the code comments/tests/commit keep the provisional **B752** label. Follows B751, which introduced the "detected from city-limits GIS" wording that exposed this latent mis-routing.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED this session тАФ sandbox+headless verified (unit tests + a new headless spec `verify-etj-detention.mjs`, all green); the live-GIS confirm on the real 27211 Hoyt Ln (Katy) site on the SIGNED-IN app parks in тП│ Verify тЖТ V267.** Being inside a city's ETJ means the city reviews the PLAT, but the COUNTY drainage district's criteria GOVERN detention тАФ it must NOT set the detention reviewer to that city.
- Verify: live
- **AUDIT-FIRST тАФ verified the repro against the LIVE GIS via curl at the parcel's coordinates (29.7722, -95.8548):** city-limits layer (TxGIO) returns **empty** (NOT in any city), the H-GAC ETJ layer returns **HOUSTON**, the county layer returns **Fort Bend**. So the parcel is unincorporated Fort Bend land inside Houston's ETJ. The bug: `authorityForJurisdiction` (`lib/detentionRules.js`) routed `cities.includes("houston") || etjs.includes("houston")` тЖТ `primary="coh"`, so an ETJ-only hit set the reviewer to City of Houston, and the UI hardcoded "(detected from city-limits GIS)" тАФ doubly wrong (it was an ETJ hit, and the city-limits layer says nothing there). Root cause predates B751 (lived in B93/B629); B751's new wording surfaced it.
- **Fix:** ETJ membership WITHOUT actual city-limits membership no longer sets `primary` to `coh`. The COUNTY drainage authority governs (Fort Bend тЖТ FBCDD here), and the Houston-ETJ status is surfaced as an informational `overlays` note + `houston-etj` flag: *"This parcel is in the City of Houston ETJ тАж, not its city limits. Houston reviews the plat, but the COUNTY drainage-district criteria govern detention here тАФ Houston's own detention rate does not apply. Verify with both the City and the county."* Rendered in the Yield/Stormwater readout (`d.etjNotes`). The genuine in-city-limits Houston path (`cities.includes("houston")`) is unchanged, so the >20-ac greater-of + "detected from city-limits GIS" wording now fire ONLY for real city-limits parcels. Removed the now-false `appliesInEtj:true` rule param + rewired the `jurisdiction-partial` flag (a failed ETJ query can no longer imply a hidden City answer; only a failed CITY-limits query can).
- **Named rules:** AUDIT-FIRST (reconciled the claim against the live endpoints before patching), LOUD-FAILURE (the ETJ note is explicit, never a silent re-label), MODULE-SCOPE-COMPONENTS (inline JSX note, no inner component).
- **Verified (sandbox):** `test/detentionResolver.test.js` updated (Houston-ETJтЖТcounty authority + `houston-etj` flag; Fort-Bend-ETJтЖТ`fortbend`; ETJ-outage no longer flags partial), full suite **3308** green, build green; new `ui-audit/verify-etj-detention.mjs` (Fort Bend + Houston-ETJ, no city limits) тЖТ reviewer reads **Fort Bend County Drainage District**, never City of Houston, ETJ note present тАФ 5/5 pass; existing `verify-b629-detention.mjs` COH pass (real city-limits) still green.
- **DEDUPE-FIRST:** searched Open/тП│/Done for ETJ┬╖extraterritorial┬╖reviewing authority┬╖city of houston drainage. Distinct from B751 (transparency/override тАФ works) and B93 (jurisdiction identify). Net-new correctness bug.

### B747 тАФ Overlay tool accepts CAD files: client-side DXF import with true-units auto-scale `[Site Planner]` (feature) #site-planner #files  *(owner-dropped 2026-07-10 as "NEW-1"; the CAD follow-on B67/B72 explicitly deferred. Minted **B747** = highest B# across both files (B746) + 1.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED this session тАФ sandbox+headless verified; the true-units/large-file/reload paths that need a signed-in live app park in тП│ Verify тЖТ V260.** Extend the B72 site-plan overlay to accept `.dxf` files alongside PDF/PNG/JPG, parsing off the main thread and auto-placing at true real-world size when the DXF declares its units.
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-10 from chat (owner NEW-1)
- **Entry point (reused, not forked):** `openOverlayFile` (`lib/overlayPdf.js`) gained an `isDxfFile` branch (extension `.dxf` OR a sniffed `0\nSECTION` header тАФ MIME is unreliable for DXF); the one dropzone + file-picker `accept` list now includes `.dxf`. No second import path.
- **Parse:** one small parse-only dependency authorized + added тАФ **`dxf-parser`** (1 transitive dep `loglevel`, ~380 KB; justification recorded in `/CLAUDE.md` dependency notes). Runs in a dedicated **Web Worker** (`lib/dxf/dxfWorker.js`, import-list test-guarded like `terrainWorker`) so a big drawing never freezes the tab.
- **Render:** hand-rolled entityтЖТSVG for the civil subset тАФ LINE, LWPOLYLINE/POLYLINE (incl. **bulge arcs**), ARC, CIRCLE, ELLIPSE, TEXT/MTEXT (basic placement, no font fidelity), INSERT (blocks expanded recursively with nested transforms). Unsupported entity types are **counted and surfaced** ("Imported тАФ N entities of unsupported types skipped"), never silently dropped. The SVG rasterizes to a transparent PNG at high resolution тЖТ feeds the existing `{src, imgW, imgH}` overlay shape and inherits every move/scale/rotate/opacity handle, `sheetOverlays` rendering, and print/export path unchanged.
- **True-units auto-scale (the payoff):** read `$INSUNITS`. Units known (ft/in/m/mm/cm/тАж) тЖТ compute `ftPerPx` exactly from model-space extents, auto-placed at true size (no B73 calibration needed). `$INSUNITS = 0` (unitless) тЖТ assume feet (correct for ~all Texas civil work) but flag visibly on the panel ("Units assumed: feet тАФ verify") with B73's Trace-a-length / scale controls offered inline. Never a silent guess without the flag.
- **Persistence:** original `.dxf` stored via `overlayStorage.uploadOverlayFile` (`fileKind` extended with `dxf`; 50 MB Storage ceiling applies and oversize now **fails visibly** тАФ a warn banner, per LOUD-FAILURE); raster is a regenerable cache exactly like the PDF path (`slimForCloud` strips it; the reload effect re-renders from stored bytes via a new `rasterizeStoredDxf` branch beside PDF/image).
- **Tests:** unit tests for the entityтЖТSVG geometry (bulge-arc math, INSERT transform composition, `$INSUNITS`тЖТ`ftPerPx`, unsupported counting) with small fixture DXFs; headless Playwright drop-a-DXF smoke.
- **DEDUPE-FIRST:** searched Open/тП│/Done for `dxf`┬╖`dwg`┬╖overlay import. **B72** = drop a PDF/image + place by hand; **B73** = scale calibration/trace; **B238** = the DWGтЖТDXF *backend*; **B364** = Doc-Review *filing* read of scanned/DWG (a different module + purpose). No prior **DXF overlay-import** item тАФ net-new, the CAD follow-on B67/B72 deferred.
