### B749 тАФ Overlay PDF rasterization quality: raise base resolution + zoom-aware re-raster `[Site Planner]` (feature) #site-planner #perf  *(owner-dropped 2026-07-10 as "NEW-3". Minted **B749** = B748 + 1.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED this session тАФ zoom-/data-density-dependent rendering is a mandatory LIVE-VERIFY class тЖТ parks in тП│ Verify тЖТ V262.** Placed PDF overlays went soft when zoomed past sheet-fit because `rasterizePage` capped the raster at `MAX_RASTER_DIM = 2600 px`.
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-10 from chat (owner NEW-3)
- **Tier 1 тАФ raise the base:** `MAX_RASTER_DIM` тЖТ **4500** (scale cap lifted so small sheets sharpen too), with a **row-banded** white-knockout pass so the `getImageData` transient stays bounded at 4500 px (the existing tolerant tainted-canvas catch is kept). Base raster stays a persisted **data URL** (the safety-critical strip/reload/cloud chain is deliberately untouched тАФ zero data-loss regression).
- **Tier 2 тАФ zoom-aware re-raster:** when the overlay's on-screen magnification exceeds ~1.5├Ч its raster pixels, re-render that PDF page at a higher scale (cap **8192 px**, the common GPU texture limit) from the in-session pdf proxy (or, after reload, from stored bytes via `rasterizeStoredPdf`), debounced behind zoom-settle, swapped in place on the SAME transform (placement is anchored to intrinsic PDF points, so resolution changes never move/resize it). The hi-res raster is a **transient revocable object URL** held in a ref (the B45 precedent) тАФ never persisted, never in undo/state bloat тАФ and is dropped back to the base raster + revoked when zoomed out, so multiple hi-res overlays can't accumulate in memory.
- **Not in scope / dedupe:** Doc-Review's separate render-sharpness / white-flash items (B45 object-URL, B414/B415 double-buffer) тАФ this is the **Site Planner overlay path only**; not merged with those.
- **Tests:** unit tests for the scale-selection math (viewport magnification тЖТ chosen raster scale, 8192 cap respected, downgrade threshold).

### B750 тАФ Clicking an element auto-opened its Properties menu; make single-click SELECT and double-click OPEN Properties `[Site Planner / Doc Review]` (feature) #site-planner #doc-review #selection #ui #markup  *(owner-dropped 2026-07-10 from chat: "I don't want clicking on any element to automatically open the properties menu тАФ single left click selects, double left click opens the properties menu." Filed this session as **B747**, but concurrent `main` (PR #569, DXF/DWG overlay import) took B747тАУB749 + V260тАУV262 in the merge тАФ renumbered to **B750** = highest B# across both files (B749) + 1; code/tests/e2e were aligned to **B750** too (тЖТ V263). Branch `claude/properties-menu-click-behavior-dkmh1i`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + unit + headless-e2e verified (Site Planner) this session; parks in тП│ Verify only for the Doc Review live click-through тЖТ V263.** Previously the Properties companion was DERIVED from the selection (`companionSel`), so a plain click popped it open. Now selection and "show Properties" are decoupled: a single click SELECTS only; a **double-click opens Properties**. Text stays editable via the owner's rule тАФ "click to select, then double-click to edit text": a double-click on an ALREADY-selected text-bearing feature (text callout, labeled line/polyline/easement, labeled centerline road) edits its text in place; any other double-click opens Properties. The type/actions menu moved off double-click and stays on **right-click**. Applies to both the Site Planner and the Review markup tool.
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-10 from chat

- **Implementation:** `SitePlanner.jsx` тАФ replaced the `propsDismissed` state with an explicit `propsFor` marker (`{kind,id}` | 'multi' | null); the companion renders only when it matches the current selection (`propsMatches`), so ANY non-double-click selection path (single click, marquee, shift-multi, programmatic, undo/redo) leaves it closed without touching the ~70 `setSel` sites. `isDoubleTap` gained a `wasSel` arg (captured on the first press, read via `dblWasSelRef`) so a double-tap can tell "already-selected text тЖТ edit text" from "тЖТ open Properties". Auto-open-on-DRAW is split by surface тАФ **Review: yes** (its Properties is an always-present rail section; skipping it leaves a blank rail), **Site Planner: no** (its companion is a pop-over тАФ the exact annoyance being removed; double-click or the Properties tab to style a fresh shape). Multi-selection reaches the shared style panel via the Properties tab. Reaching Properties of an already-selected TEXT feature = select something else and come back, or use the Properties tab (the literal consequence of the owner's text rule).
- **Verified (sandbox/headless):** updated the B679 source-text guard block in `test/bugHuntGuards.test.js` (new `isDoubleTap` signature + branches + `propsMatches`/new `companionOpen`/no-typeMenu-on-dblclick). Full unit suite green (3254) ┬╖ full e2e green (43 passed, auth-gated skipped) ┬╖ build green.
- **тП│ V263 (live/browser):** two gaps the sandbox couldn't cover тАФ (a) **Review click-through** (the fixture PDF triggers an OCR pass and the page canvas wasn't ready to accept a drawn rectangle; the repo's own per-tool Review e2e is auth-gated for the same reason): open a drawing in Review тЖТ draw a rect тЖТ Properties auto-show тЖТ deselect тЖТ the Properties section is blank тЖТ single-click the rect тЖТ still blank тЖТ double-click тЖТ Properties show тЖТ double-click an already-selected TEXT note тЖТ the inline text editor opens (not the panel); (b) **Site Planner phone тЬО pill** on a narrow viewport still opens the companion (the e2e ran desktop only).

### B745 тАФ Vector / thin-line GIS map layers (transmission, road-authority, county/city/ETJ boundaries, contours, drainage arrows, OSM/Mapillary) now composite into the PDF/PNG export `[Site Planner / GIS ┬╖ export]` (feature) #site-planner #export #gis  *(split from B739 2026-07-10 тАФ B739 shipped the raster/shaded class; this ships the vector/client-drawn class. тЖТ V259, bumped from V258 which a concurrent `main` merge (the Ctrl+Z item B746) took.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + headless-verified this session; parks in тП│ Verify (Verify: live тАФ PDF/export-parity + GIS-endpoint classes; the sandbox can't reach the live agency hosts through the cert proxy, so the real per-layer geometry-paint needs a live click-through).** Completes the "everything I have on" print request. Each ENABLED vector layer's lat/lon geometry is read live from `overlayRefs`, **reprojected into the site feet frame (`lngLatRingToFeet` тЖТ `f2p`) and redrawn as styled SVG** into the export clone, composited at the SAME z-anchor as the raster overlays (above them, below the drawn geometry).
- Verify: live
- Origin: owner asked 2026-07-10 for "everything I have on" to print; split from B739 so the raster win shipped clean.
- **Implementation:** new pure `lib/overlayVectorSvg.js` (`buildOverlayVectorFragment` + `featureToSvg` + esri/terrain normalizers тАФ LOUD-skip a whole feature on any non-finite vertex, never a partial); `exportVectorOverlaysForFrame` + per-kind adapters in `SitePlanner.jsx` read each live layer sync-only (`eachFeature`/`toGeoJSON`/`eachLayer`/the cached terrain artifact), skip+log anything not loaded / out of frame / not cached (never a silent partial); `buildExportSvg` gets a 7th param and emits each layer's fragment in a `<g data-export-vector>`. Colors/weights/dashes/radii + the terrain palette come verbatim from the live layer (PDF-PARITY); boundary names re-run `labelAnchors`/`placeLabels` against the feet-frame project; drainage arrows rebuild the fixed-px glyph around the projected center; strokes ride the export thinning pass like every plan line. ### B746 тАФ Ctrl+Z doesn't always work; make it Bluebeam-style when drawing an element `[Site Planner / Doc Review]` (bug) #site-planner #doc-review #selection #markup #ui #persistence  *(owner-dropped 2026-07-10 from chat; provisional **B745**, renumbered **B746** тАФ concurrent `main` (PR #566) took B745 for the GIS vector/thin-line export split + V257. Per repo precedent the commit keeps the provisional **B745** label; only the backlog + verification IDs bumped (тЖТ B746 / V258). Branch `claude/ctrl-z-undo-behavior-552b1t`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + unit + headless-e2e verified this session; parks in тП│ Verify only for the live-only edges below тЖТ V258.** Two complaints, one investigation (5-lens adversarial workflow, 15 confirmed root causes RC-1..RC-9): (a) **"Ctrl+Z should work like Bluebeam when drawing"** and (b) **"Ctrl+Z doesn't always work."** The Site Planner's Ctrl+Z always ran a *global* undo тАФ it never stepped back the vertex you were placing тАФ so mid-draw it either did nothing or silently reverted a previously-finished shape while the half-drawn one stayed on screen. Now, in all three canvases (Site Planner, Review, Stitcher), Ctrl+Z **peels the last placed vertex while a multi-point draft is in progress and only falls through to a global undo when no draft is active** (matches Bluebeam + the Review/Stitcher modules, which already did this). Plus a batch of "undo did nothing / undid the wrong thing" reliability fixes.
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-10 from chat
- **DEDUPE-FIRST:** searched Open / тП│ Verify / Done (BACKLOG*.md + BACKLOG_OPEN.md, `^### B` + `#selection`/`#markup`) тАФ **net-new**. Related, NOT dupes: **B32/B105** (no-op history dedup тАФ the engine this builds on), **B315** (undo read a stale baseline тАФ the `stateRef` fix reused here), **B303** (Review's own mid-draw vertex step-back тАФ the sibling pattern the Site Planner was missing), **B567** (color-pick one-frame session тАФ the coalescing pattern extended to opacity sliders here).
- **AUDIT-FIRST тАФ 9 code-confirmed root causes (each adversarially verified):**
  - **RC-1 (Bluebeam, primary):** `SitePlanner.jsx` Ctrl+Z called `undo()` directly, never `removeLastVertex()`. Fixed to `else if (!removeLastVertex()) undo();` (mirrors `DocReview.jsx` / `Stitcher.jsx`).
  - **RC-2:** `applySnapshot` didn't clear in-progress drafts тЖТ a redo/undo could leave phantom draft points floating over reverted geometry. Now nulls every draft (mirrors the siblings).
  - **RC-3:** `removeLastVertex` had no branch for the parcel-edge easement run (`easeEdges`) or the ditch cross-section point (`xsecPts`), and `xsecMode/xsecPts` were missing from the keydown deps тЖТ stale closure. Added both branches + deps.
  - **RC-4:** Split tool double-destruction (Ctrl+Z discarded the whole cut path AND reverted a prior action) тАФ falls out for free once RC-1 lands (mid-split Ctrl+Z now peels one cut point). Verified gone.
  - **RC-5:** Edits that recorded NO undo frame тАФ element fill-opacity slider, underlay opacity slider, sheet-overlay opacity slider + %-box, and **Remove aerial underlay**. Now each records exactly one frame.
  - **RC-6:** Standards / type-style edits called `pushHistory()` but `settings` isn't in the snapshot тЖТ a **dead frame** that misdirected the next Ctrl+Z into deleting a prior shape. Removed those pushes (Standards are prefs, non-undoable like the 20+ sibling settings fields) тАФ no more misdirection.
  - **RC-7:** Markup fill-opacity slider *flooded* history (one frame per `onChange`) тЖТ ~20 Ctrl+Z to undo one drag. All opacity sliders now share one `sliderHistory` coalescing helper (one frame per drag).
  - **RC-8:** Sheet-overlay position was `Math.round`ed in `histKey`, so a sub-foot (zoomed-in) nudge was dedup'd away as a no-op and skipped by undo. Removed the rounding (underlay position never was).
  - **RC-9:** The keydown input-guard diverged тАФ Review/Stitcher skipped only INPUT/TEXTAREA, so a focused `<select>`'s Ctrl+Z hit the canvas. Added SELECT/contentEditable so all three modules gate identically.
- **Fix (files):** `SitePlanner.jsx` (Ctrl+Z routing, `removeLastVertex`тЖТpure resolver, `applySnapshot` draft-clear, `histKey` overlay precision, 5 opacity sliders + remove-underlay history, RC-6 dead-push removals, deps); new pure **`lib/drafts.js`** (`resolveDraftStepBack`); `DocReview.jsx` + `Stitcher.jsx` (RC-9 guard).
- **Verified (sandbox/headless):** new **`test/drafts.test.js`** (10 cases тАФ every draft type incl. the two new ones + the "no draft тЖТ null" fall-through that keeps a real Ctrl+Z from being swallowed) ┬╖ full unit suite green (3232) ┬╖ `test/history.test.js` still green ┬╖ build green ┬╖ MAP.md regenerated (+`lib/drafts.js`) ┬╖ **new `e2e/ctrlz-undo.spec.js` (3 tests, LOGGED-OUT via "Start blank", green in headless Chromium): mid-draw Ctrl+Z peels a vertex (finished polygon has 3 pts, not 5); mid-draw Ctrl+Z does NOT revert a previously-committed shape; no-draft Ctrl+Z is a real global undo + redo.**
- **тП│ V258 (live, planyr.io):** the few edges the logged-out sandbox can't confirm тАФ (1) a **sub-foot sheet-overlay nudge at high zoom** undoes cleanly (RC-8, zoom-dependent-rendering class); (2) **Remove aerial underlay тЖТ Ctrl+Z restores it**, incl. the reload-after-undo persistence edge where the image was cloud/idb-backed (RC-5, signed-in persistence class); (3) opacity-slider undos that round-trip through Supabase/Drive persistence.

### B744 тАФ "Drop site plan" overlay hint sticks after a drag leaves the window; make it non-obscuring `[Site Planner]` (bug) #site-planner #ui  *(owner-dropped 2026-07-09 as "NEW-1"; provisional **B736**, renumbered **B744** тАФ fast-moving concurrent `main` took B734тАУB743 + V250тАУV255 across several merges. Per repo precedent the code/tests/commit keep the provisional **B736** label; only the backlog + verification IDs bumped (тЖТ B744 / V256). Branch `claude/site-planner-overlay-bugs-yzkalh`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + headless-verified this session; parks in тП│ Verify (Verify: live тАФ HTML5/OS drag interaction; the real browser drag layer only reproduces live, the synthetic e2e proves the wiring) тЖТ V256.** The full-canvas "Drop site plan to place it on the map" drag hint could stay stuck ON after a file was dragged over the canvas and then back OUT of the browser window without dropping; and while shown its light-theme fill was opaque, hiding existing geometry. The highlight is now driven by a dragenter/dragleave DEPTH COUNTER + a window-level reset, and its fill is a translucent accent wash (both themes) so the site stays visible under it.
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-09 from chat
- **AUDIT-FIRST тАФ the report's Part A does NOT reproduce.** The report described a "persistent full-canvas takeover that covers geometry + blocks clicks." It doesn't exist: the overlay (`SitePlanner.jsx` ~9453) mounts ONLY while `canvasDropOver` is true (an active file drag) and is already `pointerEvents:none`, so it never blocks a click and there is no persistent empty-state takeover (grep-confirmed: the exact hint string appears once; there is no other full-canvas prompt). **B445 already made it drag-gated + click-through.** Part A is therefore honored in *spirit* only тАФ a non-obscuring translucent fill тАФ not by gating a non-existent persistent overlay on emptiness.
- **Part B (the real defect):** the canvas wrapper's `onDragLeave` only cleared when `e.currentTarget === e.target` (false whenever the pointer was over the child `<svg>` at exit), and the window guard listened only for `dragover`/`drop` тАФ NO window `dragleave`/reset. An OS-file drag fires no in-page `dragend`, and its final window-exit `dragleave` can target `document`/`body` (outside the wrapper subtree), so nothing cleared the flag тЖТ the tan highlight stuck on with nothing under the cursor.
- **Fix (`SitePlanner.jsx`):** (1) both dropzones (canvas wrapper + References panel) now use a per-zone dragenter/dragleave DEPTH COUNTER ref тАФ highlight iff depth>0, force depth=0 on drop тАФ robust against the child-crossing flicker (a child's bubbling `dragenter` fires before the parent's `dragleave`, so depth never dips to 0 mid-hover) and replacing the fragile `currentTarget===target` guard. (2) The window guard `useEffect` gains a `dragleave` listener that hard-resets ALL drag-hover flags + both counters, but ONLY when the drag truly left the window (`relatedTarget==null` **AND** pointer coords at/past a viewport edge тАФ AND, **not the brief's OR**, because Chromium routinely reports a null `relatedTarget` on in-page moves too, so a bare OR would re-introduce the flicker), plus the window `drop` handler now also resets (catch-all for an aborted/missed drop). `preventDefault` on dragover (drop stays allowed) + the panel drop's `stopPropagation` are preserved. (3) Part A spirit: the hint fill is now `color-mix(in srgb, <accent> 18%, transparent)` in both themes (was opaque `canvasAccentSoft` in light) so geometry shows through; `pointerEvents:none` kept; the shared `canvasAccentSoft` token untouched.
- **DEDUPE-FIRST:** searched Open / тП│ Verify / Done тАФ **distinct from B445 / V131** (which BUILT this affordance; shared symbols `canvasDropOver`, the window-guard `useEffect`, `verify-overlay-dnd.mjs`). This is a GAP in B445's edge-case reset (leave-window), NOT a regression тАФ B445's drop/feedback fix still works тАФ so per the repo's gaps-get-new-numbers convention (cf. B446 "GAP in B294", B450 "follow-up to B239") it takes a new number, not a B445 recurrence. Deed dropzone (`deedDrag`, in a modal) left as-is тАФ it clears on any dragleave (never "stuck") and is now covered by the window reset.
- **Verified (sandbox/headless):** `ui-audit/verify-overlay-dnd.mjs` (logged-out, real built app on :4173) тАФ **11/11**, including the three new B736 assertions: enter├Ч2 (wrapper + bubbled child) then one child `dragleave` KEEPS the hint (no flicker) and clears only at depth 0; a window `dragleave` (`relatedTarget=null` + coords-outside) clears a stuck hint; a window `drop` preventDefaults + resets. Also repaired pre-existing harness drift (B654 renamed the rail "Overlay"тЖТ"References", the panel copy, and the overlay-row title). Full unit suite green (3161) ┬╖ lint 0 errors ┬╖ build green. (No MAP.md change тАФ no files added/removed/renamed.)
- **тП│ V256 (live, on planyr.io):** the synthetic e2e proves the wiring deterministically, but a real desktop OS file-drag exercises the browser's native drag layer end-to-end. On planyr.io: (1) canvas with a parcel + placed metes-and-bounds and no backdrop тЖТ geometry visible + canvas clickable, no full-canvas takeover; (2) drag a file in and back out of the window without dropping тЖТ no residual highlight; (3) truly empty canvas тЖТ dropping a site plan still places the backdrop; (4) drag a file over a canvas that has geometry тЖТ the site stays visible under the translucent hint (light theme).
### B742 тАФ Delete on a road silently no-ops for many clicks, then suddenly works `[Site Planner]` (bug) #site-planner #road #selection #persistence #ui  *(owner-dropped 2026-07-09 as "NEW-1"; provisional **B736**, renumbered **B742** тАФ fast-moving concurrent `main` took B734тАУB741 + V250тАУV254 across several merges. Per repo precedent the code/tests/commit keep the provisional **B736** label; only the backlog + verification IDs bumped (тЖТ B742 / V255). Branch `claude/road-delete-intermittent-tjrn4s`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + headless-verified this session; parks in тП│ Verify (Verify: live тАФ the cloud-sync half is signed-in only + a timing/persistence class) тЖТ V255.** Selecting a road and pressing/clicking Delete did nothing for ~20 tries, then one finally deleted it. Now a single Delete removes the selected road immediately (button OR keyboard) and never silently no-ops тАФ if a delete can't proceed it visibly falls through to a whole-element delete, and a failed cloud save surfaces loudly.
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-09 from chat
- **DEDUPE-FIRST:** searched Open / тП│ Verify / Done (BACKLOG*.md + BACKLOG_OPEN.md) тАФ **net-new**, no item covers this. Nearest prior art (NOT dupes): **B673** (element-sync loud-conflict + delete/edit matrix тАФ the conflict *policy*, not this local-no-op/wedge); **B230/B718** (the control-point add/delete feature this bug was mis-firing through); **B372** (a deleted *site* resurrecting тАФ different object, the localStorage unmount-flush).
- **AUDIT-FIRST тАФ three real defects, code-confirmed (not the report's single guess):**
  1. **Road keyboard-Delete trap (primary).** With a road selected and an interior control point *armed* (`selVtx`), `SitePlanner.jsx:2697` routed Delete to `deleteVtx` and `return`ed unconditionally. `deleteVtx`'s road branch (`:3638-3660`) early-returned on a non-removable/**stale** index (endpoint, 2-pt min, or an index gone out-of-range after the road's geometry changed under the armed selection тАФ e.g. a realtime refetch replaced `els`) **without clearing `selVtx`**. So every later Delete re-hit that branch and no-op'd until Escape / a background click reset `selVtx` тАФ "then it finally worked."
  2. **Right-click menu deletes stale selection** (`:12494`): `setSel({kind:"el",id}); deleteSel()` тАФ `deleteSel` reads a ref `setSel` hasn't synchronously updated, so it acted on the previous selection (wrong element, or a no-op).
  3. **Silent cloud-sync wedge** (`elementSync.js:205-230` + `elementApi.js`): the per-element commit had **no timeout**, so a hung `commit_elements` left the single `inflight` slot stuck TRUE forever тАФ all element writes (incl. deletes) piled up unsent, badge stuck "saving", flooding out only when the stall cleared (the persistence-side "then it worked").
- **Fix:**
  - `deleteVtx` now returns a **boolean** (true only when it actually removed a point) and clears `selVtx`+`roadVtxSel` on every no-op/guard path; the keyboard branch (`:2697`) gained `&& deleteVtx(...)` so a no-op **falls through** to the whole-element `deleteSel()` тАФ Delete is never a dead key.
  - `deleteSel(target)` accepts an optional explicit `{kind,id}` (guarded on `.kind` so the five bare `onClick={deleteSel}` buttons that pass an event still fall back to the live ref); the context menu passes the clicked id directly.
  - RoadVtx **drag-end** clears `selVtx`, so reshaping a control point and then pressing Delete deletes the whole road (a deliberate plain click on a dot still arms it for a targeted vertex-delete).
  - `commitElements`/`fetchElements` (`elementApi.js`) bounded by **`COMMIT_TIMEOUT_MS = 8000`** (AbortController + `Promise.race`, mirrors `PARCEL_FETCH_TIMEOUT_MS`) тЖТ a hung request resolves `{ok:false}` тЖТ `onTransportFailure` retries/backs off тЖТ after `maxAttempts` the state goes `failed` тЖТ the existing red "error"/Retry badge (LOUD-FAILURE). This also closes the resurrection window (a delete that never lands can no longer be silently rebuilt by a refetch).
- **Verified (sandbox/headless):** new `test/elementApi.test.js` cases (hung commit тЖТ `{ok:false, /timeout/}`; abort-signal wired through; hung fetch тЖТ ok:false) ┬╖ full unit suite green (3164) ┬╖ build green ┬╖ MAP.md regenerated ┬╖ **`e2e/element-delete.spec.js` (3 tests, LOGGED-OUT via "Start blank" + a real drawn centerline road, green in headless Chromium): panel "Delete element" removes the road and it stays gone after reload; keyboard Delete after arming an interior control point removes just that vertex (road survives, pts 4тЖТ3) then a second Delete removes the whole road тАФ NO WEDGE; and reshape-drag a control point then Delete removes the whole road. 0 page errors.**
- **тП│ V255 (live, on planyr.io, SIGNED IN тАФ the sandbox can't sign in):** the cloud-sync half only. Delete a road with cloud on тЖТ it persists and stays deleted across a tab-switch + reload (no resurrection); and on a genuinely slow/failed commit the sync badge flips to "error/Retry" (not stuck on "saving").

### B740 тАФ Shift-click multi-select + shared property editing (opacity/style) `[Site Planner]` (feature) #site-planner #selection #ui #markup  *(owner-dropped 2026-07-09 as "NEW-1"; provisional **B734**, renumbered **B740** тАФ concurrent `main` took B734тАУB739 + V250тАУV252. - **Visuals:** per-member rotation-aware OBB outlines (reuse `elRingFeet`/`ptsOf`) that hug an angled strip's real footprint, wrapped in `data-export="skip"` (also closes a latent export-leak of the old bare multi chrome); single-element transform grips suppressed while multi>1 (property editing only тАФ no group transform handles).

### B738 тАФ Satellite/aerial basemap missing from PDF/PNG export (plan prints on a blank white background) `[Site Planner]` (bug) #site-planner #export #gis  *(owner-dropped 2026-07-09 as "NEW-1"; provisional **B735**, renumbered **B738** тАФ concurrent `main` (PRs #557/#559/#560) took B734/B735/B736/B737 + V250/V251. Per repo precedent the code/tests/commit keep the provisional **B735** label; only the backlog + verification IDs bumped (тЖТ B738 / V252). Branch `claude/pdf-export-cors-imagery-4l1f8d`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + headless-verified this session; parks in тП│ Verify (Verify: live тАФ PDF/export parity + GIS endpoint behavior, both mandatory-live classes) тЖТ V252.** With the satellite/aerial basemap on, Print/Download PDF (and Download PNG) produced the vectors on a blank white background тАФ the imagery was dropped. The export now composites the on-screen aerial into the sheet, and a fetch that can't be inlined warns loudly instead of silently emitting a background-less file.
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-09 from chat
- **DEDUPE-FIRST:** searched Open / тП│ Verify / Done (BACKLOG*.md + BACKLOG_OPEN.md) тАФ **net-new**, no existing item covers the aerial missing from the export. Nearest prior art to BUILD ON, NOT dupes: **B50** (Done тАФ made a *tainted-canvas* export failure surface an alert instead of a silent no-op; this is a different, more common failure тАФ a **dropped** image, not a thrown taint); **B202** (Done тАФ time-boxed + parallelized `inlineImages` so a hung tile can't stall print prep; introduced the very `dropOnFail` that this bug turns silent); **B693** (the Off/Aerial/USGS basemap control). The chat's own "NEW-2/NEW-3" bullets were gotchas on this one item, not separate numbers.
- **AUDIT-FIRST тАФ the chat's leading hypothesis (a CORS-tainted canvas swallowing a SecurityError) did NOT match the code.** The export does not rasterize the live Leaflet DOM; `buildExportSvg` clones ONLY `svgRef.current`. The live basemap is a **sibling `<div ref={geoWrapRef}>`** (Leaflet tiles, `data-export="skip"`, zIndex 0) that the SVG clone never captures. So the export's only aerial source was the persisted `underlay` `<image>`. Two ways that goes blank: (1) **basemap on with no `underlay`** (a located site whose from-map capture is absent, or the underlay removed) тЖТ the SVG had no aerial at all; (2) `underlay.src` is a remote ArcGIS `export` URL and `inlineImages(dropOnFail=true)` **silently dropped** it on any fetch hiccup тЖТ white background, no error (a LOUD-FAILURE violation). CORS itself is fine: `server.arcgisonline.com` `export` **and** `tile` endpoints return `Access-Control-Allow-Origin: *` (curl-verified), so a plain `fetch` inlines cleanly to a data URL (no taint).
- **Fix (three parts):**
  1. **Capture the live basemap for the export.** New `SitePlanner.exportAerialForFrame(frame)`: when `origin && basemapOn`, synthesize a **frame-exact** aerial by requesting the ACTIVE source's `export` endpoint (`BASEMAPS[basemapSrc].export` тАФ Esri or USGS) sized to the printed area, placed in the SAME feet frame as the parcels so it aligns pixel-for-pixel. This is the same technique the from-map underlay already uses тАФ reused, not reinvented.
  2. **Geometry:** new pure `feetExtentToBbox(ext, lat0, lon0)` in `lib/arcgis.js` (planner feet тЖТ lon/lat bbox; +x EAST, +y SOUTH), which `aerialPlacement` reverses exactly (proven by a round-trip unit test). `buildExportSvg` now takes an `exportAerial` and draws `aerial = exportAerial || underlay` (so the dropped-screenshot / basemap-off paths are unchanged), tagging the `<image>` `data-export-aerial`.
  3. **LOUD-FAILURE:** `inlineImages` now returns `{ aerialDropped }`; `exportPDF`/`exportPNG` `flashWarn` the user ("тЪа Couldn't load the satellite imagery, so the PDF was exported without itтАж") on the **success path** (after the file downloads, so a later encode failure can't leave a contradictory toast), with the **`тЪа` prefix that flips the banner to the red warning colour** (without it the notice rendered on the success-green тАФ B341-class).
  4. **Extent unification (review-driven).** Both `buildExportSvg` and `exportAerialForFrame` now crop to ONE shared `exportFeetExtent(frame)` (frame тЖТ dev тЖТ parcels тЖТ underlay bounds), and a reliable data-URL underlay is drawn BENEATH the live synth as a fallback тАФ so a dropped fetch can't regress a previously-good export to white.
- **Adversarial review (4-lens Workflow + per-finding verify) caught a real gap before merge:** the first cut returned `null` from `exportAerialForFrame` for a **parcels-only site** (deed imported, no massing yet) with no print frame, because it keyed on `devExtent()` alone (which ignores `parcels`) while `buildExportSvg` still framed the parcels тАФ so that (very common) state *still* silently exported white. Part 4 above fixes it; a `test/bugHuntGuards.test.js` guard locks the shared-extent wiring so it can't regress.
- **Verified (sandbox/headless):** `test/aerialExport.test.js` (3 tests тАФ `feetExtentToBbox` north/south orientation, exact round-trip through `aerialPlacement` reconstructing the feet extent, and the `maxPx` export-ceiling clamp) ┬╖ new **B735 guard** in `test/bugHuntGuards.test.js` (shared `exportFeetExtent` + `data-export-aerial` marker + `aerialDropped` signal all present) ┬╖ **`ui-audit/verify-aerial-export-cors.mjs` (real headless Chromium, runs the ACTUAL `inlineImages` loop): a cross-origin image served with `Access-Control-Allow-Origin: *` (identical CORS to Esri тАФ asserted live by curl in the same script) inlines to a data URL, does NOT taint the canvas, and rasterizes into the backdrop (100% non-white, high colour variety); an unreachable aerial URL sets `aerialDropped=true` and drops the `<image>` (the LOUD-FAILURE contract)** ┬╖ existing `ui-audit/verify-pdf-export.mjs` still green (no regression) ┬╖ full unit suite **3,151 green** ┬╖ lint 0 errors ┬╖ build green ┬╖ MAP.md regenerated (new `arcgis.js` export). NOTE: the live Esri `export` fetch could not be exercised from the *sandbox* browser (the egress proxy resets headless Chromium's TLS tunnel to arcgisonline, and blocks `basemap.nationalmap.gov` outright тАФ 403 CONNECT; curl over HTTP/1.1 reaches Esri). So **Esri CORS `*` is curl-verified; USGS is expected (stock ArcGIS Server defaults AllowedOrigins=*) but pending the live check** тАФ and if USGS turns out non-CORS, the LOUD warning fires (no silent white). A real browser at planyr.io has no proxy.
- **тП│ V252 (live, on planyr.io):** locate a real site тЖТ confirm the satellite backdrop is ON тЖТ **Download PDF**: the imagery must be the background with parcels/setbacks/markups/massing on top (repeat with the print frame set, and once with the **USGS** source). Then **Download PNG** тЖТ same. Toggle the basemap OFF (or a dropped-screenshot underlay) тЖТ export still behaves as before. Optional: throttle/kill the network mid-export тЖТ the "couldn't load the satellite imagery" warning shows and the file still downloads (no silent white). Also spot-check that a placed site-plan overlay + the "Print overlay" toggle still composite correctly above the aerial.

### B719 тАФ Road curb/border drawn far too thick: size it to a true 6тА│ (0.5тА▓) curb, to scale `[Site Planner]` (bug) #site-planner #road #ui  *(owner-dropped 2026-07-08 as "NEW-2"; minted **B719** = highest B# across both files (B718) + 1. Branch `claude/road-editing-curb-scale-r1u2sw`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + headless-verified this session; parks in тП│ Verify (Verify: live тАФ zoom-/data-density-dependent rendering + PDF/print export parity, both mandatory-live classes) тЖТ V248.** A road's edge/curb line rendered as a fat pixel band unrelated to real size; it now represents a true **6тА│ (0.5 US survey ft)** curb, sized `curb ├Ч ppf`, so it reads as a thin to-scale line at site zoom and grows proportionally on zoom-in.
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-08 from chat
- **DEDUPE-FIRST:** B70/B71 define the curb *contract* (6тА│ default / 12тА│ trailer, three-way draw/calc/dimension rule); B180/B181 cover curb in the *cost/area* takeoff; B601 renders the centerline road surface+curb. None address the render *stroke weight* тАФ this is a pure visual-scale fix, no new number needed elsewhere.
- **Root cause:** the centerline road's pavement edge + curb stripes (and the legacy rect road's) were stroked with `strokeZoom(...)` тАФ a near-constant pixel weight (тЙИ5тАУ7px edge / тЙИ3px stripe at site zoom), clamped, with no tie to the 6тА│ curb. A real 6тА│ curb is `0.5 ├Ч ppf` px (sub-pixel at overview zoom), so the strokes read as a fat band many times the true curb.
- **Fix:** new pure `curbStrokePx(curbFt, ppf, minPx)` in `lib/roadGeometry.js` (floored so it stays visible sub-pixel, NO ceiling тЖТ proportional on zoom-in). `SitePlanner.jsx` road render: the centerline pavement edge + curb stripes and the legacy rect road's border + stripes now use `curbStrokePx(roadCurbWidth(el), ppf, CURB_STROKE_MIN_PX=0.75)`. No new geometry / data тАФ purely edge styling sized to 6тА│ (a 12тА│ trailer curb renders exactly 2├Ч via the same formula). Selection cue stays the blue handles (B619). Export parity holds by construction (`printSheet.js` clones the live SVG).
- **Verified (sandbox/headless):** `test/roadGeometry.test.js` `curbStrokePx` cases (to-scale above floor / floored sub-pixel / non-finite guard) ┬╖ `test/bugHuntGuards.test.js` new B719 guard (roads use `curbStrokePx`, not `strokeZoom`) ┬╖ full suite green ┬╖ lint 0 errors ┬╖ build green ┬╖ MAP regenerated. **`ui-audit/verify-b718-b719.mjs` (logged-out, real app): the 6тА│ curb stripe = 1.03px at fit (vs the old ~3px band) and a 12тА│ curb road = 2.06px тАФ ratio exactly 2.00, proving stroke = curb ├Ч ppf (to scale), not a fixed pixel weight; the road still renders as a filled, legible strip; 0 page errors.**
- **тП│ V248 (live, on planyr.io):** eyeball the thin to-scale curb on a real project at several zooms (and nudge the 0.75px floor up if it reads faint at overview zoom), and confirm the PDF/print export shows the same thin curb (PDF-PARITY тАФ the export clones the live SVG so parity is expected, but this is a mandatory-live class).

### B734 тАФ Account dropdown opens pinned to the top-left corner instead of under the account pill `[App Shell / UI]` (bug) #ui #infra  *(owner-dropped 2026-07-09 as "NEW-1"; **B734** = highest B# across both files (B733) + 1. Branch `claude/account-menu-positioning-frp60c`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + sandbox/headless-verified this session; parks in тП│ Verify (Verify: live тАФ the account dropdown is signed-in-only and the sandbox can't sign in) тЖТ V250.** Clicking the signed-in account pill ("Michael Butler" + avatar) at the header's top-right opened its dropdown (Profile / Team / Settings / Sign out) pinned to the **top-left corner** of the viewport; it now drops straight down under the pill, right-aligned, staying inside the screen edge.
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-09 from chat
- **DEDUPE-FIRST:** searched Open / тП│ Verify / Done (BACKLOG*.md + BACKLOG_OPEN.md) тАФ **net-new**, no existing item covers the account/user/profile dropdown position. Nearest prior art to BUILD ON, NOT a dupe: **B127** (Done тАФ built `src/shared/ui/AnchoredMenu.jsx`, the portal-to-body rect-anchored menu the account dropdown already uses; that bug was menus *clipped/behind* the rail, a different symptom). Account-name/identity-pill work (B297/B298) is the pill itself, not its menu position.
- **AUDIT-FIRST тАФ the report's guess was wrong.** The report suspected a missing `position`/lost `position:relative`. Neither: `AnchoredMenu`'s math and the account menu's `placement="below-right"` were already correct. **Real cause:** Shell built ONE `authControl` element (with a single `acctAnchor` ref + `<AnchoredMenu>`) and the keep-alive render (2026-07-05) passes that SAME element into **every visited workspace's `AppHeader`** тАФ up to 5 mount at once (Site map header + Site plan header + DocReview + Library + Scheduler), most `display:none`. All the button copies shared one `acctAnchor`, so `acctAnchor.current` resolved to whichever copy React committed last тАФ usually a hidden one. `getBoundingClientRect()` on a `display:none` element is all-zeros, so `below-right` (`left = a.right - mw`) went negative тЖТ clamped to (8px, 8px) = top-left. Explains why it was fine on a fresh load but broke after switching workspaces/modes once. Every OTHER `AnchoredMenu` consumer already creates its anchor ref *locally inside its own component* (e.g. `SettingsMenu`, `ProjectBreadcrumb`) тАФ so it never had this bug.
- **Fix:** extracted the whole auth surface into a self-contained **`src/app/AccountControl.jsx`** (own `acctAnchor` ref + `acctOpen`/`cloudNote` state per instance). Passing the same `<AccountControl/>` element to multiple `{authControl}` slots creates an INDEPENDENT component instance (independent hooks) at each fiber position, so each mounted header anchors to its OWN visible button and only the clicked one opens тАФ the SettingsMenu/ProjectBreadcrumb pattern (MODULE-SCOPE-COMPONENTS). Shell now just builds `<AccountControl user profileApi onOpenAuth onOpenAccount />` and keeps driving the `AuthPanel` modal; no workspace forwarder or `AppHeader` changed. Secondary class-wide hardening: lifted `AnchoredMenu`'s placement math into pure, unit-tested **`src/shared/ui/anchoredMenuPlacement.js` (`placeMenu`)**, which returns `null` for a zero-sized anchor so a mis-anchored menu stays *hidden* instead of pinning to the corner (all three placements тАФ `left`/`below-left`/`below-right` тАФ preserved, so no other consumer regresses).
- **Verified (sandbox/headless):** new `test/anchoredMenuPlacement.test.js` (8 cases тАФ below-right/below-left/left anchoring, right/bottom/left clamps, zero-rect тЖТ null, missing тЖТ null) ┬╖ B557 account-email null-guard test repointed to `AccountControl.jsx` (the guard rode with the code) ┬╖ full unit suite green (3147) ┬╖ lint 0 errors ┬╖ build green ┬╖ MAP.md + shared folder-pointer regenerated. Headless logged-out smoke: app boots clean, no stray menu at the corner, and another `AnchoredMenu` consumer still positions correctly (the shared-`placeMenu` refactor didn't regress it).
- **тП│ V250 (live, on planyr.io, SIGNED IN тАФ the sandbox can't sign in):** open the account pill тЖТ menu drops directly under it, right-aligned, fully on-screen; switch workspaces/modes and reopen тЖТ still anchored under the pill (never top-left, no duplicate/stacked menus); Esc + click-outside still dismiss.

### B715 тАФ Site acreage double-counts overlapping active parcels: DISSOLVE the rings so shared ground counts once (Martini 176.6 тЖТ ~88.6 ac) `[Site Planner / Yield ┬╖ Analysis]` (bug) #site-planner #yield  *(owner/Cowork intake 2026-07-08, arrived as "NEW-1"; **B715** = highest B# across both files (B714) + 1. `[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + sandbox-verified this session; parks in тП│ Verify (Verify: live тАФ repro cites real project data `smqsfzqc72pw`) тЖТ V245.** Site acreage now DISSOLVES overlapping active parcels (counts shared ground once) instead of an additive shoelace sum.
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-08 from chat
- **Root cause (grounded on `main`):** three additive sums, none union тАФ `SitePlanner.jsx:5608` `siteSqft`, `:11229` analysis header, `MapFinder.jsx:201` map tooltip/list (the last also summed EVERY parcel, no active filter). Martini (`smqsfzqc72pw`) read 176.55 ac; two attr-less hand-drawn outlines (38.76 + 49.19 ac) overlapped the real parcels тЖТ 176.55 тИТ 87.95 = 88.60 geometric.
- **Fix:** new pure `dissolvedParcelSqft(parcels[, overlapPairs])` in `lib/polyClip.js` тАФ reuses the already-bundled **`clipper-lib` `ClipType.ctUnion`** (same engine as `pondOffset.js`; feetтЖТcenti-feet integer grid). FAST PATH returns the exact additive sum when there are 0/1 valid rings or NO overlapping pair (`overlappingParcelPairs` empty тАФ adjacent lots share only an edge), so every normal, non-overlapping site is byte-identical to the old number (no rounding jitter); clipper runs only on genuine overlap. Wired into all three sites; the hot render path computes the overlap pairs ONCE and reuses them for both the area and the B652 warning. MapFinder now also filters to active parcels. B652 warning copy updated (area is now correct тАФ the warning flags the duplicate to review, no longer claims inflation).
- **Verified (sandbox):** `test/polyClip.test.js` +9 tests (disjoint/adjacent тЖТ exact sum; identical/partial/contained тЖТ union; the Martini shape: two outlines over four tiles тЖТ 10,000 not 30,000; inactive excluded; husk/degenerate rings skipped; precomputed-pairs contract) ┬╖ full suite **3,107 green** ┬╖ lint 0 errors ┬╖ build green ┬╖ MAP regenerated.

### B704 тАФ 1-ft labeled contour lines, client-generated from the raw 3DEP DEM in a Web Worker `[Site Planner / GIS]` (feature) #site-planner #gis #perf  *(owner brief 2026-07-07, arrived as "NEW-2"; **B704** = B703 + 1. Branch `claude/elevation-houston-relief-7co7do`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + headless-verified this session; parks (Verify: live тАФ GIS endpoint + zoom-/data-density-dependent rendering classes) тЖТ V240.**
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-07 from chat
- **Why client-side:** the public service's canned contour renderings are raster-only, unlabeled, and (at best preset) 2-ft тАФ no labeled 1-ft vector lines exist server-side. The raw grid path was probe-verified first: `exportImage?format=lerc&pixelType=F32&renderingRule=None` returns LERC1 (`CntZImage`), decoded with the official `lerc` npm package; a real Katy tile is committed as `test/fixtures/dep-katy-463x400.lerc` (463├Ч400 F32, 120.9тАУ149.8 ft тАФ drives the decode-contract tests without network).
- **What shipped (new deps: `lerc` + `d3-contour`, both small тАФ the two the brief authorized):**
  - **Pure core** (`lib/demGrid.js`, `lib/contours.js`): deterministic snapped-tile grid requests (key тЖФ bbox bijection; smoothing margin baked in; oversized viewports coarsen deterministically; `adjustAspectRatio=false` + size computed to match the bbox aspect exactly тАФ a silently adjusted bbox would shift every contour, and a size mismatch on decode REFUSES loudly); LERC magic-byte sniff (the dev server SPA-fallbacks `/api/*` to index.html тАФ "response arrived" тЙа "response is a grid"); meters тЖТ survey-ft on decode (`M_TO_FT` now exported from `elevation.js` тАФ one conversion for every 3DEP consumer); normalized MASKED gaussian smooth (voids never bleed; unsmoothed 1-ft contours from ┬▒0.1тАУ0.3 ft LiDAR noise are jagged spaghetti); marching squares via `d3-contour` with **sentinel-embedded voids** (never NaN тАФ d3's smoothing emits NaN coords and Leaflet throws) and **two strip passes** (grid-border frame + dilated-void halo, so lines BREAK at water instead of bridging or outlining it); pixel-space DouglasтАУPeucker (the newly exported `vectorLayers.douglasPeucker`; degree-space tolerance is anisotropic on the ground); index flag every 5 ft; sparse labels capped ~30.
  - **The repo's first Web Worker** (`lib/terrainWorker.js`, Vite `?worker`): decode/smooth/trace off the main thread; import list pinned by `test/terrainWorker.test.js` (a Leaflet/DOM import would crash at worker RUNTIME, not build time); the raw grid transfers back for the B706 readout.
  - **Leaflet glue** (`lib/terrainLayers.js`): overpass-pattern view-driven layerGroup (moveend refresh, B56d busy/pending trailing edge, `gisCache.swr` last-good painting with data age) with the terrain specifics тАФ fetch on the MAIN thread (gisCache is localStorage-bound; proxyтЖТdirect one-shot fallback mirrors wireRaster), ONE deduped fetch+compute per tile shared with B705 and the readout, grids in a small LRU Map (a Float32Array must never ride `gisCache.write` тАФ it JSON.stringifies unconditionally), canvas-renderer polylines (`interactive:false`; hierarchy by WEIGHT per the salience rule), white-halo divIcon labels, restyle-in-place `setOpacity`, worker-crash lazy rebuild.
  - **Registry** (`lib/layers.js`): `TERRAIN.contours` ("Contour lines (1 ft)"), `kind: "contours"` dispatch, vintage row; both surfaces pick it up automatically. **Zoom-gated тЙе 16** (honesty: at z15 a capped grid is ~6 m cells тАФ 1-ft contours would be mush).
  - **Calibration:** the ramp test pins d3-contour's smoothed output to the cell-center convention (measured: level 20 of an x-ramp lands at exactly px 20.5), so contours, the hover readout, and the cross-section tool can never disagree by half a cell. Elevations are NAVD88 orthometric тАФ the same vertical datum FEMA BFEs use (stated in the layer note; relevant to the future FFE-vs-BFE feature).
- **Verified here (sandbox):** 60+ new unit tests across the `demGrid`/`contours`/`terrainWorker` suites (calibration, cone closed-ring, void break-not-bridge with halo assertion, masked-smooth void-bleed, fixture decode contract, artifact under the 512 KB cache cap) ┬╖ full suite green ┬╖ build green (worker chunk emits self-contained) ┬╖ headless: ONE LERC fetch, 30 halo labels painted, real canvas ink, vintage + caveat lines render.
> **Dedup (DEDUPE-FIRST тАФ grepped contour / DEM / topo / LERC across Open/тП│/Done):** B691 (Open) = the Fort Bend COUNTY contour GIS layer (different source, CORS/proxy plumbing тАФ untouched); B497/B500 (Done) = pond stage contours (detention geometry, not terrain); B58/B23 (Done) = the getSamples profile path whose conventions this reuses. Client-generated terrain contours are net-new.

### B705 тАФ Drainage flow-direction arrows (which way the site sheets) `[Site Planner / GIS]` (feature) #site-planner #gis  *(owner brief 2026-07-07, arrived as "NEW-3"; **B705** = B704 + 1. Branch `claude/elevation-houston-relief-7co7do`.)*

Screen-spaced lattice (~70 px); arrow length + weight scale with slope (bolder = steeper тАФ salience tracks importance); slope computed in ft/ft with the cos(lat) mercatorтЖТground correction (~0.868 at Houston тАФ mercator meters overstate ground distance ~15%). **Flat/ambiguous/void samples get NO arrow** тАФ never invent a direction (the no-auto-guess principle). Rides B704's tile end-to-end: NO second DEM fetch path (the same worker job computes both artifacts). Sign-convention unit tests pin east-falling тЖТ east arrows and south-falling тЖТ down-screen arrows (grid y-down vs latitude-up is the classic silent bug тАФ uphill arrows pass every other test).

### B699 тАФ Whole content pane is the drop target; drag-onto-folder files into it; ONE empty state; folder drops preserve your subfolder structure `[Library / storage]` (feature) #library #files #filing #drive  *(owner brief 2026-07-07, arrived as "NEW-3"; **B699** = B698 + 1. Branch `claude/library-tab-refactor-suqn3m`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED this session; parks in тП│ Verify (Verify: live тАФ drag-and-drop is the timing/race class, and filing into arbitrary Drive folders is live-Drive behavior) тЖТ V237.** Explorer model throughout.
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-07 from chat
- RENUMBERED on merge-in of `origin/main` 2026-07-07 тАФ concurrent sessions took B689тАУB696 (basemap/boundary-layers batch, husk root-cause, de-creams, CORS proxy) and V232тАУV235; this branch's B689тАУB694 / V232тАУV234 became **B697тАУB702 / V236тАУV238** (= highest across both files + 1). Code comments were bumped to match.
- **What shipped:**
  - The **whole pane is the drop target**, driven by a dragenter/dragleave **depth counter** (the old naive `currentTarget === target` dragleave flickered over children тАФ the exact gotcha the brief flagged).
  - **Drag onto a folder row** in the left rail highlights it (dashed accent) and drops file straight into that folder; the "All files" row is the drop-to-auto-sort target; the drop-overlay pill names the REAL target (hovered row > selected folder > auto-file).
  - The dedicated bottom **drop card is gone**, and so is the duplicate "No files here yetтАж" line тАФ ONE empty state ("Drop files anywhere. PDFs read their own title block and file themselves; anything uncertain lands in Needs filing." + Choose files / Choose a folder). Persistent pickers moved to the toolbar (Upload files / Upload a folder).
  - **Structure preservation (decision baked into the brief):** a dropped/picked FOLDER routes each file by the user's own SUBFOLDER layout тАФ a subfolder matching an existing tree folder files straight into it (prefix/case-insensitive, plural-tolerant; `matchDropPathToFolder` in `shared/folders/folderTree.js`, unit-tested); a subfolder matching nothing goes to **Needs filing** (the tree is never auto-extended). **The dropped CONTAINER's own name never routes anything** (a generic "Drawings"/"Documents" container must not mass-file by coincidence) тАФ its direct files keep the classic B664 title-block auto-file, so a plain folder of PDFs never dumps on Needs filing. **Never-guess guards:** an ambiguous label is accepted only when its parent segment pins exactly one candidate; a unique label reached through a CONTRADICTING known parent ("Design/Reports" where the only "Reports" folder lives under Testing Contractor) is rejected and the walk files into the nearest corroborated ancestor (Design) instead тАФ cross-branch guessing is structurally impossible. An explicit target (row drop / selected folder) still wins for the whole drop (B686/B687 semantics); a drop before the tree rows load falls back to classic auto-file (no empty-tree needs-filing dump); a drag cancelled outside the window resets the pane highlight (window dragend/drop/leave self-heal); rail navigation and the queue's Triage button clear an active search so a click never looks dead. The entry-API walk now stamps `relPath` (`uploadQueue.entryToFiles`); `webkitdirectory` picks already carry `webkitRelativePath`. All ingestion still rides the ONE B260-descended queue (`makeQueueItems`/`runPool`) тАФ no forked pipeline; the folder-note summary honestly reports kept / needs-filing / skipped counts.
- **Verified here (sandbox):** unit tests (path-matcher ambiguity + contradiction rules, relPath stamping) ┬╖ full suite green ┬╖ build green ┬╖ logged-out headless smoke.
- **ЁЯФН Adversarially reviewed (2026-07-07, 4 dimensions ├Ч verify): confirmed findings all fixed same-session** тАФ the cross-branch unique-label guess (HIGH тЖТ the contradiction guard above), the container-name mass-file (container excluded from routing), a LOWERCASED folder label stamped as the discipline corrupting doc-class/category (labels now case-preserved + normalized onto the canonical discipline list), row-hop highlight flicker (targets now arm on dragenter), a depth-counter desync pinning the overlay after an out-of-window release (window-dragleave self-heal), the folderRows-empty race, over-promising drop copy (the empty state + overlay pill now name the REAL target), and dead-feeling clicks with a search active (rail clicks / Triage clear the query; typing exits the holding view).
> **Dedup (DEDUPE-FIRST тАФ grepped `drop` / `drag` / `entry` / `empty state` across Open/тП│/Done):** extends **B664** (folder drops тАФ the flatten-and-file source side) and **B687** (selected-folder targeting) with row-targeted drops + structure preservation; neither covered them. Fine tiers (zтЙе12/13) are bbox-scoped @0.0002┬░ on a snap grid. TTLs: county 30 d, city/ETJ 14 d (annexations/SB2038 move these occasionally; SWR shows age either way). Per B96's own note, the **refreshed-age stamp folded into the B236 vintage line** тАФ one surface: `as of: <vintage> ┬╖ refreshed <age> (updatingтАж)`, stale in `--warn-text` (the standalone age chip is gone).
- **Never-blank fallback (the decideVectorOrImage intent, adapted):** boundaries are always-vector (no image service exists) тАФ `minVectorZoom:0`/`maxAreaDeg:тИЮ` so no gate can flip them; a **failed pull with nothing cached** engages the injected live fallback = the previous esri-leaflet `featureLayer` path **with its B287 retry/backoff**, LOUD through the same status channel (`liveFallback`, dependency-injected from `layers.js` so `vectorOverlay` stays esri-leaflet-free). A cold-cache fetch failure now THROWS in `fetchCached` instead of resolving a silent null (LOUD-FAILURE). Fixed: (1) `engageFallback` + the zoom-gate branch now bump the request `seq` тАФ an in-flight fetch can no longer paint stale vectors OVER the live fallback or BELOW the zoom gate; (2) a SUPERSEDED request's failure no longer latches `lastVectorError` (and a successful pull clears it) тАФ a mid-pan blip can't permanently downgrade the layer to the fallback; (3) the fallback layer gets the `setOpacity` shim esri-leaflet FeatureLayers lack (the opacity slider was dead after engagement) and reports "loading", not a false-healthy "loaded", right after the failure that engaged it; (4) the basemap status dot keys off `tileload` тАФ Leaflet fires layer-`load` even when EVERY tile errored, which showed green over a gray canvas; (5) a DFW-scale city cell measured **560 KB stored** (over the 512 KB cap тЖТ silent L1-only) тАФ the widest city tier now thins at 0.003┬░/3 dp with a mid tier at z11тАУ12; (6) cache keys stamp `precision` too (`@0.002p4`) so a registry retune busts the cache instead of serving old-detail geometry for a TTL; (7) the identify popover closes on toggle-off/fallback (it used to outlive the layer); (8) a FAILED background refresh clears `lastKey` so the next map move retries (was: "(updatingтАж)" forever with no retry); (9) cold pulls no longer paint twice (swr's cold-fetch `onFresh` is skipped via the `lastKey` guard); (10) select mode neutralizes the interactive fill's `cursor:pointer` (`.pf-select-mode` + `pf-boundary-hit`, index.css) so the +/тИТ parcel cursor survives тАФ B98 extends to the cursor. **Accepted as documented limitations:** gisCache's oldest-write-first eviction could recycle the standing statewide entry under a full 3 MB namespace (a later re-pull, not a failure тАФ changing B96's shared eviction policy would touch the identify/overpass consumers), and an over-cap entry staying L1-only is graceful degradation by design.
> **Dedup:** consumes B96's cache exactly as it anticipated; keeps B287's retry as the fallback leg; does NOT collide with B371 (analysis-side offline pre-cache, still Later) or B629 (parcels).

### B692 тАФ ROOT-CAUSE fix for the B690 husk-parcel crash: sanitize the model funnel so a null/points-less entry can never be manufactured, persisted, or re-ingested `[Site Planner / model]` (bug тАФ CRITICAL, owner-reported crash; extends B690) #site-planner #persistence  *(owner chat 2026-07-07 тАФ incognito tab on planyr.io: "Site Planyr hit an error and couldn't loadтАж Try again/Reload/Ctrl-Shift-R all send me right back." First minted **B689**; RENUMBERED to **B692** on merge-in of `origin/main` тАФ the concurrent Cowork live run independently hit the SAME crash as its V231 #18, minted **B690** for it and shipped the render-side guard (shoelace/polyArea, PR #540), and also took B689 (inspector de-cream) + B691 (Fort Bend CORS); **B692** = highest B# across both files (B691) + 1. Branch `claude/site-planner-incognito-error-49h3as`. DEDUPE-FIRST тАФ same crash as **B690** (both symbolicated to `ymтЖТHpтЖТIj`), so this item is deliberately the ROOT-CAUSE COMPANION, not a duplicate: B690 guarded the reads; B692 stops the husk from ever existing тАФ manufacture (normalizeZ), persistence (createSiteModel funnel), and every ingress (rows, realtime, JSON import) тАФ and makes sanitization LOUD.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + fully repro'd/verified headless this session; parks in тП│ Verify (Verify: live тАФ the repro cites the owner's real signed-in data; the signed-in mirror path + the telemetry signal need a live confirmation) тЖТ V232.**
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-07 from chat (crash 2026-07-07 02:23тАУ02:30 UTC, 23 telemetry reports, build dca4f15, all signed-in)
- **Root cause (found via the app's own `client_errors` telemetry тАФ minified stack symbolicated against the deployed chunk):** `MapFinder.siteAcres` reduces `shoelace(p.points)` over `site.parcels`, guarded on the ARRAY but not the ENTRY. A `null` entry in a persisted parcels array (JSON.stringify turns an `undefined` entry or an array hole into `null`) survived `createSiteModel` untouched, and B671's `normalizeZ` then spread it into a `{z:0}` "husk" with no points тАФ `undefined.length` тЖТ the workspace error boundary, on EVERY load, because the poison lives in the stored record. Cloud DB swept clean (site_elements + sites blobs, all users) тАФ the husk was client-manufactured into the local mirror during the element-sync churn window (RLS-rejected commit 01:30 + create collisions + a two-tab CAS heal loop 01:33тАУ02:03).
- **Fix (funnel + belt-and-suspenders):** (1) `createSiteModel` now DROPS non-object entries from every collection (parcels/els/markups/measures/callouts/sheetOverlays/parcelDrawings/crossSections) and drops points-less husk parcels тАФ reference-stable when clean, so no state/save churn; runs before `migrateRoads` so a null can't crash the els migration passes either. (2) `normalizeZ`/`needsZ` never spread a non-object into a `{z}` husk (drop instead). (3) `MapFinder.shoelace` returns 0 for a non-array (the list can never crash on residual junk). (4) The rows-read paths (`refetchReplace` + realtime `applyRemoteInstr`) keep husk parcel rows OFF the canvas; the reconcile diff then tombstones the bad row in the cloud тАФ the husk heals into a proper delete (TOMBSTONE-DELETES). (4b) The JSON-import path now normalizes through `createSiteModel` (was raw `setParcels(d.parcels)`) тАФ a hand-edited/stale export can't re-poison the canvas (found by the parallel writer-hunt audit; the audit also confirmed via DB sweep that NO other user has husk data and no one else was affected). (5) LOUD-FAILURE: `loadSitesList` reports a `model-sanitized` telemetry event whenever a stored record needed junk dropped тАФ corruption is a visible signal, never a quiet edit. Bonus: the e2e fixture generator's parcel used `ring:` instead of `points:` (a real husk shipping in the fixture) тАФ fixed + fixtures/goldens regenerated.
- **Self-heal:** no user action тАФ the poisoned record reads clean on the next load (drop-at-read), and the next save persists the cleaned model.
- **Tests/verify (sandbox):** 2,875 green (11 new in `test/modelSanitize.test.js`: husk manufacture, per-collection drops, reference stability, idempotence, junk counting) ┬╖ build green ┬╖ **controlled repro BOTH ways headless (`ui-audit/verify-husk-parcel.mjs`): the poisoned seed CRASHES live planyr.io with the owner's exact error, and renders clean (site listed, correct 23.0 ac from the surviving parcel) on the fixed build.**

- **Fix (folder-id targeting through the whole stack):** the server `treeParentForUpload` now accepts an explicit `folderId` (a `project_folders` row id) that resolves straight to that row's mirrored Drive folder, winning over the discipline route (`x-planyr-folder-id` header, honored by `functions/api/files.js` + `тАж/resumable.js`). `reviewStore` threads `folderId` through `fileNewReview`/`storeSource`/`pushFileToDrive`/`uploadLargeToDrive` and persists it on the review (`data.folderId`, surfaced by `listReviews`, no DB migration). `FileBrowser` files a drop into the selected folder (skip auto-file, `needsFiling:false`), `placedFolder` honours `f.folderId` over the discipline placement, and the drop-strip copy + drop-anywhere overlay now say exactly where a drop lands ("Filing into 02. Electric" vs. "drop drawings on All files to auto-sort by title block").
- **Also folded in (B685 adversarial-review polish):** re-file no longer clobbers the source filename (fixed in the B685 PR); a non-PDF whose best-effort facts write missed is still classed correctly (the source filename is now AUTHORITATIVE on the review via `listReviews` `sfile`, not just the file-facts index); opening a non-PDF in Review **downloads** it instead of a dead-end note (and non-PDFs are barred from becoming the resume target, so no surprise download on load); the display-label extension strip only removes a real letter-first extension, so "Rev.3" keeps its name.
- **Tests:** `treeParentForUpload` explicit-folder cases (folderMirror.test.js), `stripFileExt` (docPersistence.test.js). Full suite green (2,836), build green, lint clean, logged-out headless smoke renders root/Library/Review with no JS errors.

- **3D massing (enhancement):** "Export with 3D buildings" extrudes each building to its clear height (`<extrude>1</extrude>` + `relativeToGround` + per-vertex altitude in metres); flat `clampToGround` is the default and the fallback when height is unknown.
- **LOUD-FAILURE:** `siteToFeatures` THROWS if any vertex reprojects to a non-finite number тЖТ the caller (`flashWarn` on the canvas, `setErr` on the map) aborts loudly, never a partial/misregistered file. Empty site тЖТ "nothing to export" (no empty file); a plan with no geo anchor тЖТ blocked with a plain-English hint. Names XML-escaped; download filename sanitized. Local download only (default-private; no sharing surface).
- **Two entry points:** map viewer right-click on empty map тЖТ exports every visible site (honoring the status-chip filter), each as its own folder, + any selected parcels; canvas right-click on empty space тЖТ exports the open plan.

(`gis-verify/kmz-gps-verify.mjs`, 13/13.) Full suite green ┬╖ lint 0 errors ┬╖ build green.

### B682 тАФ Dragging a parcel's acreage label spawns a "bunch of copies" (id-less parcels + value-based union merge) `[Site Planner]` (bug) #site-planner #persistence #selection  *(owner chat 2026-07-06 тАФ screenshot: "I just tried to move the 69.48 ac label, and it just made a bunch of copies." **B682** = highest real B# across both files (B681) + 1. Branch `claude/acre-label-duplication-ulvjys`. DEDUPE-FIRST тАФ grepped Open/тП│ Verify/Done for `acre`/`label`/`parcel` ├Ч `dup`/`copies`: NOT B651 (split double-COUNTS acreage in the yield math тАФ different defect, same area), NOT B22 (rapid-click duplicate SELECTION on the map). Net-new: the parcel-identity/merge defect.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + sandbox-verified + headless-verified this session; parks in тП│ Verify (Verify: live тАФ the accumulation is a concurrency/multi-writer MERGE class per LIVE-VERIFY, only fully exercised signed-in over cloud sync) тЖТ V225.**
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-06 from chat
- **AUDIT-FIRST root cause:** map-finder / legacy parcels can be **id-LESS**. `MapFinder.computeAssembly` emits `{points, addr, acct, attrs}` with **no `id`** (the modern `newSiteFromMap` backfills one, but records created before that тАФ or synced from an older client тАФ still hold id-less parcels). Two bugs flow from a missing id: (1) the acreage-chip drag matches `pc.id === draggedId`, and with both `undefined` it moves EVERY id-less parcel at once; (2) the cross-copy union merge (`mergeSiteContent` тЖТ `unionById`) can only dedupe id-less items by **`JSON.stringify` value**, so the instant a drag adds a `labelOffset` the edited copy no longer equals its stored twin and the union keeps **BOTH** тАФ a phantom parcel that **multiplies** with each further drag/merge. Proven with a focused `mergeSiteContent` repro (1 id-less parcel + a labelOffset edit тЖТ **2** parcels).
- **Fix (one funnel, additive):** `createSiteModel` тАФ which every load/save/merge passes through тАФ now backfills a **deterministic id derived from the parcel GEOMETRY only** (`withStableParcelIds`, djb2-xor over rounded points), so the same parcel hashes identically before/after any mutable-field edit (labelOffset/active/locked/setbacks) and the union dedupes it by id; two genuinely-distinct parcels differ in points тЖТ distinct ids. Only fills a MISSING id (in-planner parcels keep their `uid()`), idempotent + reference-stable on already-migrated data. Exact-geometry id-less duplicates collapse to one, which **self-heals the phantom copies the bug already persisted** on the next load. No change needed in `SitePlanner.jsx` тАФ parcels reaching React state now always carry an id, so the chip drag matches exactly one.
- **Verified here (sandbox):** 6 new unit tests in `test/siteModel.test.js` (backfill determinism ┬╖ geometry-only stability across a labelOffset edit ┬╖ distinct-geometry distinct ids ┬╖ existing id never rewritten ┬╖ the merge repro now yields 1 not 2 ┬╖ exact-dup self-heal) ┬╖ full suite **2,788 green** ┬╖ lint 0 errors ┬╖ build green.
- **Verified here (headless, logged-out):** seeded a site with 3 id-less parcels (2 exact-geometry dupes, one carrying a dragged `labelOffset`, + 1 distinct), opened it in the real plan canvas тЖТ exactly **2** acre chips render (dupe collapsed, distinct survived), zero page errors. (Temp spec, removed after the run тАФ the unit tests are the durable guard.)
- **тП│ V225** = the signed-in / cloud pass: on a real account whose project has (or is seeded with) id-less parcels, drag an acreage label repeatedly across cloud syncs / a second tab and confirm it stays put with NO new copies, and that any pre-existing phantom copies collapse on load.

### B667 тАФ Review remembers the last document PER PROJECT (+ the resume self-clobber fix) `[Doc Review]` (feature + bug тАФ owner request) #doc-review #persistence  *(owner chat 2026-07-05 тАФ "whatever I last reviewed, what the last document that I reviewed in that project should stay open too"; **B667** = B666 + 1. Branch `claude/module-nav-project-persistence-ryftwj`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED this session; parks in тП│ Verify (Verify: live тАФ resume needs signed-in cloud loads; timing class) тЖТ V217.**
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-05 from chat
- **AUDIT-FIRST find тАФ resume was self-clobbering (the real reason Review "started from nothing"):** the mount-time pointer writes (`lastSingleId` = this session's fresh blank id, `lastMode`="review") ran in declaration order BEFORE the boot effect read the keys back, so resume loaded a never-saved review and silently fell to the empty state on every reload. Same pattern in `Stitcher.jsx` (`lastStitchId`). Fixed structurally: the stored pointers are captured at FIRST RENDER (before any effect can write) and all pointer writes stay silent until boot resolves тАФ no clobber window at all.
- **Per-project memory:** new map `planyr:docreview:lastDoc:v1` = `{ [projectId|""]: {id, mode} }` (`lib/lastDoc.js` тАФ pure, 14 unit tests). Legacy globals keep being written and remain the fallback (migration = fallback, not a copy pass тАФ existing devices resume day one). Boot resolves ordered candidates via `resolveResume` (URL project тЖТ that project's own entry first, then legacy, still guarded by `wrongProject` on the actually-loaded record тАФ a project-matched entry now RESUMES where the guard used to drop to empty). Breadcrumb project switch inside Review lands on THAT project's last doc (flushes the outgoing doc first; a pending cross-workspace open intent or an in-flight open wins тАФ no race).
- **DEDUPE-FIRST:** no prior per-project-resume item (grepped `lastSingleId` ┬╖ `resume` ┬╖ `wrongProject`); B478 (resume-into-planner) is the Site-side analogue, different surface.
- **Verified here (sandbox):** `test/lastDoc.test.js` 14 green ┬╖ full suite green ┬╖ build green.
- **тП│ V217** = signed-in: open doc X in project A and doc Y in project B тЖТ breadcrumb AтЖФB resumes each project's own doc; reload a deep link `#/project/A/markup` reopens X; reload with an empty hash reopens the exact doc last on screen (also covers the B666 module+project restore chain end-to-end).

### B651 тАФ Parcel split double-counts acreage; make split REPLACE the parent (parent + children can never both be active) `[Site Planner]` (bug) #site-planner #yield #selection  *(owner brief 2026-07-04, arrived as "NEW-1"; **B651** = highest real B# across both files (B650) + 1. Branch `claude/parcel-split-double-count-vk8f0j`. DEDUPE-FIRST тАФ net-new: NOT B416 (Split-a-parcel discoverability / panel reachability, Done), NOT B128 (concave-cut split GEOMETRY, Done). Same feature area, different defect: those made the split tool reachable and its cut correct; this fixes what the split does to the parcel MODEL / active set.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + headless-verified this session; parks in тП│ Verify (Verify: live тАФ repro cites real project data) тЖТ V210.** A split parcel and its children occupy the SAME ground, so any active set containing a parent AND a child double-counts that acreage (owner repro: Parcel 3, 16.40 ac тЖТ 2.52 + 13.87 ac children, all three active тЖТ Yield sums тЙИ 31.8 ac).
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-04 from chat
- **AUDIT-FIRST reconciliation (code reality vs. the report):** the current `performSplit` (`SitePlanner.jsx`, since PR #444 / #468) already **replaced + tombstoned** the parent, so the exact "split tool leaves all three active" no longer reproduces via the cut tool on `main`. The owner's live тЙИ31.8 ac most plausibly came from **overlapping county parcels added separately** (a recently-subdivided tract where CAD still lists the parent + both children) or a **stale cached bundle** predating that fix тАФ which is exactly why **B652 (the overlap warning) is the real catch-all** and was built alongside. This item still had a genuine gap vs. the owner's desired UX (the old code DELETED the parent instead of retaining it), so the split was re-architected from "delete parent" to "supersede parent."
- **What shipped (branch `claude/parcel-split-double-count-vk8f0j`; lint 0 ┬╖ 2,526 tests (+21) ┬╖ build green ┬╖ lazy split intact ┬╖ headless `ui-audit/verify-b651-b652-parcel-split.mjs` 14/14):**
  - **Split is now a REPLACEMENT via supersession** (`performSplit`): one op creates + activates the pieces as CHILDREN (each carries `parentId`) and marks the parent `active:false` (superseded, non-counting) тАФ no longer deleted/tombstoned. Because the superseded parent is inactive, it drops out of every active-parcel area sum automatically (no yield-math change needed; the ~13 inline `active !== false` sums are untouched).
  - **Parent retained + nested** (`parcelOutline` in `siteModel.js`; Parcel panel): the superseded parent stays in the list, greyed + "┬╖ split", with its children indented under it. The **on-canvas** superseded outline is hidden (its active children occupy the same ground). Header "Parcels ┬╖ N" counts CURRENT lots only (excludes superseded), so splitting one lot reads "Parcels ┬╖ 2".
  - **Lineage naming** (`parcelDisplayInfo`, derived тАФ not stored): Parcel 3 тЖТ 3A / 3B тЖТ 3A1 / 3A2 (letters odd depth, digits even), tracking the parent's current number; a street address still wins as the name.
  - **Mutual-exclusion guard** (`toggleParcelActive` + `lineageConflicts`): activating a parcel auto-deactivates its ancestors AND descendants (a parent covers its children's ground; siblings are disjoint), so a parent and its split children can never both be active.
  - **Schema:** `SITE_MODEL_VERSION` 10 тЖТ 11 (additive `parentId`; existing records migrate losslessly тАФ missing = root, unchanged behavior). Fixtures/MAP regenerated.
- **тП│ V210 (live, signed-in + real project data):** on planyr.io, load a real project, split a real county parcel (e.g. Parcel 3, 16.40 ac); confirm Yield reads ~16.4 ac (not ~31.8), the parent shows greyed "┬╖ split" with 3A/3B nested, toggling the parent active deactivates the children, and the whole thing round-trips through cloud save/reload without resurrecting the parent as active. ### B644 тАФ Scheduler embed: first COLD boot throws `Cannot read properties of null (reading 'projects')` + the loader overlay exceeds the 6s backstop (self-recovers) (├Ч2) `[Scheduler / robustness]` (bug тАФ first-paint hardening) #scheduler  *(Cowork live verification 2026-07-03, from V153; minted **B644** = highest real B# across both files (B643) + 1)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + headless-verified 2026-07-05; parks in тП│ Verify (Verify: live тАФ timing/race class) тЖТ V211.** Original report: the FIRST cold SiteтЖТSchedule switch on planyr.io threw a one-time `тЪая╕П This view failed to load тАФ Cannot read properties of null (reading 'projects')` (~10.5s overlay, self-recovered on re-nav).
- Verify: live
- Recurrence: 2026-07-05 тАФ owner repro (chat "NEW-5", DEDUPE-FIRST fold тАФ same error string, same first-paint null-`projects` read): create a project via **Start blank тЖТ Schedule tab** тЖТ the same error renders **behind the connect-a-schedule modal**. Deterministic (not only the cold race); expected a clean empty state only.
- **Root cause (pinned by a live sandbox repro, not a guess):** NOT the render path тАФ the `if (!data) return <loader/>` gate was already sound. The **shellтЖТiframe nav bridge** (`planar:nav-select` / `nav-select-by-site` / `nav-link` / `nav-create-linked` / `nav-dashboard` / `nav-new` / rename / delete in `public/sequence/index.html`) queues `setData(d => тАж)` functional updaters when the shell announces the active project on a tab switch; before the async `hs-v1` load resolves `d` is **null**, and React runs the queued updater INSIDE the next `useState` mount тАФ `Object.values(d.projects || {})` throws and lands App in the error boundary. Cold boot = the race version (the bridge message beats the slow cloud load); fresh project = the deterministic version (no schedule linked, load still pending). Captured stack: updater тЖТ `Object.useState` тЖТ `App`. The prior "sandbox can't boot the embed" blocker is stale тАФ the repro serves the embed's CDN deps from local copies via request interception (see the harness).
- **Fix shipped (minimal, matches the in-file `planar:view-set` precedent):** one early gate in the nav-bridge handler тАФ drop `planar-shell` messages until `latestData.current` exists (the shell re-posts nav intents on every tab switch and retries `nav-request`, so an early drop self-heals the moment the load lands тАФ the already-documented pre-load no-op behavior, now applied to every branch) тАФ plus null guards in the three bridge-called helpers (`addProject` / `renameProject` / `deleteProject`) so a future caller can't regress the class.
- **Sandbox-verified 2026-07-05:** `ui-audit/verify-b644-fresh-null.mjs` (new, self-contained тАФ fetches the four CDN deps once via curl, serves them by request interception): pre-fix it reproduces the exact owner error + stack; post-fix it PASSES (embed renders, zero null-`projects` errors). `jsxcheck-sequence` OK ┬╖ build green.
