### B672 (├Ч2) тАФ Element-level sync, phase 3/5: realtime read path + rejoin refetch (read cutover; blob frozen) `[Site Planner]` (feature) #site-planner #persistence  *(owner brief 2026-07-06, arrived as "NEW-3"; minted **B672** тАФ see B671's renumber note. Branch `claude/site-elements-schema-sync-4p2x5b`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED this session; parks in тП│ Verify (Verify: live тАФ cross-tab propagation is a multi-session timing class) тЖТ V229.** Each open site now subscribes to its `site_elements` rows and applies changes LIVE; with the edit lock still on, a read-only tab updates in real time. This is also the READ CUTOVER: signed-in loads come from rows + a slim header, and the whole-doc blob is FROZEN (`sites.data_backup` = the ~30-day rollback copy).
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-06 from chat
- **Recurrence (2026-07-07, from the Cowork V229 live run тАФ re-opened, FIXED same session, back to тП│ Verify):**
  **V229 #5 FAILED with a reproduced LOST UPDATE (data-loss class).** Repro: session B's realtime socket
  dropped (`pfSupabase.realtime.disconnect()`), A edits an element (rev 9тЖТ10), B rejoins тЖТ the DB ends up
  clobbered back to B's stale geometry at rev 11; reproduced twice. **Root cause тАФ the refetch-replace
  stale-reconcile race:** after `eng.seed(freshRows)` the old `refetchReplace` reconciled against
  `stateRef.current`, which still holds the PRE-replace canvas (setState hadn't rendered) тАФ on a
  socket-dropped tab that canvas is genuinely stale, so the diff committed OLD geometry as valid
  rev-guarded updates on top of the fresh revs. (#4 passed because a hidden tab still receives events;
  only a dropped socket leaves the canvas stale.) Compounding hole: `flush()` clears the dirty map
  up-front, so the batch IN FLIGHT was invisible to both `applyRemoteRow` and the refetch substitution.
  **Fix (this session):** `refetchReplace` now reconciles against EXACTLY the substituted collections it
  just placed (rows тИк pending local edits), never `stateRef`; it defers wholesale while `busyRef` is live;
  the engine tracks `inflightKeys` during a flush тАФ in-flight commits are protected like dirty everywhere
  (`applyRemoteRow` keeps local + adopts rev; `dirtyEntries()` includes them so the refetch substitution
  keeps a mid-commit edit; `reconcile` skips re-enqueueing data already on the wire; shadow revs stay
  monotonic when an ok result lands after a newer remote rev was adopted; an identical incoming row is
  adopted silently and drops a duplicate queued write). 6 new unit tests pin the exact #5 sequence +
  in-flight invariants (`test/elementSync.test.js`, "refetch-replace safety"). **Re-run V229 #5 live with
  true DevTools offline** (the Cowork run's disconnect() only severed realtime, not the RPC path тАФ DevTools
  offline exercises the queued-commit + rejoin path end-to-end).
  - *Watch note (Observation B, same run):* two transient paint freezes were seen under automation-driven
    load; nothing reproduced organically. No action тАФ watch during the V229 re-run; escalate to its own B#
    only if it shows up under human use.
  - *Related churn fixed same session (Observation A):* the autosave pushed a content-identical slim header
    on every element edit тАФ each push bumped `sites.version` and CAS-ping-ponged every other tab (a heal per
    edit; noise, and it masked #5's mechanism). `cloudUpsert` now skips a push whose header content is
    unchanged (`headerSig` тАФ the slim header minus `updatedAt`; baseline seeded from `cloudList`, advanced on
    every successful push, cleared on delete/user-switch; the unload keepalive shares the skip). Trade-off,
    accepted: `sites.updated_at` advances only on REAL header changes (meta/settings/overlays) тАФ element
    recency lives on the `site_elements` rows. +3 headerSig tests in `test/headerSlim.test.js`.
- **Realtime read path:** one channel per open site (`postgres_changes` filtered to `site_id`); the apply is idempotent per row (`applyRemoteRow`: incoming.rev must BEAT the shadow rev, so our own committed echoes are no-ops); a tombstoned row removes the element; a row for a locally-dirty element keeps LOCAL data and adopts the remote rev (its commit re-targets the fresh row). Remote applies buffer mid-gesture (never yank the canvas mid-drag). **Full refetch + REPLACE on every join/rejoin + tab wake** (visibilitychange) тАФ never trust event gaps; dirty entries substitute back in; value-identical replaces keep state references (an idle wake re-trues nothing, saves nothing). A failed refetch changes nothing and retries (B54 discipline). No-realtime fallback: a plain fetch still seeds + replaces once, so writes work even if WebSockets are blocked.
- **Header slimming (same commit):** `slimForCloud` strips the 5 vector collections + marks `elementsInRows: true`; `mergePulledSites` understands slim rows (local elements kept тАФ empty тЙа deleted; header-only re-push signature тАФ no perma-push; a slim row's stale `deletedIds` are excluded from the union so they can never drop a row-restored element).
- **Kill list executed:** the B459 thin-clobber guard + `siteContent`/`siteTombs` baselines + `noteLocalContent` (a slim header would always read as "thinned"; element safety now lives in per-row rev guards); doc-level `cloudConflict` state + the blocking "changed in another session тАж Take over editing" banner (a stale header CAS now SELF-HEALS inside `cloudUpsert` тАФ refetch the version, re-push once; the B455/B460/B558/B596 false-conflict class is retired BY ARCHITECTURE); the cloud-active storage-event union fold (signed-out keeps it). `deletedIds` refinement: element ids are reconciled against live rows on every refetch (an id with a live row is purged тАФ rows are deletion-canonical), and it keeps serving header-side collections + signed-out mode.
- **DB executed via Supabase MCP:** backfill re-run captured the phase-1тЖТ3 gap (els 496тЖТ523 тАФ real owner edits); found + fixed a guard edge (the boot re-push can rewrite blob CONTENT, e.g. the v12 `z` normalization, without advancing `updatedAt` тЖТ the update guard is now `<=`, engine rows stay strictly newer and untouched); fidelity after heal: **27/28 sites byte-identical, 1 site's rows strictly AHEAD of its blob** (rev 19, server-stamped 400ms after the last blob snapshot тАФ the healthy dual-write case, rows-canonical). `data_backup` frozen for all 28 sites (`db/site_elements_freeze.sql`).
- **e2e seeds** now explode fixture sites into rows (seed.sql + seed-fixtures.sql), so seeded fixtures open under the rows-canonical read path.
- **Verified here (sandbox):** lint 0 ┬╖ 2,835 tests (+19: `elementApply` matrix incl. the composite-key twin case, `headerSlim` merge/no-perma-push/stale-tombstone cases; `cloudThinGuard.test.js` retired with its guard) ┬╖ build green ┬╖ headless smoke 3/3 (signed-out planner unaffected тАФ engine + channel are cloud-active-only).
- **тП│ V229 (live, two signed-in sessions):** see VERIFICATION.md тАФ cross-tab <2s propagation, rejoin refetch, tab-wake re-true, and the no-conflict-banner regression. Folded into the consolidated Cowork runbook (docs/COWORK-ELEMENT-SYNC-LIVE.md, lands with B674).
- DEDUPE-FIRST: net-new (see B670); B127/B90 (Done) were the localStorage-era cross-tab folds this replaces for signed-in use.

### B673 тАФ Element-level sync, phase 4/5: loud-conflict surface + delete/edit matrix `[Site Planner]` (feature) #site-planner #ui #persistence  *(owner brief 2026-07-06, arrived as "NEW-4"; minted **B673** тАФ see B671's renumber note. Branch `claude/site-elements-schema-sync-4p2x5b`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED this session; parks in тП│ Verify (Verify: live тАФ conflict paths are two-session timing) тЖТ V230.** No overwrite is ever silent: both sides of a per-element collision get a toast naming who changed what, with **Show** (zoom-to-element + select) or **Restore** riding along. Whole-element granularity, last-write-wins, no field merging тАФ non-blocking BY DESIGN because nothing is lost.
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-06 from chat
- **The matrix (pure, unit-tested тАФ `lib/conflictToasts.js`):** edit-vs-edit тЖТ the losing tab re-commits (LWW) and reads "тЯиelementтЯй was also just edited by тЯиnameтЯй тАФ your version was kept"; the overwritten tab (a foreign rev inside the ~15s authored window) reads "тЯиnameтЯй changed тЯиelementтЯй you just edited тАФ their version is showing" (over-trigger inside the window is by design). Editing a deleted element тЖТ tombstone hit тЖТ the deletion shows on canvas + "тЯиelementтЯй was deleted by тЯиnameтЯй" with **Restore** (a new `restore` op: clears the tombstone, writes your data, new rev; racing a live row adopts THEIRS + a follow-up notice). Deleting a just-edited element тЖТ the delete re-applies at the fresh rev (delete wins, silent for the deleter); the editor's side gets the removal + supersede notice. Create-vs-create тЖТ impossible by construction (per-tab salted ids, B591) тАФ telemetry assert only. Remote changes OUTSIDE the window stay quiet (that's just live sync).
- **Attribution (`lib/editorNames.js`):** self-uid тЖТ "you (another window)"; teammates via the SECURITY DEFINER `list_team_members` roster RPC (profiles RLS is own-row-only), cached per site session; roster miss тЖТ "a teammate", never blank. Element labels via `describeElement` тАФ buildings by their on-canvas display number ("Building 3"), others by type/kind.
- **Toast component (`src/shared/ui/Toast.jsx`, reusable):** non-blocking stack, auto-dismiss 8s with HOVER-HOLD (mouse over pauses the timer), optional action button, cap 4 + "+n more", `role="status"`, theme tokens only, solid fill + weight (never faded text; amber accent bar тАФ red stays reserved for genuine alert). MODULE-SCOPE components.
- **zoom-to-element:** new `zoomToElement(kind, id)` frames the element's bbox (the frameToActiveParcels math over `featBBox`) + selects it тАФ no per-element zoom existed before.
- **Verified here (sandbox):** lint 0 ┬╖ 2,852 tests (+17: the full matrix mapping both sides + quiet passes, restore op ok/conflict flows, name resolver cache/self/fallback, describeElement, toast pure helpers) ┬╖ build green ┬╖ headless smoke 3/3 (signed-out untouched).
- **тП│ V230 (live, two signed-in sessions):** same-element race both-sides toasts with correct names, restore end-to-end, delete-vs-edit supersede notice. Until B674 removes the lock, same-browser tabs can't race (read-only gate) тАФ the matrix is reachable cross-DEVICE now and fully same-browser after B674; folded into the consolidated Cowork runbook (docs/COWORK-ELEMENT-SYNC-LIVE.md, lands with B674).
- **2026-07-07 Cowork run: NOT faithfully exercised** тАФ both sessions were the same account, so the named-toast halves ("тЯиnameтЯй changedтАж") and the team-roster attribution never fired ("you (another window)" is the only reachable label same-account). Still тП│ pending a run with a SECOND account on a team-shared site (the one owner-side input тАФ see OWNER-TODO).

The pure `presenceSummary` renders the pill only when someone else is here: "N here", names on hover ("You" first, "You (2 windows)" nuance), through AppHeader's existing `saveSlot` (zero header API change).

### B714 тАФ Sharing a project silently REVERTS: any ordinary save from the owner's open tab overwrote `sites.team_id` back to null, locking the collaborator out `[Site Planner / Review / teams ┬╖ RLS]` (bug тАФ data-integrity class) #site-planner #persistence #auth  *(owner live repro 2026-07-08 with the Cowork session: right-clicked Goose Creek тЖТ Share to michael.butler@hillwood.com тЖТ the site APPEARED on the test account, then broke тАФ red cloud, elements gone after reload, no conflict toasts. Cowork's DB forensics found team "HIP Houston" + both members present but 0 sites linked, and filed it as "Share never sets team_id" (their NEW-1). First minted **B692**, then **B714** тАФ BOTH taken by concurrent sessions on successive merge-ins of `origin/main` (B692 = the husk-parcel root-cause fix; B714 = dock-high truck-court pricing); settled as **B714** = highest B# across both files (B714) + 1.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + unit-verified this session; parks in тП│ Verify (Verify: live тАФ the share round-trip is two-account/auth-only) тЖТ V244.** Sharing now survives every save: the sharing pointer can only be changed by the explicit Share/unshare action, never by a content autosave.
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-08 from the owner's live session (Cowork brief NEW-1 + NEW-2)
- **AUDIT-FIRST тАФ the reported diagnosis was half right; the code reality is worse and explains everything.** `lib/sharing.js` DOES set `sites.team_id` correctly (UPDATE by `group_id`; the row's `group_id` is populated; the owner passes the rehome-guard trigger) тАФ that's why the site initially appeared on the test account. The real bug: **every ordinary content push re-stamped `team_id` from the client's IN-MEMORY model** (`cloudUpsertCore` + `keepaliveCloudPush` for `sites`; `upsertReviewCore` + `keepaliveFlushReview` for `doc_reviews`; `upsertFileFacts` for `file_facts`, whose filing callers never even carry a teamId тЖТ hard `null`). The owner's open Goose Creek tab predated the share, so its next autosave wrote `team_id: null` тАФ silently unsharing (the B486 rehome guard deliberately exempts the OWNER, so it never fired; a signed-in tab never re-reads the store, so it never learned the share happened). Timeline confirmed live: team created 2026-06-24, both members admins; the site row rewritten to v61 the same night with `team_id` back at null.
- **Fix тАФ team_id is write-isolated to the sharing flow, everywhere:** `siteRowFor` / `reviewRowFor` (new pure row builders) OMIT `team_id` on every update тАФ CAS autosaves and unload keepalives physically cannot carry the sharing pointer anymore; a brand-NEW row (first insert) still stamps the model's teamId so a plan/review created inside a shared project is born shared. `upsertFileFacts` sends `team_id` only when a caller explicitly provides one (the plain-upsert update leg then leaves the column untouched). `slimForCloud` additionally strips `teamId`/`ownerId` from the stored jsonb тАФ the columns are the single source of truth, overlaid onto models at read time (`cloudList`/`loadReview`), and this keeps `headerSig` share-neutral so the B672 unchanged-header skip still works on shared sites.
- **Cowork's NEW-2 (realtime RLS "leak") тАФ resolved by the same root cause, no leak.** The test account saw the owner's building move BEFORE its lockout because at that moment the site WAS legitimately shared (team_id set, RLS satisfied); the subsequent autosave-revert then produced the red cloud (writes rejected) and empty reload (reads rejected). Supabase `postgres_changes` enforces RLS per-subscriber, and the un-share also kills the subscription's row visibility. The V244 run includes a sanity check on a genuinely-unshared site.
- **Follow-on (small, filed not lost):** a file FILED into an already-shared project lands with `team_id null` (fact-row callers don't know the project's team) until the next re-share stamps it тАФ pre-existing behavior, now explicit. Fix later by resolving the project's live team at filing time.
- **Verified here (sandbox):** 8-test `test/teamShareGuard.test.js` pins the rule for every writer (update rows carry NO team_id key; insert rows inherit; slim jsonb stripped; headerSig share-neutral) ┬╖ full suite green ┬╖ build green.
- **Data heal (prod):** the owner's intended share re-applied after deploy тАФ `sites.team_id = 454aa114тАж(HIP Houston)` restored on group `smqfy48tlk9j` (Goose Creek) via MCP SQL (rehome-guard trigger safely bypassed for the one maintenance UPDATE; re-verified after).
- **тП│ V244 (live, two accounts тАФ both already exist):** see VERIFICATION.md.
- DEDUPE-FIRST: net-new (no prior B# covers the share flow or team_id write-isolation); DISTINCT from the concurrent **B692** (husk-parcel model sanitize тАФ the other half of the same live run's findings); B486 (Done) is the non-owner rehome guard this bug walked around by BEING the owner. The same owner brief's NEW-3 = **B690**/**B692** (render guard + root cause, both shipped) and NEW-4 = **B672 (├Ч2)** (fixed + merged 2026-07-08) тАФ the live session ran on build 40884e6, which predates those fixes; no new numbers minted for them.

### B623 тАФ User-editable schedule conventions (working week, holidays, month/year roll behavior) `[Scheduler]` (feature)  *(owner-dropped 2026-07-02 as "NEW-3", filed to Later/Roadmap by owner instruction тАФ do NOT build until moved up; provisionally NEW-3/"B617", renumbered **B623** on the `origin/main` merge-in that took B615тАУB620; B623 = highest real B# across both files (B622) + 1)*

Reasonable extension since holiday selection already exists (`ensureHolidays` / `HOLIDAY_SET` in `public/sequence/index.html`). **Same loud/visible discipline as the rest of the schedule:** the working week and roll direction silently change every derived date, so any change must **re-run cascade and SURFACE the shifted dates** (before/after diff, same discipline as B621's migration), never move them quietly. Depends on the B621 duration model (week-factor is currently the hard-coded `DUR_WD_FACTOR.w = 5` + the weekend test inside `addBD`/`workdaysBetween`/`rollForwardToWorkday` тАФ those become the parameterized seam) and the B622 conflict-surfacing pattern (reuse the banner/row-flag). **Do NOT parameterize the week inside B621** тАФ that was deliberately deferred here.

### B371 тАФ GIS screening cache Phase 2: regional Houston-metro snapshot / offline pre-cache `[Site Planner / Analysis]` (feature) тАФ Phase 2 of B367  *(filed 2026-06-22; minted **B371**)*

Phase 2 is the owner's "cache most of Houston" idea: a **regional pre-cache/snapshot** of the Houston-metro source layers (+ a coverage mask), refreshed on a schedule, so a **never-seen** parcel with no features resolves **offline** to "No <layer> mapped (source vintage <date>)" instead of waiting on (or failing) a live query. Deferred deliberately behind Phase 1 per the brief; pick up once Phase 1 proves out in the field.

### B340 тАФ Auto-assembly CV tails behind the B335тАУB339 seams `[Doc Review / Stitch]` (feature) тАФ the hard minority  *(filed 2026-06-21 as the deferred remainder of the B335тАУB339 batch; minted **B340** тАФ a hot `main` took B325тАУB334)*
`[ ]` The B335тАУB339 headline flow (drop a set тЖТ auto-group тЖТ auto-stitch тЖТ crop тЖТ auto-calibrate) is **shipped + verified** for the common case тАФ CAD vector PDFs with a real text layer. (Scanned-sheet **OCR** was the 4th tail and is now **DONE тЖТ B352**, shipped + verified this session.) Three computer-vision tails remain, deferred behind clean injectable seams because each needs vector-graphics analysis we can't yet headless-verify тАФ and the manual-Align safety net already covers them:
  1. **Graphic scale-bar reading (B339 tail)** тАФ when there's no stated scale text, measure the drawn scale bar to set `ftPerUnit`. Needs vector-graphics/CV analysis, not text.
  2. **Geometric edge-line match (B337 middle fallback)** тАФ when match-line *labels* are missing, match the cut geometry across two sheets' edges. Today, label-less sheets correctly drop to the 2-point manual Align **pre-seeded** with detected seam endpoints (the spec's final safety net, already wired) тАФ this is the CV step between labels and manual.
  3. **Legend symbol-union (B338 tail)** тАФ extract each sheet's graphical legend entries and union them into the pinned Composite key (today the key lists the grouped plan + auto-scale; the crop + pinned panel ship). Needs symbol/vector extraction.
> Each is gated behind a seam exactly like the app's other not-yet-provisioned heavy compute (the AI title-block reader, the APS converter). Pick up when there's a way to verify (a CV pass we can headless-check). Coupled to the тШЕ north-star "map тЖТ drawings тЖТ latest set."
>
> **AMENDMENT 2026-07-03 (owner pulled the CV tails into active scope, Cowork brief) тАФ the PURE ENGINES for all three now ship + are unit-tested; the browser EXTRACTION + live verification remain.** These reduce manual-Align on *real* plan sets; they do **NOT** fix the JACINTOPORT schedule-set wall (that was B630тАУB633). What landed this session:
> 1. **Graphic scale-bar reading** тАФ `src/shared/files/scaleBarRead.js` (`readScaleBar` + `clusterBars`/`ticksNearBar`/`tickLinearity`), wired fail-open via `sheetRead.scaleBarCalibration` as a fallback in `groupCalibration` (stated scale still wins). Reads a drawn bar's geometry + tick labels тЖТ `feetPerUnit`; only applies on a high-confidence, feet-unit read, never over a stated/manual cal.
> 2. **Geometric edge-line match** тАФ `src/shared/files/edgeGeomMatch.js` (`fitEdgeLine` PCA/total-least-squares + `orderEndpoints` + `matchSeamEdges`), wired fail-open via `autoStitch.seamEndpointsFor` (prefers a drawn seam's geometry over the rectangle edge; improve-only, keeps the pre-seeded 2-point net). The vector path complementing the raster fitter (`matchLineFit.js`, B413).
> 3. **Legend symbol-union** тАФ `src/shared/files/legendUnion.js` (`unionLegendEntries` + `legendFromPlaced`), wired into the Stitcher Composite key (rendered only when non-empty).
> **STILL OPEN (why this stays here):** each engine consumes geometry that a **browser vector/CV extractor must supply** тАФ the `scaleBar` fact, per-sheet `seamGeom`, and per-sheet `legendEntries` тАФ and **nothing populates those seams yet**, so all three are **dormant / zero behavior change today** (dormant exactly like the OCR/APS seams). None can be headless-verified тЖТ the extraction + real-browser proof on the owner's sets is **V201**. Fail open throughout; never present a topology-only placement as "aligned."

Do it incrementally as code is touched тАФ explicitly **not** one big sweep (UI must stay identical at each step), which is why it lives here rather than as a discrete Open task.

### B259 тАФ Scheduler off in-browser Babel тЖТ a real build step `[Scheduler / build]` (project)  *(orig "P1/M1"; minted **B259**)*
`[ ]` The entire Scheduler (`public/sequence/index.html`, ~9.6k lines) is compiled by `@babel/standalone` in the browser on every load. Project-level work: move to a real build step / modularize. **Entangled** with the file's ability to save its own data back into itself (the File System Access auto-save rewrites the `<script id="planar-data">` block inside the HTML), so any change must preserve self-save. Plan deliberately; not required for any other Scheduler item. Deferred by design.

### B272 тАФ Rule out a main-thread stall from non-Workerized heavy parsing `[Core / Site Planner]` (bug, low priority)  *(owner-dropped 2026-06-20 via chat; arrived as "NEW-2"; minted **B272** тАФ secondary hypothesis to B271)*
`[ ]` Secondary hypothesis for the same "unclickable canvas" symptom: heavy CAD/PDF parse (or other compute) running on the **main thread** instead of a Web Worker, jamming the tab. **Investigated 2026-06-20 (B271 session):** PDF parsing already runs **off** the main thread тАФ PDF.js uses its worker (a separate `pdf.worker` chunk in the build); DWGтЖТDXF conversion is a **backend** (`/server`) concern, never in the browser. The reported incident's symptom (a frozen grab/hand cursor + clicks swallowed, with **no** Chrome "Page Unresponsive тАФ Wait/Exit" prompt) is the signature of stuck pointer state, not a CPU stall, and is fully explained + fixed by **B271**. **No actionable main-thread-stall bug found.** Per the owner's note this drops to **low priority** now that B271 resolves the lockout тАФ kept here (not closed) so it stays on the radar. **Escalate only** if an actual stall is ever observed: then instrument long-task timing, reproduce with a large drawing, and move any straggler heavy compute into a Worker per the standing architecture rule.

- **Enforced merge gate via GitHub branch protection** (the settings half of **B63**): require a PR + a passing build check + "branch up to date before merging" on `main`, plus repo auto-merge. On the **private** repo this only *enforces* on a paid plan (GitHub Pro+); on Free the rules save but don't block тАФ so B63's branch тЖТ PR тЖТ green discipline is the backstop until then. Keep it a manual owner toggle rather than granting the Claude Code app admin rights on a credential-bound repo.

- **B150 тАФ Wire dedicated county appraisal districts (CADs) for the Austin & DFW metros** `[Site Planner / map]` (feature) тАФ *filed 2026-06-18 as a later-feature note (owner asked to park it).* Today only **Harris / Fort Bend / Chambers** have dedicated CADs in `lib/counties.js` (`COUNTIES` + `COUNTIES_MAP`). Austin (Travis/**TCAD**, Williamson, Hays) and DFW (Tarrant/**TAD**, Dallas/**DCAD**, Denton, Collin) parcels currently work **only via the statewide TxGIO fallback** (B137) тАФ coverage is complete (verified: Travis 835K, Tarrant 757K, Dallas 694K, Williamson/Hays/Denton/Collin all present) and returns owner/situs/market-value/acreage, but the statewide copy can **lag** a county's live CAD and carries a **thinner field set** than the district's own service. Wire each county's dedicated CAD (verify it publishes a reachable, **CORS-clean** parcel service first тАФ same vetting as the ETJ sources; some counties publish cleanly, some don't) so Austin/DFW get the same first-class, most-current parcel/appraisal data Houston has via HCAD/FBCAD; add per-county bbox routing to `candidateCountiesForPoint` as each lands.
  - **Bundle the county-mislabel fix:** a parcel in a non-configured county is presently tagged `chambers` (the statewide source's key) because the **B36(a)** `countyAtPoint` relabel only maps to the 3 wired CAD keys тАФ so an Austin/DFW lot saves with the wrong `county`. Record the **true** county name even when no dedicated CAD is wired (cosmetic today; matters for the saved Site Model + which jurisdiction defaults show).
  - Coupled to **B11 / B13 / B36 / B137** (the county-resolution theme). **Not urgent** тАФ the statewide fallback keeps Austin/DFW functional meanwhile; pick up when the owner is actively working those metros (start with Travis, Tarrant, Dallas).
